# DECISIONS LOG вҖ” "The Civil War" autonomous build run

Per Aaron's locked operating parameters (run i, 2026-06-13): **run the whole arc В· always decide & log В· auto-commit AND push at gated milestones В· content-complete each phase.** Every design fork I resolve mid-run is recorded here with rationale so Aaron can override in review. Aaron-locked decisions (via popup) are marked **[AARON]**; ones I made under "always decide & log" are **[CLAUDE]**.

Format: `Dn В· [who] В· phase В· decision вҖ” rationale (reversible? / impact)`

---

## Run-i operating parameters вҖ” [AARON] (popup, 2026-06-13)
- **D0a** Run scope = **run the whole arc** (S0вҶ’S5 then tactical), stop only at an unresolvable fork / unfixable gate failure / done; auto-handoff at context pressure.
- **D0b** Fork policy = **always decide & log** (never pause mid-run; this file is the log).
- **D0c** Commits = **auto-commit AND push** at each gated milestone (clear message + RUN-LOG entry).
- **D0d** Content = **content-complete each phase** (real citation-grade data + PD images per system; slower per phase, less rework). NOTE: the S0 cabinet is the one explicit exception вҖ” Aaron chose engravings-now / PD-photos-in-S2 in the same popup round (D4); the content-complete policy governs S1 onward.

## S0 вҖ” President's-Desk shell + build system
- **D1 В· [AARON]** Build system = **frozen `build/base.html` (byte copy of the run-h monolith) + ordered `src/*.js` modules + zero-dep `tools/build.mjs`** that concatenates + splices before the unique engine-end anchor and re-emits `civil_war_generals.html`, gated in-memory (parse/hex/collision) before writing. вҖ” Honors the handoff's "modularize via a zero-dep concat build step, keep the current HTML as the base." Classic stays frozen (base never edited). (Reversible.)
- **D2 В· [AARON]** Desk structure = **expand the War Department in place** вҖ” `openWarDept` redeclared to render the President's Desk; its 1864 Clock / Muster Roll / War Room become tabs alongside new The-War-Effort / Cabinet / Theater-Map tabs. One owner-mode screen, no parallel system (В§1/В§11). (Reversible.)
- **D3 В· [AARON]** Strategic-turn surface = **auto-surface, one-click skip** вҖ” a "To the Executive Mansion" interstitial between battles (wraps `openUpgrade`); Continue proceeds to the Quartermaster, or open the desk. (Reversible.)
- **D4 В· [AARON]** Cabinet (S0) = **stub now with procedural engraved portraits** (4 named secretaries per side); real advisor auto-manage/teach (R25) + PD photos in S2. (Reversible.)
- **D5 В· [CLAUDE]** Main-menu button relabel **DEFERRED to S1** вҖ” `openMainMenu` is a 124-line broadsheet builder; redeclaring it to rename one cosmetic button (`#gnWarDept` вҶ’ "The President's Desk") is the highest-churn override in S0 for a purely visual gain. The existing button already opens the (now-expanded) desk; the desk is also reachable from the interstitial. вҖ” Risk/benefit. (Reversible; do in S1 once stable.)
- **D6 В· [CLAUDE]** Keep the generated `civil_war_generals.html` **committed** (not gitignored) вҖ” the deliverable premise is open-and-play from a fresh clone with no build step for the player; the build is a developer tool. `build/base.html` is the source of truth for the frozen foundation. (Reversible.)
- **D7 В· [CLAUDE]** **No `_SAVE_VER` bump** for S0 вҖ” new `G.campaign.president` is additive plain data that rides `serializeSave` automatically; back-compat = idempotent `presInit` (lazy migration on next desk-open or battle-resolve). Bumping the version would silently erase every existing ver-1 save. (Reversible only forward.)
- **D8 В· [CLAUDE]** Strategic-date cadence = **~1 month per battle placeholder**, synced up to the 1864 Clock's year. вҖ” S0 is a shell; real variable pacing (weekly in season, compressed in winter, В§22) lands with the strategic-turn-loop content in S1. (Reversible.)

## S1 вҖ” economy (content-complete from research)
- **D9 В· [CLAUDE]** Economy content gathered via a **citation-grade research workflow** (8 agents) вҶ’ `HISTORICAL-DATA-ECONOMY.md` (digest + 28 debate cards) + `data/economy.json` (game-ready params). вҖ” Honors "content-complete each phase." (Source of truth on disk.)
- **D10 В· [CLAUDE]** Build is now **data-driven**: `tools/build.mjs` injects `data/*.json` as a `GAME_DATA` global so `data/economy.json` is the single source of truth while the deliverable stays single-file. вҖ” Cleaner than inlining params in modules; sets up all of S1. (Reversible.)
- **D11 В· [CLAUDE]** S1a = **the finance core first** (the spine + the most teachable system): three funding levers (bonds/taxes/printing), an EMERGENT inflation model (thin CS bond absorption + ~0.10 tax efficiency force the printing press вҶ’ compounding spiral; US bonds+taxes cover demand вҶ’ anchored), inflationвҶ’`clock.weariness` interlink. Production/cotton-blockade/manpower are S1bвҖ“S1d. вҖ” The asymmetry must be emergent from real params, not scripted (R29). (Reversible.)
- **D12 В· [CLAUDE]** Treasury is **delegated to the Secretary by default** (auto-managed historical mix), opt-in to self-manage (balance principle В§27). New "The Treasury" tab (7th desk tab). (Reversible.)
- **D14 В· [CLAUDE]** S1b production layer **EXTENDS the War Room** (reads `wr.nodes` as inputs; does NOT redeclare wr вҶ’ zero regression risk) rather than a parallel system. Asymmetric matГ©riel: US well-found; CS throttled by iron ceiling + import-dependence + IRREVERSIBLE rail decay (~7%/turn) вҶ’ ragged/hungry armies, emergent. Surfaced in the War Effort overview (no new tab). Probe-verified: US rail100/equip100/arms85 vs CS rail42/equip24/arms4/food19%. (Reversible.)
- **D15 В· [CLAUDE]** Local commits only, **no GitHub push** вҖ” Aaron confirmed (run i): "just use local commit, should be fine not pushing to github." Supersedes the D0c push intent. (Reversible.)
- **D13 В· [CLAUDE]** Inflation **calibration**: per-turn `_ecDEMAND=100`, US `inflCoeffвүҲ0.06`/cap 4%, CS `inflCoeffвүҲ0.18`Г—`spiralCoefficient^hiPrintTurns`. Probe-verified over 12 turns: US Г—1.13, CS Г—87.5 (вүҲ historical ~90Г— target), ratio 1:77. These are calibration starts per `economy.json` designerGaps вҖ” playtest to tune; turnCount still unset (rates documented for a 16-turn war). (Reversible.)

## S1c вҖ” cotton / blockade / foreign recognition
- **D16 В· [CLAUDE]** S1c **EXTENDS, does not redeclare**: new `src/60-blockade.js` + `G.campaign.blockade` (sibling state); the production `importFactor` placeholder is wired by EDITING the `prodOnResolve` body (a src module I own, not the frozen base) to read `C.blockade.importFactor` with the static `cfg.importFactor` as fallback вҖ” no new manifest override. `blockadeOnResolve` registered in the existing `_t1Resolve` override BEFORE `prodOnResolve` so the fresh importFactor gates CS arms the same turn. вҖ” Lowest-regression wiring; zero new overrides. Probe-confirmed off>full arms. (Reversible.)
- **D17 В· [CLAUDE]** The 1861 cotton **self-embargo is ON by default for CS** (historical: planters/committees drove it) and **auto-expires at yearвүҘ1862** (Richmond's hunger for hard currency overrode coercion). Player can lift it early via the Diplomacy tab. Recognition gained while the embargo is active = 0 (the trap: coercion against a glutted Britain bought nothing). вҖ” Models the self-sabotage as a *tempting* lever that quietly bleeds the treasury (per the `cotton-self-embargo` card takeaway), not a scripted penalty. (Reversible.)
- **D18 В· [CLAUDE]** Foreign recognition is **foreclosed at yearвүҘ1863** (decay 0.5, boostsвҶ’0), with a 1862 window where it rises (Lancashire famine + early CS wins) then collapses. The S1c numbersAudit endorsed exactly this ("model a recognition window that narrows sharply after Sep 1862 and effectively closes by spring 1863," not a hard Proclamation cutoff). Recognition pulls `clock.intervention` toward itself (Г—0.30/turn) so even CS battlefield wins can't conjure intervention. вҖ” Honest contingency: the one real window, then the door shuts. (Reversible.)
- **D19 В· [CLAUDE]** **Erlanger correction applied to `data/economy.json`**: `netProceedsPct` 0.72 вҶ’ **0.45**, added `issuePriceToErlanger:77` / `publicOfferPrice:90`. The S1c numbersAudit (Gentry 1970) found 77 was Erlanger's BUY price (90 the public offer), and after the post-Vicksburg/Gettysburg slide + Confederate price-propping repurchases the net realized was ~ВЈ1.4M of ВЈ3M (~45%, not 72%). The Erlanger LEVER itself is deferred to S1d/S2 finance; the corrected figure is on disk for when it's built. Audit also flagged the `cottonBlockade.aggregateExportThroughputVsPeacetime: 0.11` as muddled (true blockade-run cotton to Europe ~3-4% of normal), but the sim doesn't read that field вҖ” the revenue-collapse curve (129вҶ’53) carries the teaching point; flagged for playtest, not changed. (Reversible.)
- **D20 В· [CLAUDE]** **Citation-grade content via an 11-agent workflow** (5 research вҶ’ 5 adversarial-verify вҶ’ 1 numbers-audit) вҶ’ `data/diplomacy.json` (multi-voice cards: consensus + scholarly dissent + named-and-countered Lost Cause + primary sources, Verified/Inferred provenance) + `HISTORICAL-DATA-DIPLOMACY.md`. The Verify pass removed 3 fabricated/misattributed citations (e.g., Egnal's *Clash of Extremes* mis-cited; a fabricated "Weidenmier & Brown" co-author). вҖ” Honors content-complete + the adversarial-verify quality bar. (Source of truth on disk.)

## S1d вҖ” manpower / conscription (the war-ender)
- **D21 В· [CLAUDE]** S1d EXTENDS: new `src/70-manpower.js` + `G.campaign.manpower` (sibling); `manpowerOnResolve` registered in `_t1Resolve` AFTER prod (reads `B.casualties[side]` + the year). No new manifest overrides. **`C.manpower.strength` (0-100) is the army-strength index the S5 pre-battle bridge will read** вҖ” S1d produces the strength number that conditions battles. (Reversible.)
- **D22 В· [CLAUDE]** The **replacement-ratio collapse is the war-ender**, modeled as the decisive asymmetry: US holds 1.0 (deep refillable pool); CS falls **0.9вҶ’0.6(1863)вҶ’0.3(1864)вҶ’0.1(1865)** by year. The S1d numbersAudit marked the precise ratios DISPUTED ("DIRECTION confirmed; precise ratios not a published statistic") вҖ” so they stay **calibrated designer values** (economy.json `replacementRatio._inferred:true`), directionally correct. Probe-verified: CS strength 99вҶ’53 (melting), poolвҶ’0 by 1865; US strength holds 100. (Reversible вҖ” playtest to tune.)
- **D23 В· [CLAUDE]** Mechanics from the verified data: **Union draft = a coercive STIMULUS** (Г—1.2 volunteer inflow at 1863), NOT a direct manpower add вҖ” only ~6% of Union soldiers were direct draftees (Geary; audit CONFIRMED); **CS draft load-bearing** (1862, a year earlier); **USCT one-time +180k pool at 1863** (a new pool from the South's labor base); **immigrant inflow US-only** (~25% foreign-born). CS age-band widens 18-35вҶ’17-50 (1864) as a visible crisis 'tell'. Surfaced as a **"The Ranks" overview block** in the War Effort tab (NOT a 9th desk tab вҖ” tab economy; pairs with the production block), delegated to the Sec. of War, ambient teaching line (R26). (Reversible.)
## S1e вҖ” Paths to Victory (the South can win; performance, not script) вҖ” [AARON directive]
- **D25 В· [AARON]** **The asymmetric collapse must be EMERGENT, not scripted.** Aaron caught that S1c/S1d keyed the Confederate death spiral to the calendar (ratio by year, recognition foreclosed 1863, ports fall on schedule), making defeat feel inevitable вҖ” contra В§5 (deterministic by performance), В§8 (the South wins by not losing), В§29 (fair sandbox). FIX: `src/80-victory.js` adds `vicMomentum(C)` (a 0..1 war-fortunes signal from win-rate/will/capital); blockade + manpower now read it. **Winning вҶ’ desertion ~0, ranks refill, ports hold, recognition stays open.** History is only the default-if-losing. Probe-verified (winning South: str 93/desert 9/ratio 0.83/ports held; losing: str 38/desert 297/ratio 0.22/foreclosed). (Reversible вҖ” but this is the locked design intent.)
- **D26 В· [CLAUDE]** The replacement-ratio year curve became a "if losing" FLOOR (raised 1865 floor 0.1вҶ’0.18 so a passive South isn't instant-doomed) that momentum lifts toward 0.95; desertion = `(1-momentum)^1.6 * 16`. New `C.strategy.enemyWill` (the opponent's resolve) вҖ” winning erodes it вҶ’ at вүӨ30 (1864+) the **negotiated-peace victory** becomes reachable (`victoryReady`). The S5 win-screen reads this. (Reversible.)
- **D27 В· [CLAUDE]** **Executable Southern counter-levers** (new "Paths to Victory" 9th desk tab, side-aware): invest in blockade-runners (+importFactor), commission commerce raiders, fortify ports (hold past historical fall), pursue recognition (keep window open), deserter amnesty, arm-and-free the enslaved (Cleburne, +600 pool +0.3 ratio floor, one-time legitimacy shock). The US gets a mirror (Conquer / Hold Political Will / Strangle by Blockade). вҖ” Gives the player real avenues to execute each path (Aaron). (Reversible.)
- **D28 В· [AARON]** **Wild-card catalog вҖ” alt-history gambits for BOTH sides, tiered plausibleвҶ’long-shotвҶ’fantastical/preposterous** (Aaron: "creative and absurd to preposterous okay if I'm entertainedвҖҰ this is a game"). 11 CS (Trent crisis, invade North, burn-cotton, Cleburne, repeater smuggling, Northwest Conspiracy, Hunley fleet, Maximilian's legions, Stonewall-lives, **the Decapitation Plot** [momentum-gated: lands or backfires], Arizona gold) + 10 US (Hard War, radical 1861 emancipation, Anaconda overdrive, repeater army, Grant-early, greenback firehose, Gatling legions, Russian alliance, rail artillery, the general strike of the enslaved). Each one-shot, effect in `_vicApplyWild`. (Reversible; expandable.)
- **D29 В· [CLAUDE]** probe-manpower/probe-blockade reframed to drive a LOSING South (the historical-default trajectory) for their collapse assertions; the WINNING-escapes case is proven by the new `tools/probe-victory.mjs` (12/12). (Test-only.)

## S1d вҖ” manpower / conscription (the war-ender)
- **D24 В· [CLAUDE]** Manpower teaching content via an 11-agent workflow вҶ’ `data/manpower-teaching.json` (`GAME_DATA["manpower-teaching"]`; 5 multi-voice cards вҖ” Geary/Murdock/Moore/Anbinder/Lonn/Glatthaar/Levine; Black agency front-and-center, Lost Cause erasure countered) + a 9-claim audit (7 CONFIRMED, 1 DISPUTED [ratio direction], 1 CORRECTED [date precision: CS Black-soldier statute Mar 13 vs GO No. 14 Mar 23 1865 вҖ” `economy.json` already lists "Mar 13/23 1865", no change needed]). Verify pass removed a misattribution (Fry's Final Report is a standalone 1866 doc, not OR Series III). **Unlike S1c, no sim data correction was required.** (Source of truth on disk.)

## D41 вҖ” BATTLE ROSTER, MORALE RESOLUTION, CADENCE вҖ” [AARON] (popup round 23, 2026-06-14)
Full text in `AUTONOMOUS-RUN.md` В§8 addendum 11.
- **D41.1** Build next: Antietam, Vicksburg, Chickamauga/Chattanooga, Atlanta/the March (on top of existing Bull Run/Shiloh/Fredericksburg/Gettysburg/Malvern/Franklin).

## D42 вҖ” A1 CANNON CORPS: hardening + the CS artillery asymmetry made mechanical вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
Finishing the scaffolded A1 Cannon Corps. An adversarial bug-hunt workflow (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 21 agents) confirmed **9 real findings** (7 correctly refuted as unreachable/cosmetic); all 9 fixed in `src/56-artillery.js` + `data/artillery.json`.
- **D42.1 (save integrity)** `artInit` now guards arrays explicitly (`Array.isArray`) at BOTH the `C.artillery` and `.batteries` levels вҖ” `typeof [] === "object"` let a corrupt/imported array survive, and a JSON round-trip serializes an array as `[]` and drops every named property вҶ’ the whole park silently wiped on the next save. Battery COUNTS are now coerced/sanitized at the same chokepoint (`"3"`вҶ’3; drop null/NaN/objects/вүӨ0).
- **D42.2 (the balance bug)** the 4-vs-6 guns-per-battery handicap was **purely cosmetic** (shown in the UI, zero mechanical effect вҖ” CS and US scored identically). `artBatteryScore` now scales coverage by the side's gun ratio (CS 4/6 вүҲ 0.667), so a CS battery fills the park ~2/3 as fast; the South needs ~18 batteries to match a full Union park.
- **D42.3 (CS stacking penalties вҖ” designer calibration, Inferred)** the STRATEGIC pre-battle score now also models, CS-only: fuze unreliability Г—0.96 (expected-value haircut for shell/case duds; solid shot & canister immune), horse/forage mobility Г—0.95 from 1862 / Г—0.88 from 1864, mixed-caliber resupply Г—0.94 at 3+ calibers; plus the **1863 massing reform** as a both-sides bonus (US Г—1.08 / CS Г—1.04 вҖ” the Union's larger factor stands in for the army-level Artillery Reserve the ANV abolished after Chancellorsville). The per-shot fuze roll, the Whitworth ammunition cap, and gun-loss-on-retreat are **DEFERRED to the battle-day layer (A6) / tactical engine (P-phases)** where they belong as live rolls, not score haircuts. `_designNote` updated to record implemented-vs-deferred.
- **D42.4 (Whitworth import)** the rare British import now costs BOTH sides a premium (CS Г—1.5 blockade / US Г—1.2 foreign-import) instead of the Union buying the catalog's best gun at base price; `csOnly` kept false (both sides fielded a handful).
- **D42.5 (hardening)** `_artCost` honors a configured cost of 0; no-`id` guns are skipped in scoring + refused at purchase; `_artEsc` escapes data fields before `innerHTML`; `artBuy` coerces `n` via `Number()`; the baseline is clamped into [0,100]. *(The parallel unescaped-data gap in `55-weapons.js` is the same latent, non-triggering issue вҖ” flagged as a follow-up hardening item, not fixed in this A1-scoped commit.)*
- **Verified:** probe-cannon now **9/9** (added a US>CS divergence assertion that also asserts CS isn't crushed to baseline вҖ” accessible default per D35/В§8.15); full no-regression suite green (diag-classic Classic paints, desk 12/0, weapons 8/0, bridge 6/0); 0 pageerrors. Sample (1863, 6Г— howitzer12 Q58): **US 44 vs CS 33**; bridge artillery facet 8вҶ’63 lifts overall 76вҶ’83.

## D43 вҖ” A2 ENGINEERING WORKS CORPS: buildable engineer arm + the rail-repair-that-can't-rebuild вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The Engineering Works Corps вҖ” the third buildable in The Armory (after small arms + the Cannon Corps). Four capabilities raised in levels 0-3 with funds: Construction Corps (Haupt's USMRR rail/bridge repair), Field Fortifications (the spade), Pontoon Train (river crossings), Siege Works (saps/parallels). New `src/57-engineering.js` + `data/engineering.json` + `C.engineering`. Feeds the battle bridge as an additive `engineering` facet (weight 0.10); construction raises the supply facet, pontoons lower fatigue; the Construction Corps claws back a FRACTION of each turn's rail loss (slows but never stops the CS rail collapse). CS pays a 1.25Г— materials premium вҖ” Union engineering vastly outstripped the South's (the USMRR rebuilt faster than the CS could wreck).
- **Content:** an 8-agent research+verify workflow вҶ’ **4 Verified multi-voice teaching cards** (Haupt/USMRR; the spade & fieldworks; pontoon mobility; siege engineering). Anti-Lost-Cause: Solonick's "Vicksburg was dug out, not starved out"; the rifle-musket-vs-entrenchment debate surfaced (Griffith vs Hess); the Cold Harbor "7,000 in minutes" myth corrected (Rhea, ~6,000 Union for the day); Vauban dated correctly (17th c.). Every citation independently fact-checked; the verify pass fixed real errors (rank anachronisms, Petersburg mileage, the Foote attribution).
- **Mechanics (designer calibration, Inferred):** baseline 12; scorePerLevel construction 8 / fortifications 7 / pontoons 6 / siege 7 (full park вүҲ 96); construction supply +4/level; pontoons fatigue вҲ’3/level; costPremiumCS 1.25.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 19 agents) вҶ’ **5 confirmed findings, all fixed** (9 correctly refuted as dev-console-only / intended-design):
  - **D43.1 (the real one)** the rail-repair was a CONSTANT additive (`level Г— 1.6`) against MULTIPLICATIVE decay вҶ’ a stable equilibrium, and with the rail War-Room node funded it **pinned rail at 100 forever** (and recovered net-positive from a low point) вҖ” flatly contradicting the locked "irreversible decay, still declines" intent. **Fix:** `prodOnResolve` now stashes `railLossLast`; `engOnResolve` claws back only `min(0.70, 0.24Г—level)` of that loss (a sub-1.0 fraction), so the net trend is strictly negative for every decay/level/node combination. Probe asserts rail never pins at 100 and declines monotonically with the rail node maxed (verified: 100вҶ’84 with full construction, vs 55 without).
  - **D43.2** `perLevelEffect`/`scorePerLevel` lacked NaN/negative guards (a data typo could NaN or *invert* supply/fatigue) вҶ’ Number/isFinite/floor-guarded; a configured `scorePerLevel` of 0 is now honored.
  - **D43.3** boolean-in-save coerced to level 1 (`Number(true)===1` вҶ’ a free capability) вҶ’ `engInit` rejects non-number/string before coercion. **Parity fix applied to `artInit` (A1) too.**
  - **D43.4** `_engEsc` didn't escape quotes but `b.id` sits in a `data-engbuy="вҖҰ"` attribute вҶ’ quote-escaping added. **Parity fix to `_artEsc` + the `data-artbuy` attribute (A1) too.**
  - **D43.5** a bare `&` in static render text вҶ’ `&amp;`.
- **Verified:** probe-engineering **9/9** (incl. the new equilibrium-regression assertion); full no-regression green (diag-classic Classic paints; production/cannon/bridge/desk unaffected вҖ” the prod `railLossLast` + artillery parity edits caused no regression); 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ947KB.

## D44 вҖ” A3 TERRAIN COVER HIERARCHY: the first frozen-engine override вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The first frozen-engine override under В§8.2. Six named cover types (Stone Wall, Entrenchments, Sunken Road, Boulders, Dense Forest, Rail Fence) slotted into the engine's EXISTING terrain/defense model. New `src/58-terrain-cover.js` + `data/terrain-cover.json`.
- **Mechanism (NO fire-function override вҖ” lowest engine risk):** combat reduces fire damage by dividing by `TERRAIN[tile.t].def`; the `.cover` field was defined but UNUSED. The module MUTATES the frozen consts `TERRAIN`/`TCOL`/`PALETTE` at load (adding keys to a const object is legal) to install the 6 cover types with real `def` values + period colors, so combat applies them automatically through the existing `.def` path. def ladder: stonewall 2.00 > trench 1.95 > sunkenroad 1.85 > boulders 1.70 > forest 1.50 > woodfence 1.25 (between clear 1.00 and works/fort 2.10). A stone wall halves casualties (probe: 100вҶ’50).
- **Placement:** OVERRIDES `authoredMap` (verbatim base body + a `tcDecorateMap` pass; added to manifest overrides вҶ’ 2Г— collision-gate). `_tcCoverFor` matches feature labels вҶ’ cover: Sunken RoadвҶ’sunkenroad, Marye's Heights/Stone WallвҶ’stonewall, Devil's Den/Round TopвҶ’boulders, the woods/WildernessвҶ’forest, redan/redoubt/lunette/salient/retrenchmentвҶ’trench. 11 stamps across 6 of 10 authored maps. Positions already `fort` (def 2.10) вҖ” the Vicksburg redans, Antietam's Bloody Lane вҖ” are correctly LEFT by the no-weaken guard. Procedural `genMap` battles aren't decorated (already carry woods/town/works cover).
- **Content:** 1 Verified teaching card (cover as graded killing ground вҖ” Fredericksburg's stone wall & sunken road; Hess / NPS-ABT / Griffith, the A2-vetted sources).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 13 agents) вҶ’ 2 confirmed findings (both medium; the const-mutation timing + idempotency were probed and confirmed SAFE by the refuted set), both fixed:
  - **D44.1** `"trench"` substring-matched "The Retrenchment" (an accidental hit stamping a road tile). Fixed: dropped bare `"trench"` вҶ’ `"trenches"` + added explicit `"retrenchment"` (anchored intent вҖ” The Retrenchment is a genuine Franklin fieldwork, kept as cover).
  - **D44.2** stamping swaps `tile.t`, which the engine also reads for MOVEMENT cost вҖ” and one case (Marye's ridgeвҶ’stonewall) made high ground CHEAPER to cross, contradicting the "def only" claim. Fixed: stonewall cost 1вҶ’2 (a wall is an obstacle) + a **no-speedup guard** (never stamp if `cover.cost < tile.cost`) so decoration never reduces traversal cost; reframed the docs as an honest terrain swap (defвҶ‘, cost neverвҶ“, never water, preserves objectives/elevation).
- **Verified:** probe-cover **8/8** (def ladder, render colors, label matching incl. a Dunker-Church negative, stamping across 6 maps, Antietam Sunken Road strong-cover, never-weaken, the terrain-swap invariant [11 stamps: 0 weaker def, 0 cheaper-to-cross], combat reduction); diag-classic Classic paints (no regression from the override); full no-regression suite green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ962KB.

## D45 вҖ” A4 WIRE THE ARMORY вҶ’ THE BATTLEFIELD: the weapons you buy are what your brigades fire вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The small arms bought in The Armory (`C.armory.loadout`) become what the player's brigades actually carry and fire. New `src/59-armory-field.js`. Frozen-engine override (В§8.2): `genForce`.
- **Mechanism:** a battle unit's firepower is decided entirely by `WEAPONS[u.weapon].pow` (resolveFire ~1037). The module OVERRIDES `genForce` (verbatim base body + a re-arm pass) so a fraction of the PLAYER's fresh infantry are re-armed from the loadout, mapped armory-id вҶ’ engine WEAPONS key (`smoothbore`вҶ’smooth вҖҰ `henry`вҶ’henry, quality-MONOTONIC so a better buy is never a worse field weapon). Buy Spencers вҶ’ a slice of the line carries "spencer" (pow 2.05 vs the musket's 1.00 = +105% fire). The remainder keeps standard issue; veterans keep their earned weapon; the enemy is untouched (no arsenal to draw on).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 16 agents) вҶ’ 5 confirmed findings (the override fidelity confirmed byte-identical by the refuted set), all fixed:
  - **D45.1 (HIGH вҖ” Classic regression)** the re-arm fired whenever `G.campaign` merely existed (gated on `G.campaign.side`), so a **Free Battle with a saved campaign in memory could re-arm the AI ENEMY with the player's arsenal** (or silently self-buff a same-side free-battle force) вҖ” breaking Classic/Free-Battle independence from campaign state. Fixed: gate on `campaignCore` (the engine passes it non-null ONLY for the player force in a real `fromCampaign` battle; the enemy force and BOTH Free-Battle forces get null) вҖ” the exact discriminator.
  - **D45.2 (MED)** engine-era bypass: the armory's `data/weapons.json` year-gates are looser than the engine's `WEAPONS.era`, so the player could field e.g. Sharps at an 1861 battle the era-locked AI couldn't. Fixed: skip any weapon whose `WEAPONS.era` > the battle year (the bought arm fields only once the engine would issue it вҖ” fair vs the AI, no anachronism).
  - **D45.3 (LOW)** float drift: 0.1Г—10 = 0.9999вҖҰ вҶ’ `floor` left one brigade un-armed on a "100%-armed" line. Fixed: snap `fr>0.9995вҶ’1` + an epsilon on the floor.
- **Verified:** probe-armory-field **9/9** (monotonic mapping, player-not-enemy re-arm, fraction lower-bound, whole-army float-safe, veterans keep their weapon, Spencer +105% pow, off-campaign no-op, the engine-era gate [1861 SharpsвҶ’0 fielded], Free-Battle isolation [`{spencer:1.0}` live but core=null вҶ’ not all armed = no leak]); diag-classic Classic paints (no regression from the `genForce` override); full no-regression suite green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ970KB.

## D46 вҖ” A5 TARGETING: VERIFIED the player already picks specific fire targets вҖ” NO engine change вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The backlog asked to "verify the player can pick specific targets + expose/polish it." Investigation + an empirical probe confirm the frozen engine ALREADY supports full player target choice, so A5 ships as a **verification**, not new code.
- **Mechanism (already in the engine):** `fireTargets(u)` (base ~1003) returns every alive, in-range, visible enemy hex; `onHexClick` (base ~1273) fires at the EXACT clicked hex (`resolveFire(sel,c,r)`) when in fire mode вҖ” the PLAYER chooses the target, not an auto/best pick (only the AI uses `chooseBestFireTarget`). Valid targets are highlighted (red circle + crosshair, both 2D Classic and 3D); full keyboard aiming (F вҶ’ arrows вҶ’ Enter).
- **Verified (probe-targeting 5/5):** two enemies placed in a player unit's weapon range вҶ’ `fireTargets` returns BOTH (a real choice); entering fire mode populates/highlights `G.fireT`; clicking ONE specific enemy damages THAT enemy (512вҶ’483, 29 cas) and NOT the other (no auto-target leak); the firing unit is marked fired; an already-fired unit offers no targets (ammo/turn discipline). 0 pageerrors; the probe doubles as a post-A1вҖ“A4 battle smoke test (boot вҶ’ select вҶ’ fire вҶ’ resolve all work).
- **Decision (decide-&-log):** ship NO engine change. The feature is complete and correct; bolting redundant targeting UI onto a working frozen engine would be over-engineering (В§27) and needless В§8.2 override risk. Optional future polish (a louder target highlight / hover "click to fire" tooltip) is deferred вҖ” not worth the risk now. No adversarial bug-hunt run (no new game code to attack; the empirical probe is the verification). Deliverable unchanged; only `tools/probe-targeting.mjs` added.

## D47 вҖ” A6a BATTLE-DAY CONDITIONING: the strategic war shapes the army that takes the field вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The bridge already COMPUTES the conditioned army (`bridgeArmy`) + prep; A6a APPLIES it. New `src/86-battle-conditioning.js` overrides `startBattleRuntime` (frozen-engine В§8.2; verbatim base body + a `_a6Condition()` pass after `G.battle` is built). Campaign battles only (`B.fromCampaign`) вҖ” Free Battle / Classic / diag-classic untouched.
- **What it does:** scales the player force by `bridgeArmy(C)` вҖ” strength Г—[0.88..1.12], morale +(facetвҲ’60)Г—0.3 вҖ” and applies `C.battlePrep` (entrench вҶ’ +2 ent; forcedMarch вҶ’ вҲ’6 morale; raidSupply вҶ’ enemy вҲ’6 morale & вҲ’20% ammo). Field Fortifications (A2) вҶ’ trench cover on ~25%В·level of the line when the entrench order is given (the A2вҶ’A3вҶ’battlefield tie, end-to-end).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 15 agents) вҶ’ 4 confirmed findings (the override confirmed byte-faithful by the refuted set), all fixed:
  - **D47.1 (В§27 calibration вҖ” the key one)** a fresh campaign's `bridgeArmy.overall` is ~74-76, NOT 50, so anchoring `strengthMul` at 50=1.0 silently buffed every no-investment army ~+10% vs the frozen enemy. Re-anchored at 74 вҶ’ a fresh army plays вүҲ Classic (probe ratio **1.009**); a well-run war earns up to +12%, a failing one вҲ’12%.
  - **D47.2 (В§27 over-stack)** narrowed the strength band Вұ20%вҶ’Вұ12%, and **gated the auto-trench on the entrench prep order** (a deliberate slot, not a free always-on stack) so the tactical fight still decides at the extremes.
  - **D47.3 (feature gap)** the Field-FortificationsвҶ’trench tie was inert on the ~29/40 procedural-map battles (no `M.deploy`); now falls back to the player's own occupied hexes (the line they dig in on).
  - **D47.4** entrenching no longer re-terrains objective tiles (skip `t.obj`; preserve authored terrain).
- **Verified:** probe-conditioning **6/6** (strong>weak in-band; free-battle untouched; entrench +2 ent; raid-supply saps enemy morale; **fresh вүҲ Classic, ratio 1.009**; fortifications trench gated on entrench вҖ” 68/91 when ordered, 0 without); diag-classic Classic paints (no regression from the `startBattleRuntime` override); full no-regression suite green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ977KB. **A6b вҖ” the bridge AUTO-RESOLVE (playable end-to-end) вҖ” is next.**

## D48 вҖ” A6b BRIDGE AUTO-RESOLVE: the owner-mode war is playable end-to-end вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run j, 2026-06-14)
The В§8.19 keystone. New `src/87-auto-resolve.js` + an "Auto-resolve" button in the pre-battle briefing (`src/85`). Resolve a battle from the army your war fielded, without playing the tactical fight; "To the Field" (fight it) remains.
- **Mechanism:** `bridgeAutoResolve` builds the CONDITIONED battle (`startBattleRuntime` вҶ’ A6a), `bridgeResolveOutcome` decides the result, then it drives the engine's OWN `campaignAdvance` вҖ” so an auto-resolved battle reconciles the roster, runs `_t1Resolve` (manpower/clock/strategy/enemyWill/victory), awards funds, and advances the chain IDENTICALLY to a fought one. Seeded RND вҶ’ deterministic-by-performance (your strategy, not luck, decides it).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— independent verify, 24 agents) вҶ’ 11 confirmed findings (deduped to 6 fixes; the `campaignAdvance` contract + no-field-flash confirmed sound by the refuted set), all fixed:
  - **D48.1 (HIGH вҖ” the big one)** the original margin compared the raw 0-100 `overall` ~1:1 vs the enemy, so a competent Union could NEVER lose and auto-resolve was strictly *easier than fighting* (a foregone-conclusion click-through). Re-anchored on the EDGE OVER BASELINE (meвҲ’74 vs foeвҲ’64 вҖ” the same anchors A6a / `_arEnemyRating` use), so a baseline army is a real gamble (losable like Classic) and auto-resolve is outcome-equivalent to fighting. Verified: strong war wins (margin 11), weak war loses (margin вҲ’28) вҖ” real jeopardy restored.
  - **D48.2 (HIGH вҖ” audio)** auto-resolve bypassed `endBattle`, so the battle music/wind bed played over the result/interstitial. Now calls `_audLeaveBattle()` + sets `G.mode="result"` + a win/loss bugle, matching `endBattle`.
  - **D48.3 (MED)** honors `C.flipAtk` (recovery role-flip) exactly as `launchCampaignBattle` вҖ” a recovery battle resolves in the correct defend orientation.
  - **D48.4 (MED)** XP parity вҖ” a win credits surviving regiments by magnitude (decisive вҶ’ kills 2 вҶ’ the +2 XP a decisive win deserves; normal вҶ’ +1), matching the fought path.
  - **D48.5 (LOW)** symmetric casualty clamps + a winner-shatters-loser floor (decisive 72% / win 42%) so funds / `stats.infl` / enemyWill-erosion rewards match fighting (enemy bleeds ~40% on a win).
  - **D48.6** removed dead `_arSideStrength`.
- **Verified:** probe-auto-resolve **7/7** (strong out-resolves weak WITH jeopardy; both bleed, loser more; kill attribution; flipAtk honored; enemy-rating asymmetry CS 61вҶ’45 / US 55вҶ’63; `campaignAdvance` advances the war + feeds the tick; briefing offers Auto-resolve + Fight); diag-classic Classic paints; full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ987KB.
- **вҡ‘ THE BATTLE LAYER (A1вҖ“A6) IS COMPLETE вҖ” the owner-mode war is now PLAYABLE END-TO-END:** run the strategic desk вҶ’ field a conditioned army (manpower/production/blockade/arms/cannon/engineers/morale) вҶ’ at each battle auto-resolve or fight вҶ’ the result feeds manpower/clock/strategy/victory вҶ’ win via the chain or a path-to-victory. **NEXT: the strategic arc S2вҖ“S5** (cabinet/advisors, 3-layer morale, 1864 election, press, command/generals, emancipation, civil liberties, events).

## D49 вҖ” S2 m1 THE CABINET & ADVISOR SYSTEM (R25 linchpin / В§8.22 / В§8.54) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The first S2 sub-system: the full historical cabinet replaces the S0 4-secretary stub. New `data/cabinet.json` + `src/31-cabinet.js` (overrides `presRenderCabinet`/`presWireCabinet`; `cabInit`/`cabOnResolve` registered in `90-president-register.js`). The S0 cabinet research run-id was from a prior session (unrecoverable), so content was researched fresh.
- **What it does:** the FULL roster per side is DATE-AWARE вҖ” the current holder of each office is whoever historically held it at the strategic date, so the CHURN is mechanical (Davis's revolving War office WalkerвҶ’BenjaminвҶ’RandolphвҶ’SeddonвҶ’Breckinridge; Benjamin's three-post rotation WarвҶ’State; Chase out July 1864; CameronвҶ’Stanton). Each of the 4 principal advisors (war/treasury/state/navy) gives a one-line **recommendation keyed to the war state** (`_cabReading`: inflationHigh / armyWeak / recognitionRisk / blockadeLoose / always), a one-click **Heed** or **Delegate**, an expandable **why** (reasoning + teaching + provenance), and an **ambition tell** that surfaces for self-servers (high-ambition men always; moderate when their domain struggles). Plus a full-roster expander (the churn made legible) and the two cross-cutting teaching cards. Secondary offices (justice/post/interior) are roster/teaching-only.
- **Content:** the `s2-cabinet-research` workflow (21 agents, **web-grounded** + 2-pass adversarial verify) вҶ’ 18 principal profiles + cross-cards, merged conservatively into `cabinet.json` (structure/tenures/condition-vocabulary preserved; voice/ambition/ambitionTell/stance-prose/cards grafted) then entity-normalized (decode HTML entities in the data so the render layer escapes exactly once вҖ” `&amp;`вҶ’`&`). Verified, multi-voice (4вҖ“7 perspectives/card), anti-Lost-Cause: Benjamin's antisemitic scapegoating, Memminger's structural finance failure ("why the South could not pay for its war"), Davis's micromanagement & states'-rights paralysis as real causes of defeat, the Union team-of-rivals that out-governed Richmond.
- **Mechanics (designer calibration, logged per В§8.7):** Heed = a bounded once-per-turn nudge вҖ” base **+1 political capital at most once per strategic turn TOTAL** (D49.5 fix) + a per-domain micro-effect (treasury weariness вҲ’2 / war supply +2 / state intervention Вұ2 toward the side's interest / navy: CS importFactor +0.02 capped 1.1, US supply +1). Delegate = the auto-manage flag (flavor in m1; domain systems read it later). Ambition thresholds: вүҘ75 always-active, 45вҖ“74 active-when-domain-bad, <45 never. `cabinetLeadership(C)` (a 0вҖ“100 competence index from the sitting War/Navy secretaries, anchored 64) is **exposed but NOT yet consumed by `bridgeArmy`** вҖ” wiring + tuning deferred to the generals/command milestone (m5) where leadership is the headline; m1 is therefore a purely additive UI/teaching milestone with **zero battle-balance change** (D49.7 confirmed this by grep).
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) the cabinet Delegate and the per-system delegates (econ treasury) are independent surfaces in m1 вҖ” unifying them is later polish. (b) G.W. Smith's ~3-day acting War tenure is omitted from the holder roster (mentioned in card text) to keep date-selection clean. (c) per the owner's directive, **WebSearch/WebFetch grounding is now folded into the content workflows** (this one already was), strengthening the вүҘ2-source Verified bar.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— 3-skeptic independent verify, **62 agents**) вҶ’ **8 confirmed of 19 raw (11 refuted)**, all fixed:
  - **D49.1 (HIGH вҖ” save integrity)** a corrupt/imported save with `president` (or `P.date`) as a non-object primitive throws a strict-mode TypeError in `presInit` (assigning a property to a primitive), aborting the cabinet render. Fixed: `presInit` now coerces a primitive `president` to null (rebuild) and guards `date`/`head`/`cabinet`/`pendingChoices`/`log` against non-object/array shapes; `presRenderCabinet` wraps its init calls in try/catch (defense-in-depth).
  - **D49.2 (MED вҖ” silent dead UI)** a `cabinetState` persisted as an ARRAY passed the bare object check, so the per-domain keys cabInit added were dropped on the next JSON round-trip вҶ’ Heed/Delegate became permanent no-ops. Fixed: `Array.isArray` rejection (matches the artInit/engInit idiom).
  - **D49.3 (MED вҖ” teaching accuracy)** `cabOnResolve` named the predecessor from the STALE domain snapshot, so a date that leaps across >1 tenure in one tick (the clock.year sync can jump a year) named the wrong predecessor and skipped offices. Fixed: new `_cabPrevHolder` names the tenure-immediate predecessor.
  - **D49.4 (LOW вҖ” content)** the CS Attorney-General had a NovвҖ“Dec 1863 tenure gap; the no-window fallback resurrected Bragg (gone ~20 months) as "in office." Fixed in data: Watts's end extended 1863-10 вҶ’ 1864-01 to abut George Davis.
  - **D49.5 (HIGH вҖ” balance)** cross-domain Heed stacking added +1 capital PER domain PER turn (up to +64 over the war), and capital feeds the 1864 reelection referendum вҖ” the engagement nudge could decide reelection over battle outcomes. Fixed: capital gated to **once per turn total** (`P.heedCapTurn`); domain micro-effects unchanged.
  - **D49.6 (LOW вҖ” consistency)** navy Heed was pure free capital; gave it a bounded side-appropriate micro-effect (above).
  - **D49.7 (LOW вҖ” scope confirm, NOT a bug)** `cabinetLeadership` confirmed not consumed by `bridgeArmy` вҶ’ zero battle-balance change this milestone (validates the deferral). The exact m5 wiring is recorded.
  - **D49.8 (LOW вҖ” latent XSS hardening)** the President's-log render was unescaped `innerHTML`, and the cabinet now writes dynamic dispatch text into it; escaped both render sites with `_cabEsc` (trusted data today, defense-in-depth).
- **Verified:** probe-cabinet **12/12** (incl. 3 new steps locking D49.1/.2/.3/.5); full no-regression green (diag-classic Classic paints; desk 12/12 вҖ” updated to the new advisor UX; conditioning/auto-resolve/bridge/economy/victory/blockade/manpower/weapons/production/cannon/engineering/cover/armory-field/targeting unaffected); 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ1130KB. **NEXT: S2 m2 вҖ” curated decision cards + the `president.pendingChoices` loop (emancipation as a dated decision + civil-liberties dilemmas), `data/decisions.json`.**

## D50 вҖ” S2 m2 CURATED EXECUTIVE DECISIONS + the pendingChoices loop (В§8.27 emancipation-dated В· В§8.62 civil liberties В· В§8.68 cadence) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The S0 `president.pendingChoices` STUB becomes a real, non-blocking decision system. New `data/decisions.json` (an 8-card deck) + `src/32-decisions.js` (the engine). Decisions surface in the between-battles interstitial AND a new **"Decisions" desk tab** (the 11th); each card presents a real choice with honest bounded effects + teaching, or is left for later.
- **What it does:** `decOnResolve` (registered after pres/cab) OWNS the queue вҖ” adds eligible cards by trigger at the **В§8.68 cadence (вүӨ2 new non-hinge per turn; the hinge always surfaces)**, drops resolved/expired (re-validated through `_decEligible`). `presOnResolve` no longer clears `pendingChoices` (the S0 reset removed; decisions persist until answered). `decResolve` applies each option's bounded, clamped, LOGGED effects (the numbers live in the data; the applier maps fieldвҶ’game state: weariness/capital/intervention/importFactor/strength). The marquee card is **EMANCIPATION** вҖ” a dated Union HINGE (the war's sole hinge) with three real options (issue / go-radical-now / refuse), trading border-state loyalty (capital) against foreign opinion (intervention) and USCT manpower. It sets `C.president.emancipation`, which the **manpower module now reads to gate the USCT pool**: issue вҶ’ unlocks (even pre-1863 if radical); refuse вҶ’ never; **no decision вҶ’ the historical 1863 calendar default holds (zero regression)**. Civil-liberties + home-front cards both sides: habeas corpus (US + CS), Vallandigham/Copperheads, the NYC draft riots, press censorship, the Richmond bread riot, the twenty-slave law.
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-decisions-research` workflow (17 agents, WebSearch/WebFetch + adversarial verify) вҶ’ real public sources WITH URLs (National Archives Emancipation Proclamation, Library of Congress, the Freedmen & Southern Society Project, Dickinson's House Divided, the Greeley/Browning/Corning letters, Neely's *The Fate of Liberty*, McCurry's *Confederate Reckoning*, Foner, Oakes). Merged conservatively (the 3 scaffold cards' ids/option-ids/effects preserved so the probe + engine contract held; 5 new cards translated from qualitative tradeoffs into bounded effects), then entity-normalized. Anti-Lost-Cause + Black-agency-centered (Du Bois's general strike; the self-emancipating enslaved forcing the question; the twenty-slave law's "rich man's war").
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) **emancipation is the ONLY hinge** вҖ” the research merge marked 6 cards as hinges, which would surface 4+ at once and break the cadence; reset to emancipation-only so cadence stays "1вҖ“2/turn, more at the hinge." (b) the cabinet Delegate and decision queue are independent surfaces. (c) the USCT gate keeps the 1863 calendar as the default so old saves + a player who ignores the card behave exactly as before.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— 3-skeptic verify, **56 agents**, 3.0M tokens) вҶ’ **12 confirmed of 17 (5 refuted)**, all fixed:
  - **D50.1 (MED вҖ” cross-module save integrity)** `manpowerOnResolve` read `C.president.emancipation` RAW and ticks BEFORE `decOnResolve`, so a corrupt primitive emancipation could mis-drive the one-way USCT latch. Fixed: manpower calls `decInit(C)` first (sanitizes the field вҶ’ treated as "no decision").
  - **D50.2 (LOW)** `decInit` de-dups `pendingChoices` (corrupt/double-push вҶ’ duplicate cards with colliding DOM ids).
  - **D50.3 (LOW)** the resolved-history render skips non-string option ids (no "[object Object]").
  - **D50.4 (MED)** `decOnResolve`'s drop-filter delegates to `_decEligible`, so a corrupt cross-side/ineligible id is evicted on the next tick.
  - **D50.5 (LOW)** probe-decisions enforces card-id uniqueness at the gate.
  - **D50.6 / D50.7 (HIGH)** `decResolve` had NO idempotency guard вҖ” a card could be re-resolved, re-applying effects and flipping emancipation issueвҶ”decline AFTER the manpower gate irreversibly banked the USCT pool. Fixed: resolved cards are TERMINAL + only a currently-pending card can be resolved.
  - **D50.8 (HIGH вҖ” balance)** the applier upper-clamped capital at 100, but the frozen clock treats capital as unbounded-above (and the 1864 referendum reads it) вҶ’ decisions silently DESTROYED capital above 100. Fixed: capital is floor-only (`Math.max(0, вҖҰ)`), matching the clock.
  - **D50.9 (LOW)** Array guards on `c.options` (malformed deck degrades, no throw).
  - **D50.10 (LOW)** the strength applier floor aligned to the manpower module's own floor of 5.
  - **D50.11 (LOW)** card/option ids sanitized (`_decIdSafe`) identically on the render-attribute and `getElementById`-selector sides (defensive).
  - **D50.12 (scope confirm вҖ” NOT a bug)** decisions are strictly campaign-gated; cannot perturb Classic / Free Battle. Added a save-round-trip + null-field probe step.
- **Verified:** probe-decisions **14/14**; probe-desk **13/13** (incl. the new Decisions tab); probe-manpower **9/9** (the USCT-gate edit no-regression); diag-classic Classic paints; full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ1237KB. **NEXT: S2 m3 вҖ” 3-layer morale (troop/leader/public-will-decides-late) wired to the 1864 election hinge.**

## D51 вҖ” S2 m3 THE THREE-LAYER MORALE SYSTEM + the 1864 election hinge (В§8.61/D39.2 В· В§8.67/D41.2) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
Three interacting, visible morale layers + the home-front-decides-the-war wiring. New `src/33-morale.js` + `C.morale`; surfaced as a **"The Nation's Will"** block in the War Effort overview.
- **What it does:** `moraleCompute(C)` derives three layers fresh each turn from the war state, with the INTERACTIONS in the formulas: **TROOP** morale (battle conditioning via `bridgeArmy.morale` + supply, **lifted by leadership**); **LEADER** reputation (win-rate + the sitting cabinet's `cabinetLeadership`, dragged down by an active ambition tell); **PUBLIC** will (**sunk by the accumulating casualty toll** [D35.6 human-cost] **and runaway inflation**, lifted by victories + the South's hope of recognition, modulated by leadership). The block also shows a **1864-election forecast** mirroring the frozen clock's own support formula.
- **The 1864 election вҶ’ strategic outcome (D41.2):** the frozen `clkOnResolve` already resolves the referendum from `100 вҲ’ weariness + capital/2 + winRateВ·20` (weariness IS the public-will proxy). m3 adds the CONSEQUENCE in `moraleOnResolve` (runs AFTER clk, BEFORE vic): when the verdict lands (once, `electionApplied` latch), it feeds the EXISTING `C.strategy.enemyWill` вҖ” **re-elected вҶ’ enemyWill вҲ’8** (a determined administration grinds the enemy down toward your negotiated-peace win); **repudiated вҶ’ enemyWill +12 + a public-will hit** (the home front broke; the enemy takes heart). So you can win every battle and still lose the war if the public will fails вҖ” and the ballot box is the South's surest road to a negotiated peace (В§8.52).
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) **morale is a computed READOUT with exactly ONE sim coupling** (the bounded one-time electionвҶ’enemyWill nudge) вҖ” it writes NOTHING to the frozen clock/economy/manpower, so it cannot regress their assertions; the 3 layers are derived, not accumulated (no feedback loop). (b) The election coupling feeds the EXISTING victory module (enemyWillвҶ’victoryReady, D26) rather than a new path; full victory/defeat *resolution* (incl. a US-side election-loss ending) remains S5's job. (c) The casualty toll is a SEPARATE accumulator from the clock's per-battle weariness (intended вҖ” the toll is the cumulative human cost that sinks public will over the whole war). (d) `morale.troop` mirrors the battle-side morale the bridge already uses; wiring morale BACK into the bridge is deferred (battle-balance protected this milestone).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— 3-skeptic verify, **29 agents**) вҶ’ **7 confirmed of 8 (1 refuted вҖ” it validated that morale writes nothing to the frozen clock/economy/manpower)**, all fixed:
  - **D51.1 (HIGH вҖ” save migration)** the one-time electionвҶ’enemyWill latch (`electionApplied`) was presence-checked, so a legacy/pre-morale save already past the 1864 verdict (`resolved1864` true, no `C.morale`) would RE-FIRE the enemyWill nudge on load. Fixed: `moraleInit` seeds `electionApplied = !!(clk.resolved1864)` (a verdict already resolved at init = already applied) вҖ” migration-safe, no `_SAVE_VER` bump (the D7 pattern).
  - **D51.3 / D51.5 (HIGH/MED)** the latch was burned BEFORE the effect landed, so a turn with `C.strategy` absent would seal it and lose the consequence forever. Fixed: the latch is now set ATOMICALLY inside the `S && enemyWill` guard (mirrors D49.5) вҖ” it only seals when the nudge applies, and retries next turn otherwise.
  - **D51.2 (MED)** a corrupt negative `casualtyToll` inverted the casualty penalty and pinned public will to 100. Fixed: `moraleInit` floors the toll to вүҘ0 (`!(x>=0)` also catches NaN/вҲ’Infinity); `casPenalty` lower-bounded `Math.max(0, вҖҰ)`.
  - **D51.4 (MED/LOW)** the repudiation `M.public вҲ’= 10` was an inert one-tick write (public is recomputed each tick, clobbering it). Fixed: replaced with a DURABLE `M.repudiated` flag that `moraleCompute` reads (a persistent вҲ’12 public-will penalty) вҖ” the "home front breaks" now actually shows and lasts.
  - **D51.6 (refuted вҶ’ NONE)** the integration lens confirmed morale writes ONLY `C.morale` + the one bounded enemyWill nudge (no frozen-clock/economy/manpower writes; `moraleCompute` only READS `bridgeArmy`/`cabinetLeadership` вҖ” no recursion), so the no-regression guarantee holds by construction.
- **Verified:** probe-morale **10/10** (the 3 layers + interactions, casualty/inflation sinks, leadership-lifts-troops, toll accumulation, the 1864 electionвҶ’enemyWill in both directions, render, AND the D51.1/.2/.3 corrupt/legacy-save hardening); full no-regression green (probe-victory **12/12**, blockade/manpower/bridge/auto-resolve/desk/economy/decisions/cabinet/conditioning/weapons/production/cannon/engineering/cover/armory-field/targeting all green; diag-classic Classic paints); 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ1249KB. **NEXT: S2 m4 вҖ” the press / public-opinion system (В§8.57/D38.1): period papers react to your war вҶ’ public morale + the 1864 election; censorship/Vallandigham as a lever; ties the broadsheet UI to the 3-layer morale.**

## D52 вҖ” S2 m4 THE PRESS / PUBLIC-OPINION SYSTEM (В§8.57 / D38.1) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The real Civil War newspapers, North and South, react to your war with period broadsheet editorials вҖ” a real driver of the public will that decides the 1864 election. New `data/press.json` (12 papers) + `src/34-press.js` + `C.press`; surfaced as a new **"The Press"** desk tab (the 12th, period broadsheet).
- **What it does:** each paper has a real political LEAN (radical / administration / war-democrat / copperhead / fire-eater / abolitionist) that sets HOW it reacts. `pressOnResolve` (runs BEFORE `moraleOnResolve`) reads the turn's condition (victory / defeat / stalemate / heavy-casualties / emancipation-once), each paper runs a matching editorial and shifts its FAVOR toward/against the war effort (strongly-for +8 вҖҰ strongly-against вҲ’8, clamped 0-100; a paper with no editorial for today's news drifts back toward its standing lean), and the aggregate SENTIMENT feeds `moraleCompute`'s public-will layer (`pressTerm = (sentimentвҲ’50)В·0.2`, Вұ10) вҖ” so the press is a real driver of the home front. The tab shows the day's headlines, each paper's stance, and the aggregate.
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-press-research` workflow (7 agents, WebSearch/WebFetch + adversarial verify) вҶ’ 12 real papers with real editors + URLs (Greeley's *Tribune*, Garrison's *Liberator*, Medill's *Chicago Tribune*, Curtis's *Harper's Weekly*; the *NY World*, *Chicago Times*, *Crisis*, *Herald* Copperhead/Democratic sheets; the *Richmond Examiner* & *Charleston Mercury* savaging Davis, the *Enquirer* defending him, the *Dispatch*). Merged conservatively (the 4 scaffold ids/leans preserved). Anti-Lost-Cause throughline: BOTH presses were bitterly divided вҖ” the Confederate press was no propaganda monolith but raged at Davis, conscription, and impressment; the *Herald*'s ahistorical "war-independent" lean was mapped to the contract's `war-democrat`.
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) the press is a READOUT + ONE read-only coupling (morale reads `pressSentiment`) вҖ” it writes nothing to the frozen clock/economy/manpower/strategy (zero regression); `pressSentiment` is a NEUTRAL 50 until the press first reacts, so it perturbs nothing at init / in the morale probe. (b) the cross-cutting teaching cards intentionally name papers from BOTH sides (a press-landscape lesson) вҖ” they are NOT side-filtered; only the player's PAPER LIST is side-scoped. (c) the censorship/Vallandigham LEVER is the existing m2 decision cards (`us-press-censorship`/`us-vallandigham`) acting on public opinion; a deeper standing-censorship tie to per-paper favor is a future deepening.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 lenses Г— 3-skeptic verify, **44 agents**) вҶ’ **7 confirmed of 13 (6 refuted)**, all fixed:
  - **D52.1 (MED вҖ” save integrity)** `pressInit` repaired only the array-ness of `C.press.headlines`, not the entries, so a corrupt/legacy save with a `null` headline entry crashed `pressRenderTab` вҶ’ froze the whole Press tab (the `_wdRefresh` dispatch isn't wrapped). Fixed: `pressInit` filters headlines to well-formed objects + a `!hd` continue-guard in the render.
  - **D52.2 / D52.6 (LOW)** the sentiment guards were NaN-blind (`typeof NaN === "number"`). Fixed: `pressInit` + `pressSentiment` reject non-finite / out-of-range sentiment (so a corrupt NaN can't poison `moraleCompute`'s public will).
  - **D52.3 (LOW вҖ” calibration)** the heavy-casualties priority ran over a victory's rally, but the heavy-casualties editorials were `neutral` вҶ’ a bloody win read as a no-op. Fixed in data: the "mournful column" вҶ’ `against` (a bloody victory now visibly TEMPERS the press вҖ” historically faithful to the bloody 1864 victories that sapped Northern morale); the abolitionist "blood atones" stays neutral (its distinctive framing).
  - **D52.4 (LOW)** the emancipation-once latch was set whenever the condition was active even if no paper actually printed an emancipation editorial. Fixed: the latch is set ONLY when a paper ran an emancipation editorial (`firedEmancipation`).
  - **D52.5 (LOW)** `_prsConditions` trusted the caller's `"draw"` string for stalemate; now also treats `winnerSide == null` as a stalemate (mirrors `endBattle`).
  - **D52.7 (LOW)** an editorial with an empty headline could push an empty broadsheet line; gated on `ed.headline`.
- **Verified:** probe-press **10/10** (papers load side-correct, neutral-until-reacted, victory>defeat sentiment, the Copperhead turns on a defeat, emancipation-splits-once latch, the pressвҶ’public-will coupling anchored at 50, CS paper-list correctness, render, AND the D52.1/.2/.4 hardening + the bloody-day dampener); probe-desk **13/13** (the new Press tab); probe-morale **10/10** (the `pressTerm` edit anchored = no change); full no-regression green; 0 pageerrors. Deliverable вүҲ1300KB.
- **Tooling note:** running TWO browser-probe batteries concurrently collides on the shared `:8765` server + `tools/shots/*.json` вҶ’ ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED / goto-timeout flakes + cross-overwritten result files. **Run probe batteries SEQUENTIALLY, one battery at a time.**

## D53 вҖ” S2 m5 COMMAND: the NAMED-GENERALS system + the bridge LEADERSHIP wiring (В§8.24/В§8.58 В· D31.4/D38.2 В· GRAND-STRATEGY В§19) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-14)
The LAST big S2 sub-system: the President appoints / promotes / relieves the commanding general of his principal army, and the sitting general (skill + evolving reputation) blended with the cabinet finally drives the **bridge LEADERSHIP facet** that was a `var leadership = 64;` placeholder since the battle layer (D49.7). New `data/generals.json` (20 generals) + `src/35-command.js` + `C.president.command`; a new **"Command"** desk tab (the 13th).
- **What it does:** each historical commander carries traits (**skill / aggression / caution**), an **evolving reputation** (rises with victory, falls with defeat вҖ” `cmdOnResolve`), and **ambition** (the McClellan problem). A **date-aware DEFAULT** holds the post if the player never intervenes (`_cmdHistoricalDefault`, the `_cabHolder` idiom): the single-slot **iconic-army chain** вҖ” US Army of the Potomac вҶ’ general-in-chief (Scott вҶ’ McClellan вҶ’ Burnside вҶ’ Hooker вҶ’ Meade вҶ’ Grant), CS Army of Northern Virginia (J.E. Johnston вҶ’ Lee). Appointing a specific general LOCKS the post; **relieving costs political capital** (`clock.capital`), gated for a `very-costly` (popular, politically dangerous) general вҖ” the McClellan dilemma made mechanical, with a free "restore the historical command" escape valve.
- **THE KEY WIRING (the milestone's point):** `commandLeadership(C) = clamp(42,88, 64 + (genRatingвҲ’64)В·0.7 + (cabinetLeadershipвҲ’64)В·0.3)`, `genRating = 0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation`. **Anchored at 64** вҖ” a neutral general + neutral cabinet = 64 = the old constant, so a fresh/default command is byte-equivalent to Classic (the A6a/D47.1 anchor lesson). `src/85` line 90 now consumes it, and `bridgeArmy.overall` gains a **bidirectional leadership edge** `+(leadershipвҲ’64)В·0.18` (mirrors the additive artillery/engineering arms, but signed) вҖ” a masterful command lifts the army a few points, a poor/discredited one drags it; at the anchor the edge is exactly 0. The general's temperament also nudges the **auto-resolve margin** (`commandMarginEdge`: aggressive presses the attack, cautious is sound on defense; deterministic, Вұ~2). Reputation evolution (win +3 / decisive +6 / loss вҲ’4 / decisive вҲ’8 / draw вҲ’1, clamped 5вҖ“98) means a defeated commander's army weakens while a victor's separation widens.
- **Content:** the web-grounded `s2-generals-research` workflow (10 agents: 4 research clusters + 4 adversarial-verify + cross-roster balance + teaching cards; WebSearch/WebFetch) вҶ’ 20 generals (US 10 / CS 10) + 4 multi-voice teaching cards (the McClellan problem; the Lost Cause & the generals; "Grant the butcher" rebutted; what makes a general). **Anti-Lost-Cause throughout:** Lee excellent-not-infallible (Gettysburg/Pickett's Charge); Grant/Sherman/Thomas top-tier; Forrest's bio NAMES Fort Pillow + the KKK + slave-trading; Bragg/Hood poor army commanders.
- **Decide-&-log:** (a) **single-slot default = the iconic army** (the bridge fields one army; the West/secondary commanders вҖ” Thomas, Sherman, Sheridan, Halleck, A.S. Johnston, Beauregard, Bragg, Hood вҖ” are fully APPOINTABLE via `availableFrom` but `commandFrom`-null so they don't hijack the default chain or jump theaters). (b) **the general is confined to the BRIDGE + auto-resolve, NOT the m3 morale leader layer** вҖ” `33-morale.js` deliberately keeps `cabinetLeadership` (NOT `commandLeadership`): routing the general in would double-count the cabinet (commandLeadership already folds it in) AND confound the cabinet-isolating morale probe (which varies the DATE to vary the cabinet, also varying the date-derived default general). Folding the general into morale is deferred. (c) **anchored zero-regression** вҖ” every battle-layer + morale assertion holds (verified empirically below).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (8 dimensions Г— independent skeptic verify, **20 agents**) вҶ’ **9 confirmed of 12, all fixed:**
  - **D53.1 (HIGH вҖ” data) Thomas wrongly defaulted the US chain.** Thomas commanded the Army of the *Cumberland* (West), but his `commandFrom` (1863-10, later than Meade's 1863-06) made `_cmdHistoricalDefault` pick him over Meade Oct 1863вҖ“Mar 1864. Fixed: `commandFrom/commandTo вҶ’ null` (appointable, not default). My first chain-probe missed it (didn't sample 1863-10вҶ’1864-03).
  - **D53.2 (MED вҖ” data) Sherman same.** His `commandFrom` (1864-03, the Military Division of the Mississippi) tied Grant's; nulled (appointable). US chain is now bulletproof: вҖҰMeade вҶ’ Grant.
  - **D53.4 (HIGH вҖ” recursion landmine) `bridgeArmy вҶ’ commandLeadership вҶ’ cabinetLeadership вҶ’ _cabAmbitionActive вҶ’ _cabReading("war") вҶ’ bridgeArmy`.** m5 closed a cycle that would stack-overflow whenever the sitting War Secretary has `ambitionTell` + ambition in [45,75). Dormant under current data (probes were green) but a data-change crash. Fixed: a re-entrancy guard `_brgLeadGuard` in `bridgeArmy` вҖ” a nested call uses the neutral 64 anchor, the outer call gets the true value. (Chose the guard over the verifier's "_cabReading uses manpower.strength" so the cabinet's war-reading heuristic + its probe stay intact.)
  - **D53.5 (HIGH вҖ” edge) post-war fallback jumped to the FIRST commander.** `_cmdHistoricalDefault`'s no-window fallback returned the earliest `commandFrom` (Scott) when a campaign ran past the last tenure end. Fixed: before the first tenure вҶ’ earliest; after the last вҶ’ the LATEST-ending commander (continuity).
  - **D53.6 (MED вҖ” save) `_activeId` rode the save unvalidated.** The handover-detection cache could reference a removed/wrong-side general after a roster change. Fixed: `cmdInit` clears it if not in the side roster (a just-died-but-in-roster id is KEPT so the succession still logs).
  - **D53.7 (MED вҖ” UX) capital soft-lock.** The pool rounded `clock.capital` for display but `cmdAppoint` gated on the raw value вҶ’ a fractional capital could show an affordable button that silently failed. Fixed: round at the gate too.
  - **D53.8 (MED вҖ” XSS) `_cmdTraitBar(label,hint)` unescaped.** Call sites are hardcoded today, but the signature was injection-prone; now `_cmdEsc`'d (D43.4 discipline).
  - **D53.9 (MED вҖ” DOM) wire/render id-escape mismatch.** Render escaped the appoint-button id, `cmdWireTab` didn't; harmless for kebab ids but inconsistent. Now both `_cmdEsc`.
  - **D53.10 (LOW) dead inner ternary** in `_cmdGenRow` (the outer guard already proved `availableUntil` truthy). Simplified.
- **Verified:** probe-command **14/14** (data/schema, cmdInit + reputation seeding, the **fresh anchor 72вҶ’overall 77 Classic-safe**, date-aware default, appoint Grant lead 87 vs Burnside 52, reputation 88вҶ’98 win / 88вҶ’64 loss, the McClellan relief gate at 27 capital, the trait margin edge, the **D53-decoupling** [general moves the bridge, leaves the cabinet-driven leader layer], lock/revert, side-correctness, render, + the **D53.4 recursion guard** and **D53.5 post-war** regression guards); full no-regression GREEN вҖ” bridge 6/6 В· conditioning 6/6 (the fresh-Classic anchor) В· auto-resolve 7/7 В· cabinet 12/12 В· morale 10/10 В· desk 13/13 В· press/decisions/victory/manpower/economy/production/blockade/weapons/cannon/engineering/cover/targeting/armory-field/cab-exploit all green В· diag-classic Classic paints; **0 pageerrors** throughout. Deliverable вүҲ1392KB. **S2 is COMPLETE (m1вҖ“m5). NEXT: S3 alt-history В· S4 education/codex/tutorial/WCAG-AA В· S5 victory + graded report + Reconstruction В· then the run-k graphics/footage + survival/loot directives.**

## D53-OPS вҖ” STANDING INSTRUCTION: push to GitHub ONLY after PROPER VETTING вҖ” [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-14)
