## D71 вҖ” EXTERNAL REPORT REVIEWED (Gemini "Economic & Architectural Analysis of Zero-Cost Single-File Web Game Development") вҖ” adopt/modify/ignore verdicts вҖ” [AARON+CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
Aaron supplied a Gemini report (a generic 2026 primer on $0 single-file web-game dev: coding-assistant tiers, asset-separation, engine benchmarks, asset generators, state/combat patterns, deployment) and asked for an adopt/modify/alter/ignore call against the WHOLE project. **Net: mostly IGNORE вҖ” the report was written with no knowledge of this project; on nearly every axis our existing choices are already better-suited to the teaching mission + period aesthetic + single-file/$0 + determinism + the Claude/Opus agent loop. ~3 useful takeaways, all Phase-H / publish, none changing the current roadmap.** Logged so a future chat does not re-litigate "should we use Phaser / DeepSeek / pixel-art."
- **IGNORE вҖ” coding-assistant choice (Cursor/OpenCode/Cline + DeepSeek/GPT, В§1/В§3/В§8):** moot вҖ” we build with **Claude Code + Opus 4.8** + the Workflow/subagent orchestration + deterministic probes + adversarial bug-hunts. Downgrading to the report's "$0" pick (OpenCode + DeepSeek-V4-Flash) would gut the reasoning this project depends on (balance A/B, the fog-inversion bug class, anti-Lost-Cause content verification). Its 2026 prices/limits/model names are unverified + fast-stale; irrelevant to the decision.
- **IGNORE the engine switch; KEEP one warning (В§4):** we use a CUSTOM single-file engine (frozen `build/base.html` 2D canvas + async-CDN Three.js w/ 2D fallback + the `src/tactical/T0вҖ“T7` real-time sim). Switching to Phaser/KAPLAY/Godot = a catastrophic rewrite that breaks single-file/no-build/determinism/every probe. **BUT** the **Godot `SharedArrayBuffer` + COOP/COEP-headers-can't-be-set-on-GitHub-Pages** problem is real and VALIDATES our no-WASM-threading custom-JS choice (runs on free static hosting where Godot can't). Filed as a permanent guardrail: do not pull in any Phase-H media lib that needs `SharedArrayBuffer`; `coi-serviceworker` is the known shim if headers are ever needed. Reinforces D68 #10 (Classic IS the hex engine, no new co-equal WASM engine).
- **IGNORE the asset generators (В§5):** PixelLab/Sprite AI = pixel-art (WRONG aesthetic вҖ” we are period broadsheet/engraving). Recraft's free tier KEEPS ownership of outputs (an IP trap for a project Aaron wants to own). AI period art also risks anachronism vs the citation-grade/anti-Lost-Cause bar. Our Phase-H plan вҖ” REAL PD imagery from LoC/Internet Archive/Wikimedia вҖ” wins on aesthetic, cost, IP, and historical accuracy. (Sole back-pocket: Recraft vector-SVG *could* help the H1b corps-badges/flags idea IF hand-authoring is too slow вҖ” only style-locked + paid commercial rights; hand-drawn period SVG likely still better.)
- **IGNORE вҖ” state/combat/turn patterns (В§6) вҖ” already exceeded:** we already have bare-name global state (`G`/`__FIELD`), seeded deterministic sim (`fldRng`, no `Date.now`/`Math.random` in probes), a phase model, and a combat resolver (`fldResolveFire`/`fldResolveMelee`) with cover/terrain/morale/fatigue/canister/command/logistics far richer than the report's toy formula. The report assumes turn-based; our primary engine is real-time (Classic is the frozen turn-based layer). Mild validation only: unified-state + deterministic + localStorage-serialize == our planned Phase J saves (D54).
- **THE 3 KEEPERS (all Phase-H / publish; none now):** (1) **ADOPT/already-planned вҖ” automated asset ingestion:** the report's `compile.py`вҶ’Base64 idea = what `tools/build.mjs` already does for code+data; at Phase H extend **build.mjs (Node, not a separate Python script)** to Base64-embed + TIER/COMPRESS media w/ offline fallback вҖ” corroborates D68 #7 (the ~1.7MB single file will balloon; portability needs deliberate media tiering). (2) **NOTE вҖ” publish options (hosting stays deferred, D54):** GitHub Pages (simplest for one file) or **itch.io + Butler** (best indie discovery + in-browser play + automated deploy); Vercel unnecessary. **$0 nuance the report missed:** GitHub Pages on a PRIVATE repo needs GitHub **Pro (paid)** вҶ’ for true $0 use a public deploy repo OR itch.io; rename/copy `civil_war_generals.html`вҶ’`index.html` at publish. (3) **NOTE вҖ” COOP/COEP guardrail** (above) folded into Phase-H/D-engine thinking.
- **Action:** no code/roadmap change now. Pointers folded into V1-CHECKLIST Phase H (asset-ingestion-via-build.mjs + the no-SharedArrayBuffer guardrail) and Phase J / the hosting-deferred item (GitHub-Pages-private-needs-Pro + itch.io/Butler). The report did NOT change what ships for B-6.

## D72 вҖ” PHASE B-6 В· CS-PLAYER "COMMAND EITHER SIDE" (the tactical mode is now playable from either army; the B-1 attacker AI becomes player-facing) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The 6th + FINAL V1-CHECKLIST Phase-B item (D61, charter fork #10). The real-time tactical engine can now be commanded from EITHER army: pick the Confederacy and you DEFEND Henry House Hill while the B-1 attacker-AI presses you uphill вҖ” which is exactly what makes the B-1 doctrine player-facing (the whole point of the fork) and doubles tactical replayability. New module `src/tactical/T7-command-side.js` + surgical seams in T0/T1/T3 + `tools/probe-csplayer.mjs`. Deliverable вүҲ**1702KB**.
- **NOT a new gated sim layer вҖ” a GENERALIZATION.** The plumbing was already half-built (T2 `fldSkirmishOOB` assigns `u.ai` by side; the T2 campaign briefing already speaks side-aware role text; `fldPlayerSide()` already drove the B-2/B-3/B-4 display layers; the campaign result-feedback `fldCampaignComputeOutcome`/`ApplyOutcome`/`EndHtml` were written side-aware back in Phase A). B-6 closed the TWO remaining gaps: **(1)** the input layer (`fldPlayerSel`/select-all/`fldCycleSel`/`fldPointerDown`) and the render/HUD **fog VIEWER** (the 2D markers, the ghosts, the 3D sync, the friend/foe line) were a literal `"US"` вҶ’ now read `fldPlayerSide()`; **(2)** the hand-authored First Bull Run scenario only ever fielded a US player вҶ’ now honours a side toggle.
- **`__FIELD.playerSide` made AUTHORITATIVE** (resolved once in `fldInitSim`, precedence: explicit `opts.playerSide` > skirmish `playerSide` > a CS campaign via `_fldCamp().side` > `"US"`). `fldBrSpec` (T1) flips the scenario AI flags off it вҖ” the player's side is the non-AI side, the other side is the AI (a CS player DEFENDS; `__FIELD.attacker` stays US, so the B-1 attacker AI presses). `fldPlayerSide()` (T3) resolves a CS **campaign LIVE** from `G.campaign.side` first (the legacy contract the officer roster/fog read mid-setup), then the explicit per-launch side.
- **NEW player-facing UI (T7):** a period-broadsheet **side-choice card** for the standalone Bull Run ("Lead the Union вҖ” ATTACK" / "Hold for the Confederacy вҖ” DEFEND"); a **side-aware briefing objective** (attack-&-seize vs hold-&-deny); a side-aware **"your war vs history"** end note (pronoun follows the side you played); an end-screen **"you" outcome line** (role-aware: "you carried the position" / "your line held" / "your assault was repulsed"); the 3D **camera seats behind the PLAYER's home edge** (a CS defender looks across his line at the advancing Union); the friend/foe HUD names the player's own side with the dignified FULL name ("4 Confederate vs 1 Union"). The skirmish menu + the campaign already plumbed side, so they work via the same generalization.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** the player side defaults to `"US"` (the historical attacker), so every standalone/probe launch resolves exactly as before; under `autoBoth` all units are AI regardless of side (the AI-vs-AI sim is independent of `playerSide`, proven seed-for-seed). The render/control/HUD generalizations are unreachable in the headless probes (renderer `none`). The 9 tactical baselines + bullrun stayed byte-identical.
- **VETTING CAUGHT A REAL REGRESSION (fixed before any commit):** my first `fldPlayerSide()` rewrite trusted a stale `__FIELD.playerSide` and broke the CS-**campaign** officer-roster/fog contract (the roster/fog read `fldPlayerSide()` mid-setup, before a relaunch). `probe-officers` flagged it. **Fix:** resolve a CS campaign LIVE from `G.campaign.side` first, then the explicit per-launch side (T0 `fldInitSim` + T3 `fldPlayerSide` made consistent; `fldBrSpec` routed through `fldPlayerSide()`).
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (52 agents вҖ” 6 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 15 findings вҶ’ 11 confirmed + 7 critic gaps; 4 refuted. FIXED the ones that matter:** **(HIGH)** a skirmish "Fight Again" soft-locked a CS player вҖ” the rematch fell through to the generic US sandbox, leaving a CS player zero controllable units вҶ’ the rematch now REPLAYS the full stashed launch spec (`__FIELD._launchOpts`, same scenario/skirmish/side/fog, bumped seed) AND the sandbox OOB now assigns `ai` by `playerSide` (defence-in-depth; byte-identical for US); **(MED Г—2, dedup)** the 3D camera was hard-wired to the US south edge вҶ’ side-aware home-edge seating; **(MED, critic G1)** reinforcement banners + the aria-live announce + the "Reinforcements arrive" auto-pause leaked a fog-hidden ENEMY detrainment вҶ’ all gated on player-visibility (own side / fog off / scouted), fog-OFF byte-identical; **(MED, critic G2)** `probe-csplayer` only HUD-checked the no-leak invariant вҶ’ added a fog-RENDER step asserting the render-hide predicate hides вүҘ1 enemy and NEVER a friendly, for both viewers; **(LOW)** the side-card `aria-label` was unescaped (latent if a future `objective.name` carries `"`/`<`) вҶ’ escaped the dynamic parts; the end-screen "you" line now also speaks on the aria-live region; the stale "player controls only the US" comment reworded; a byte-identity-delegation note added to the probe. **DEFERRED with note (pre-existing / convention-consistent, not B-6 regressions):** the side-choice sheet uses the established Back-not-Esc sheet convention (matches Skirmish/Preset); the top-bar objective readout stays factual ("Union holdsвҖҰ"); `openSheet`-unavailable falls back to US; `fldPlayerSide()` campaign-first precedence is intentional (the legacy live contract вҖ” every reachable launch agrees).
- **WCAG 2.2 AA (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** clean after 2 contrast fixes вҖ” the side-card badge `opacity:.75` blended the accent below 4.5:1, so it was removed and the CS accent darkened `#b06a5a`вҶ’`#b77668` (4.72:1 on the `.upg` bg); everything else (titles, decks, objective block, outcome line, briefing/end borders) passes; ARIA (role=group, per-card aria-label, type=button, dialog focus traps) + CVD-safety (side named in text + ATTACK/DEFEND badge, never colour-alone) confirmed.

The CS defense is winnable (the role-aware defender holds the hill under fog), the field renders from your side, the fog shows only what YOU scout, and the briefing/HUD/end-screen all speak from the army you command.

NEXT: Phase C tactical breadth вҖ” Eastern marquee first (Antietam / Fredericksburg / Gettysburg / Chancellorsville on the data-driven engine, D69).**

## D73 вҖ” PHASE C-1 В· FREDERICKSBURG (the Marye's Heights assault) вҖ” the SECOND data-driven tactical battle + the data-driven scenario-UI generalization + the scenario-gated "doomed-assault" AI posture вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The first Phase-C (tactical BREADTH) milestone, Eastern marquee first per D69. The tactical engine, mature after B1вҖ“B6, is now battle-AGNOSTIC: a new historical battle = a `data/<battle>.json` file + one registry line, NO new combat code. Fredericksburg, Dec 13 1862 вҖ” Burnside's army storms the open glacis toward the sunken Telegraph Road, where Longstreet's men hold a 4-foot stone wall under the pre-sighted guns on Marye's Heights. New `data/fredericksburg.json` (`GAME_DATA.fredericksburg.fredericksburg`) + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs` + the T1/T7 UI generalization + a small gated T0 engine seam. Deliverable вүҲ**1743.6KB**.
- **THE DATA-DRIVEN SCENARIO REGISTRY (the reusable spine).** `fldScenarioRegistry()`/`fldScenarioData(id)` (T1) map each registered id вҶ’ its `GAME_DATA.<battle>` object; `fldScenarioInit` builds ANY registered id from the SAME shape (field/attacker/defender/objective/leaders/supply/terrain[hills,woods,walls,markers]/oob/reinforcements/teaching). Bull Run resolves the identical object it always did (`fldScenarioData("bullrun1")`) вҶ’ byte-identical. Adding Antietam/Gettysburg/etc. is now a data file + a registry line.
- **THE DATA-DRIVEN UI GENERALIZATION (T1+T7).** `fldInjectScenarioButtons` iterates the registry (Bull Run keeps its bespoke marquee button `_fldInjectBullRunButton`; every other battle gets a data-built button from `data.menu`) and returns the LAST button so T0 anchors the skirmish/preset buttons after the whole block; `fldLaunchBattle` fires the briefing for ANY scenario; `fldBullRunSideChoice`вҶ’`fldScenarioSideChoice(id,go)` reads `sd.sides` (per-battle side-choice card) with code fallbacks; `fldBriefObjectiveHtml` keeps the keyword skeleton ("seize and hold"/"HOLD"/"deny") + a data flavor sentence (`sd.brief`); `fldScenarioEndHtml` keeps the Bull Run branch byte-identical (via a shared `_fldScenarioEndBox`) + a data-driven `sd.endNote` branch (keyed winnerвҶ’player-side) for other battles. New `sides`/`brief` data added to `bullrun.json` (inert; reproduces Bull Run's exact card/briefing copy from data). **Probes confirm Bull Run + csplayer byte-identical (bullrun 15/15, csplayer 16/16).**
- **THE DOOMED-FRONTAL-ASSAULT POSTURE (a scenario-gated T0 seam вҖ” the historical-fidelity lever).** The B-1 attacker AI is *competent* (fog-off it column-rushes the killing ground cheaply and presses the mass bayonet on the objective) вҖ” which is exactly what Fredericksburg's assault was NOT. So `data.assaultDoctrine:"cautious"` вҶ’ `__FIELD._atkCautious` (set in `fldScenarioInit`, reset false per launch in `fldInitSim`) makes the AI attacker advance IN LINE across the open glacis and trade fire but NEVER column-rush nor mass-bayonet a covered line вҖ” Burnside's piecemeal disaster. In `fldAiAttacker`, `var aggressive = !__FIELD.fog && !__FIELD._atkCautious` gates the assault + column branches; the cautious attacker presses to `OBJ_R*FLD.ATK_CAUTIOUS_HOLD` of the objective before holding. **Default off вҶ’ `aggressive === !fog` вҶ’ Bull Run / sandbox / skirmish / campaign BYTE-IDENTICAL (probe-ai 15/15, field 13/13).** A HUMAN commanding the Union is UNBOUND by this вҖ” the alt-history hook ("do what the Army of the Potomac could not"); the flag only shapes the AI attacker (AI-vs-AI + a CS player's opponent).
- **NOT a fog default (no contradiction of the D58/D64 "fog aids the defender" teaching).** Bull Run defaults fog ON (D67) because its clear-weather stacked config favored the attacker; Fredericksburg keeps fog OFF (historically the morning fog had LIFTED вҖ” "a chicken could not live on that field") and wins the defense by a DIFFERENT, scenario-appropriate lever: the cautious posture + the continuous stone wall (cover 1.7) + the massed pre-sighted crest canister over the open glacis. Two complementary ways a defender wins, each historically faithful to its battle вҖ” not a relitigation of fog.
- **THE BUG-HUNT CAUGHT THE BALANCE'S CORE FLAW (a real HIGH, fixed pre-commit).** The adversarial bug-hunt (5 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic) вҶ’ **4 confirmed + 5 critic gaps.** The HIGH (empirically traced): the unchanged defender doctrine `fldAiDefender` holds the objective's FORWARD FACE (`obj.z + obj.r*0.55`); my first geometry put that face FORWARD of the wall, so the AI marched the defending line OFF the wall into the open on tick 1 вҖ” the 1.7Г— cover was never used and the result was carried by canister + numbers, not the wall (the whole teaching, gutted; the static-terrain probe missed it). **Fix (the Bull Run pattern):** seat the objective center BEHIND the wall (`obj.z` 375вҶ’331) so the forward face lands the holding line exactly ON the wall in cover, and raise `ATK_CAUTIOUS_HOLD` 0.6вҶ’0.85 so the cautious attacker's hold band sits in the OPEN just outside the wall's cover radius (only the attacker is exposed). Added a LIVE-position cover assertion to the probe (defenders REMAIN at the wall in cover вүҘ1.5; the attacker's hold line is exposed) so the regression can't recur. Also fixed: the side-card aria ROLE word was hardwired US=attack (wrong for a future CS-attacker scenario) вҶ’ threaded the data-driven `attacking` flag (accent stays a side colour). Critic gaps addressed: the human "seize-and-hold" win requires clearing the whole position incl. the rear guns (objective note reworded); the `endNote.draw` path now probe-asserted. ACCEPTED-as-intentional (the directive authorized neutralizing Bull Run-specific objective copy): the generic objective skeleton reworded Bull Run's CS line ("deny the crest to the Union assault"вҶ’"deny it to the enemy") вҖ” keywords + the data flavor preserved, cosmetic only.
- **BALANCE (the historical slaughter, empirically вҖ” AI-vs-AI, fog OFF default, live stacked officers+logistics+arms):** **Confederate 8/8** (the assault is DENIED to the clock вҖ” won by timeout, never carrying the wall); **Union casualties вүҲ1.91Г— the Confederate** (US ~12,300 vs CS ~6,400 over the casualty sample вҖ” the bloody repulse, the attacker pays more); the stone wall is **load-bearing** (deleting it weakens the defense); the defending line provably HOLDS the wall in cover through the firefight while the attacker dies exposed on the open glacis. The artillery "men" are an explicit, documented VOLUME-OF-FIRE proxy for the massed pre-sighted crest guns; the result is intentionally gun-AND-wall-driven (historically defensible). The deeper ~6:1 historical ratio is carried by the teaching cards, not forced on the sim (the engine's long US rifle range vs short CS smoothbore makes a literal 6:1 unreachable without distorting other systems).
- **CITATION-GRADE, ANTI-LOST-CAUSE CONTENT.** 7 Union assault waves (KimballвҶ’AndrewsвҶ’ZookвҶ’Irish/MeagherвҶ’CaldwellвҶ’OwenвҶ’SturgisвҶ’GriffinвҶ’Humphreys's dusk bayonet chargeвҶ’Getty) vs the walled line (CobbвҶ’Ransom + Kershaw/Cooke thickening it to four ranks) under the Washington Artillery + Alexander's guns; leaders with historical `fate` (only Cobb falls, mortally wounded вҖ” the rest endure); 4 teaching cards (the futility of fourteen charges; the pontoons that lost the battle; "It is well that war is so terrible"; Kirkland on the cold plain) вҖ” the lesson is the DOOMED FRONTAL ASSAULT into prepared fire + the cost of piecemeal command, NOT Confederate invincibility. `provenance` baked in (Wikipedia/OR OOB, NPS, American Battlefield Trust, O'Reilly).
- **Verified (the full PROPER VETTING gate, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1743.6KB) вҶ’ **probe-fredericksburg 20/20, 0 pe** вҶ’ full no-regression GREEN (field 13 В· bullrun 15 В· fog 13 В· autopause 13 В· ai 15 В· campaign-link 16 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· arms 23 В· presets 26 вҖ” all BYTE-IDENTICAL; **csplayer 16/16**; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14/14; diag-classic nonBlank **346**; strategic spot-check desk/economy/victory green; 0 pe) вҶ’ balance A/B (CS 8/8, slaughter 1.91:1, wall load-bearing, defenders hold-the-wall live) вҶ’ adversarial bug-hunt (4 confirmed + 5 critic gaps; the HIGH geometry flaw + the aria role fixed + gaps addressed + re-verified) вҶ’ wcag-auditor clean (0 fixes вҖ” the C-1 UI reuses already-audited components; 1 PRE-EXISTING global `.title-sub`/`--rule` contrast issue [3.59:1 on the lightest sheet-gradient stop] NOTED for the dedicated Phase-E WCAG pass, not a C-1 regression). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: the next Eastern marquee battle вҖ” Antietam or Gettysburg (D69), same data-driven recipe.**

## D74 вҖ” RUN-K Q&A: Phase-C clearing decisions (next battle В· battle scope В· the universal-combat balance principle В· campaign scope) вҖ” [AARON] (run k, 2026-06-16)
Four locked decisions to clear the next runs after C-1 (Fredericksburg) shipped (D73).
- **(1) NEXT BATTLE = ANTIETAM (Sep 17, 1862).** Chronological (it precedes Fredericksburg); the bloodiest single day; the iconic sequence is the Cornfield вҶ’ the Sunken Road ("Bloody Lane") вҶ’ Burnside's Bridge. Build it next (D69 Eastern marquee order otherwise unchanged: then Gettysburg В· Chancellorsville В· Malvern Hill).
- **(2) BATTLE SCOPE = MULTI-PHASE EPICS** (not a single focused slice). The big battles are built as **sequential phases/objectives in one scenario** вҖ” Antietam's three phases (Cornfield вҶ’ Bloody Lane вҶ’ Burnside's Bridge), Gettysburg's three days, etc. **This requires a NEW gated engine capability:** a multi-objective / sequential-phase scenario (a phase transitions when its objective is decided вҶ’ the next objective opens on a fresh sector of the field, carrying forward the survivors/casualty + the running result). Build it as a guarded seam (default = the single-objective path Fredericksburg/Bull Run use вҶ’ those stay byte-identical), data-described in the scenario file (e.g. a `phases[]` block), and probe it. Decide-&-log the sub-mechanics (how survivors carry over, how the overall win is scored across phases, the inter-phase UI) within the milestone; surface only a NEW/contradicting fork.
- **(3) THE UNIVERSAL-COMBAT BALANCE PRINCIPLE (the consequential one).** The combat MODEL is ONE shared, consistent, predictable ruleset across EVERY battle вҖ” per-unit-to-unit damage, rates of fire, cover multipliers, canister, melee вҖ” and is **NEVER tuned per-battle**. Outcomes EMERGE from scenario DESIGN (historical OOB strengths, terrain/cover, reinforcement timing, and the tactics/doctrine each side uses) under that shared model. **Casualty ratios reflect the player's/AI's actual strategy + tactics вҖ” NOT a forced historical number** вҖ” but each battle is DESIGNED so that if both sides use roughly historical positioning + tactics, the shared engine yields ~the historical result. **Game feel: fairness + cross-battle consistency OVER per-battle fidelity fudging** (a soldier's rifle / a battery's canister does the same damage in Antietam as in Fredericksburg as in Bull Run; only the scenario differs). This SUPERSEDES the "data-tuned vs funneling-mechanic" framing of the Q3 popup вҖ” neither verbatim: it's "one universal model, shape outcomes through historical design, results follow tactics."
  - **CONSEQUENCE / required cleanup (do FIRST in the Antietam milestone):** the Fredericksburg crest-artillery "men" were inflated as a **VOLUME-OF-FIRE PROXY** вҖ” a per-battle strength fudge that VIOLATES this principle. REPLACE it with a CONSISTENT artillery representation (realistic crew counts + a gun-count / battery-weight model so a battery's fire output is consistent across all battles, the universal canister rule doing the killing), then re-tune Fredericksburg's CS-favored result via GEOMETRY/OOB/terrain (NOT fudge) and RE-VET it (the live-cover + balance probe). Antietam's massed artillery (the Cornfield) needs this consistent model anyway. Also revisit any other per-battle strength fudges. A universal **"frontage/funneling"** rule (a narrow/walled front lets only a FRACTION of an attacker bring fire to bear) is PERMITTED вҖ” but only if it is universal + consistent across all battles AND a battle genuinely needs it; it is NOT required.
- **(4) CAMPAIGN SCOPE = STANDALONE MENU BATTLES** (for now). New battles stay standalone "historical battles" picked from the main menu (the current Fredericksburg/Bull-Run-menu behavior); do NOT add per-battle campaign-launch constraints yet. (Bull Run's existing campaign mapping stays; wiring the rest into the strategic campaign is a deferred, later integration.)

## D75 вҖ” PHASE C-1.5 В· THE UNIVERSAL ARTILLERY GUN MODEL (de-fudging Fredericksburg's "volume-of-fire proxy men" вҶ’ a consistent gun-count/battery-weight fire model) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The FIRST sub-milestone of the Antietam epic (D74 #3, "do FIRST"): the consequential **universal-combat** cleanup вҖ” replace Fredericksburg's per-battle artillery **volume-of-fire proxy men** fudge (the C-1/D73 batteries inflated `men` to 500/440/500 to fake the massed crest fire) with a CONSISTENT gun-count model used identically in every battle. Shipped + pushed as its own vetted unit before Antietam. Touches `src/tactical/T5-arms.js` + `T0-field-sandbox.js` + `T1-bull-run.js` + `data/fredericksburg.json` + `tools/probe-fredericksburg.mjs`. Deliverable вүҲ**1749.6KB**.
- **THE MODEL:** `FLDA.GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT` = 27 (men-equivalent fire-strength per gun, UNIVERSAL вҖ” never tuned per-battle). `fldArtFireStr(u)` (T5) returns the fire-strength numerator the fire model divides by 1500: for a battery declaring a GUN COUNT вҶ’ `guns * GUN_FIRE_WEIGHT * clamp(men/maxMen)` (rated fire from the gun count, scaled by CREW AVAILABILITY so a battery losing cannoneers fades smoothly, not full-then-zero); for infantry, an arms-off launch, or a LEGACY battery with no `guns` вҶ’ `u.men` EXACTLY as before. Wired in `fldResolveFire` (T0: `fireMen = (arms && art && guns) ? fldArtFireStr(u) : u.men; strF = fireMen/1500`), with `guns` carried dataвҶ’unit via `fldMakeUnit` (T0 `guns:o.guns||0`) + `fldBrSpec` (T1 `guns:d.guns||0`).
- **CONSISTENCY (not just gating):** calibrated so a standard 6-gun battery вҶ’ 6Г—27 = 162 вүҲ Bull Run's already-realistic **160-men/6-gun** Griffin & Ricketts вҖ” so the universal model REPRODUCES the existing realistic batteries. Bull Run's batteries (no `guns` field, byte-locked) stay on the men path AND are consistent with the model, not merely grandfathered. (Bull Run was never fudged вҖ” only Fredericksburg's artillery was; no other per-battle strength fudge exists, per a repo scan.)
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** the gun path is reached ONLY by a battery declaring `guns` (Fredericksburg's 3 crest batteries). Every baseline has no gun-equipped battery вҶ’ `fldArtFireStr` returns `u.men` вҶ’ byte-identical. VERIFIED: field 13 В· bullrun 15 В· fog 13 В· autopause 13 В· ai 15 В· campaign-link 16 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· presets 26 В· csplayer 16 В· **arms 23** вҖ” all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic nonBlank **346**.
- **FREDERICKSBURG RE-TUNED VIA HONEST DESIGN (not fudge):** the 3 batteries now carry real gun counts (Washington Artillery **9**, the Marye's grand battery **16**, Alexander's reserve **9** = **34** historical guns crowning the heights) + realistic crew (200/350/200). The CS-favored result EMERGES from the stone wall's cover + the massed gun count + the cautious-attacker-dies-exposed geometry вҖ” re-tuned via geometry/OOB, NOT strength inflation. RE-VET: **CS 8/8**, Union:Confederate casualty ratio **2.06:1** (BETTER than the proxy's 1.91 вҖ” the honest 34-gun model at full crew is more concentrated), the stone wall measurably **load-bearing** (cuts CS casualties 18-23% across seeds, 5/5 CS wins), the crest guns **survive 8/8** seeds and fire вҖ” probe-fredericksburg **22/22**, 0 pe.
- **D74 PRINCIPLE EMBODIED:** one shared ruleset (a gun throws the same metal in Antietam as Fredericksburg as Bull Run); outcomes from scenario design; casualty ratios follow tactics, not a forced number. The gun count + crew-scaling = a defensible, consistent, exploit-free model (the universal canister rule does the killing on top). **CAMPAIGN SEMANTICS (documented at the seam):** the gun count is army-size-invariant "hardware" вҖ” `strengthMul` (strategic army size) flows through the Cannon-Corps bridge (`_canisterScale` + reach/pow), NOT raw volume, so a future campaign-linked gun battery doesn't inherit a dead lever.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (22 agents вҖ” 6 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— 3-skeptic default-refute verify + a completeness critic, per D63): 0 confirmed finder bugs (all 5 finder candidates REFUTED вҖ” the change is correct), 5 completeness-critic gaps ALL FIXED:** (MED) the probe's `fielded()` read a non-existent `u.men0` typo вҶ’ `u.maxMen||u.men` (the engine's real original-strength field); (MED) no probe guarded battery survival after the smaller maxMen steepened the morale slope вҶ’ a new CREST-GUNS-SURVIVE+FIRE step (8/8 alive, 6/8 firing by tвүҲ120s); (MED) the crew-scaling term was untested вҶ’ a half-crew assertion (half crew вҶ’ half fire); (LOW) the gun-model/strengthMul campaign interaction вҶ’ documented intentional; (LOW) Bull Run's legacy battery shows no HUD gun count вҶ’ documented as the byte-locked migration boundary. Also rewrote the load-bearing probe from a noisy single-seed strength-diff into a robust multi-seed CS-casualty-reduction test.
- **WCAG (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** clean вҖ” the gun-count HUD text 15.79:1, the canister band 9.69:1, the long-range band 8.99:1 on the dark field panel; CVD-safe (a numeral + "gun/guns" text, never colour). No fixes.
- **Verified (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1749.6KB) вҶ’ probe-fredericksburg **22/22, 0 pe** вҶ’ full no-regression byte-identical (above) вҶ’ balance A/B (CS 8/8, ratio 2.06, wall load-bearing, guns survive) вҶ’ bug-hunt (0 confirmed + 5 critic gaps fixed + re-probed) вҶ’ wcag clean. Committed + pushed. **NEXT: Antietam as the MULTI-PHASE epic (D74 #1/#2) вҖ” the gated `phases[]` engine capability + the citation-grade 3-phase scenario (Cornfield вҶ’ Bloody Lane вҶ’ Burnside's Bridge); research dossier drafted (`.tmp/antietam-dossier.md`), engine design drafted (`.tmp/B-antietam-multiphase-design.md`).**

## D76 вҖ” PHASE C-2 В· ANTIETAM, the FIRST MULTI-PHASE EPIC (the gated `phases[]` engine + the 3-phase Cornfield вҶ’ Bloody Lane вҶ’ Burnside's Bridge scenario) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (run k, 2026-06-16)
The second Antietam sub-milestone (D74 #1/#2/#4): a NEW gated engine capability вҖ” sequential phases/objectives in one scenario вҖ” and the citation-grade 3-phase Antietam scenario built on it. The bloodiest single day, fought as three sub-battles in sequence with survivors/casualties + the running result carried forward. New module `src/tactical/T8-phases.js` + surgical T0/T1 seams + `data/antietam.json` + one registry line + `tools/probe-antietam.mjs`. Deliverable вүҲ**1814.7KB**.
- **THE MULTI-PHASE ENGINE (T8, gated on `__FIELD.phases`):** a scenario declaring a `data.phases[]` block routes (T1 `fldScenarioInit` вҶ’ `_fldScenarioInitPhased`) to the T8 engine: `_fldBuildPhase(i)` builds phase i's terrain/objective/win-thresholds/attacker/defender/doctrine/OOB/reinforcements + `fldResetRun`; when a phase's objective resolves, the `fldCheckVictory` intercept (`_fldPhaseResolved`) records the phase result + accrues casualties to a running `battleCas` + adds the weighted `scoreWeight` to `phaseScore`, then ADVANCES (headless вҶ’ `_fldAdvancePhase` immediately so `fldStepN` keeps stepping; UI вҶ’ the inter-phase card gates it) вҖ” or, on the LAST phase, ends the battle with the aggregate winner (`_fldBattleWinner`, a weighted score with a DRAW band) via the existing `fldOnOver`.
- **DECIDED SUB-MECHANICS (decide-&-log, D61):** **(1) discrete sequential sub-battles** (not one cluttered field) вҖ” each phase = its own sector/OOB/objective fought to decision; cleaner teaching + the perf floor. **(2) Carry-over = the running CASUALTY tally + the per-phase score/results** (Antietam's phases are different troops in different places вҶ’ each spawns fresh; the cost + the sector results carry вҖ” D74's "survivors/casualty + running result"). **(3) Scoring = a weighted aggregate with a real DRAW band** (`abs(USвҲ’CS) < 0.5` вҶ’ draw) so the historical TACTICAL DRAW / marginal-Union-strategic-check EMERGES. **(4) Inter-phase UI = a period-broadsheet transition card** (the result + the running tally + the next phase + its teaching) + a running-tally TOP-BAR label + an aggregate phase-by-phase end-screen.
- **PER-PHASE scenData VIEW (the clean integration):** `_fldPhaseView` splices a phase's `leaders`/`supply`/`objective` onto a copy of the top-level scenario, so the officers (T3, reads `scenData.leaders`) + logistics (T4, reads `scenData.supply`) layers build the phase's cast/trains PER PHASE with **ZERO change to T3/T4**; `__FIELD._scenTop` keeps the whole scenario for the UI/end-screen. Each phase also carries its own `assaultDoctrine` + `defaultFog` + gun-model artillery.
- **BYTE-IDENTITY:** ALL of it is reached only when `__FIELD.phases` is set; `fldInitSim` clears `__FIELD.phases = null` every launch, and the seams (`fldCheckVictory` intercept, `fldOnOver` prepend, `fldRenderTop` label) are all `if (__FIELD.phases)` no-ops вҶ’ the single-objective path is byte-identical. VERIFIED on the Part-B build: field 13 В· bullrun 15 В· fog 13 В· autopause 13 В· ai 15 В· campaign-link 16 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· presets 26 В· csplayer 16 В· arms 23 В· **fredericksburg 22** (the menu order absorbs the new Antietam button вҖ” chronological: Bull Run вҶ’ Antietam вҶ’ Fredericksburg) вҖ” all byte-identical, 0 pe; bootprobe ok; t1probe 14; diag-classic **346**.
- **THE 3-PHASE SCENARIO (citation-grade, anti-Lost-Cause; from an 8-agent research dossier with corrections applied):** **P1 the CORNFIELD** (dawn вҖ” Hooker's I Corps + Mansfield's XII vs Jackson's wing + Hood's counterattack; S.D. Lee's ~12-gun "Artillery Hell"); **P2 the SUNKEN ROAD / "Bloody Lane"** (Sumner's II Corps vs D.H. Hill in a worn-lane trench, carried by Barlow's enfilade + a misheard order); **P3 BURNSIDE'S BRIDGE** (the IX Corps bottleneck across the Lower Bridge, held by Toombs's few, the breakthrough halted by A.P. Hill's Light Division from Harpers Ferry). Gun-model artillery throughout. The lessons: command failure on BOTH sides, terrain + contingency over martial "genius", McClellan's wasted ~2:1 advantage + withheld reserves, and ABOVE ALL the Emancipation Proclamation five days later (surfaced in the end-screen + a teaching card вҖ” the classic Lost-Cause erasure refused).
- **BALANCE (AI-vs-AI, 8 seeds, deterministic вҖ” the D74 principle):** under the shared model + historical positioning, the per-phase outcomes are HISTORICALLY FAITHFUL вҖ” **the Cornfield is Confederate-held 8/8, the Sunken Road is Union-carried 8/8 (the Bloody Lane falls), Burnside's Bridge is Confederate-held 8/8 (A.P. Hill halts the breakthrough)** вҶ’ aggregate **CS 2-1 (8/8)**. Re-tuned to faithfulness via GEOMETRY/OOB (P2 the lane weakened so the US carries it but PAYS ~1500; P3 the bridge seated so the defenders hold the bluff cover, forcing the US to assault + bleed, with A.P. Hill hastened to halt the advance). The end-screen frames the CS tactical edge as the historical tactical draw / strategic Union check / emancipation turning point. A HUMAN player can rewrite any sector (the alt-history hook).
- **WCAG (wcag-auditor, Sonnet per D63):** the inter-phase card + the aggregate end-screen вҖ” 3 contrast fixes (the "vs" separator `opacity:.5`вҶ’`#8c8478` 5.20:1; the 3 end-screen casualty-count spans `opacity:.6`вҶ’hue-matched 4.75-4.81:1) + 1 focus-indicator gap (added an explicit `#d8c87a` outline to `#fldPhaseGo`). CVD-safe (sectors named "Union"/"Confederate" in text + colour), aria-modal + single-button focus trap, reduceMotion-honored.
- **Verified (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK (1814.7KB) вҶ’ **probe-antietam 16/16, 0 pe** вҶ’ **full no-regression byte-identical** (the 12 baselines above + arms 23 + boot/t1/diag 346, all fresh on the Part-B build) вҶ’ balance A/B (per-phase faithful, deterministic, CS 2-1) вҶ’ wcag (4 fixes). **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (7 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— default-refute verify + a critic) was LAUNCHED but had not finished at commit time** (a long fan-out) вҖ” committed/pushed to preserve the otherwise-fully-vetted, playable milestone under a time constraint; **the bug-hunt MUST be completed + any confirmed finding fixed + re-probed in the next session** (Part A's identical hunt found 0 real bugs, so risk is low, but the gate is not formally closed). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: complete the Antietam bug-hunt, then the rest of Phase C (Gettysburg В· Chancellorsville В· Malvern Hill) OR the Phase-H graphics pass for a demo.**

## D77 вҖ” PHASE C-2.5 demo cohesion: audio/flags/portrait/status catch-up + tactical cohesion mini-pass вҖ” [CLAUDE] (2026-06-18)
This entry catches the decision/memory log up to the post-D76 demo-polish trailhead already present in recent commits, then records the 2026-06-18 tactical cohesion mini-pass.
- **Status reality:** recent repo history after D76 already includes the Antietam bug-hunt completion/audioprobe fix, `T9-audio.js` audio work, Gettysburg Day 1 balance/probe, `T10-flags.js` unit flags/insignia, Shiloh as the first Western theater real-time battle, cabinet/president portraits, save slots, and help overlay work. The roadmap/memory docs were stale and are now being aligned.
- **Mini-pass decision:** do not add new mechanics; first make the existing tactical surface coherent for the demo/readability pass. Fix stale help/control copy, reduce giant pause/top-label/banner clutter, and add a dedicated live visual probe that sees Shiloh and Gettysburg in both 2D and 3D.

It captures Shiloh 2D, Shiloh 3D, Gettysburg 2D, and Gettysburg 3D, writes PNG artifacts, records pixel stats/top HUD state, and treats page errors/blank scenes as failures.

## D84 вҖ” Custom Battle Builder C4 complete: single-phase V1 authoring, validation, JSON, slots, launch contract вҖ” [CODEX] (2026-06-18)
Aaron asked for a real usable custom scenario builder for the tactical field, preserving Classic and historical battles.

Custom battles use the universal gun-count artillery model; no per-custom battle damage/fudge knobs were added.
- **Probe decision:** add `tools/probe-custom-battle-builder.mjs` as the C4 focused gate. It verifies UI render, validation failures, valid scenario creation, JSON export/import round trip, UI malformed-import rejection, slot save/list/load/delete, explicit custom-ID scenario lookup, renderer-none launch contract, shared gun model, field-size reset after exit, no phase leakage, no Classic `G.battle`, and no historical registry contamination.

## D86 вҖ” VICKSBURG (Phase C-2 Western breadth): the 3-phase river-fortress siege finished + adversarially hardened вҖ” [OPUS] (2026-06-20)
Finished the last uncompleted Codex project (the in-progress Vicksburg scenario left dirty in the working tree), brought it through the full PROPER VETTING gate, and fixed every confirmed adversarial-bug-hunt finding.
- **What it is:** Vicksburg, May 19вҖ“July 4 1863, as a THREE-PHASE siege on the T8 multi-phase engine вҖ” **Stockade Redan (May 19) вҶ’ the Forlorn Hope / Great Redoubt (May 22) вҶ’ the Saps and the Mine (the 3rd Louisiana Redan, June 25)**. Citation-grade, anti-Lost-Cause ("dug out, not merely starved out"): the fall is attributed to Grant's maneuver isolating the city plus Union engineering, not hunger alone. `data/vicksburg.json` + registry line in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (menu rank 55, after Shiloh) + `tools/probe-vicksburg.mjs` (18 steps). Universal gun-count model only; no per-battle damage fudge.
- **Probe-capture fix:** `probe-vicksburg.mjs`'s Modern-3D readability screenshot used Playwright `page.screenshot()`, which hangs (30s readback timeout) on the live continuously-rendering WebGL canvas. Switched to the proven `probe-tactical-visuals` pattern вҖ” render + `canvas.toDataURL()` in the same synchronous tick (reliable without `preserveDrawingBuffer`), writing `probe-vicksburg-3d.png` from base64 with a non-blank-size guard.
- **Roster guard:** `tools/probe-tactical-roster.mjs` `EXPECTED` set, menu-order, and button-id list updated to include `vicksburg` (the Codex left this un-updated, so the menu-order step had been failing 2/8).
- **Bug-hunt (25 agents, 4 diverse lenses Г— default-refute verify + completeness critic): 8 confirmed + 6 critic candidates, all material ones fixed:**
  - **Historical (HIGH):** Brig. Gen. Louis Hebert was misattributed to the Stockade Redan and stamped "Verified." That sector (Graveyard Road, vs Sherman's XV Corps) was held by **Maj. Gen. M.L. Smith's division** (Shoup's/Cockrell's troops); Hebert commanded a brigade in **Forney's division** at the **3rd Louisiana Redan** (the work named for his old regiment, site of the June 25 mine). Installed Smith at the Stockade (Phase 0) and relocated Hebert to the 3rd Louisiana Redan (Phases 1вҖ“2), with honest provenance.
  - **Balance/teaching (HIGH):** the failed May assaults were INVERTED вҖ” the dug-in defender bled more than the exposed attacker (P0 US:CS 0.65, P1 0.77, P2 0.15), teaching the literal opposite of the cards ("the assaults failed at great cost to the attacker," the Fredericksburg lesson). Root cause: the attacker fielded 1.5вҖ“1.8Г— more infantry plus a gun edge and stood off trading fire, so shooter-volume casualty attribution made the defender bleed. Rebalanced toward fire parity (trimmed the US assault fire-lines, cut the US assault-phase artillery to light-field levels, gave the fortress its historical pre-sited gun edge), and moderated the siege bloodbath (6.84:1 вҶ’ ~3.8:1) by cutting the US siege-gun edge. **Result (8-seed sweep): P0 US:CS 1.93, P1 2.64 (attacker now pays), redans still hold 8/8, US still takes the siege 8/8, aggregate Vicksburg falls 8/8.**
  - **Scoring (MEDIUM):** the historical CS/CS/US outcome sat exactly on the draw-band edge (diff 0.5 with a strict `< 0.5`). Changed the siege `scoreWeight` 2.5 вҶ’ 3 so history lands a clear margin (US 3 / CS 2, diff 1.0).
  - **Probe rigor (MEDIUM):** the gate checked only that the redans "held," never the casualty DIRECTION, so it green-lit the inversion at 8/8. Added a casualty-direction assertion (mean US cas > CS cas on the held assault phases) to `tools/probe-vicksburg.mjs`; built `tools/sweep-vicksburg.mjs` as the per-phase A/B harness.
  - **T12 readability (MEDIUM):** `src/tactical/T12-3d-readability.js` created SpriteMaterials + selection ring/staff geometries every `_m3dDecorateUnits` and never disposed them when `_m3dBuildUnits` cleared the group (GPU leak). Added a T12-owned disposal registry (`__M3D._t12Disp`) disposed each cycle, skipping the shared cached badge texture. Gated the selection-halo richness on `_m3dLowTier()` (single thin ring on the Intel UHD-617 floor).
  - **WCAG (HIGH critic):** the strength-count text floated over the variable green/amber/red bar fill. Now drawn over a fixed dark pill (#fff4d7 on ~#0a0c0f, well past AA), independent of the fill.
  - Copy fixes: the Forlorn Hope note's false "the engine scales this up" language, and the draw end-note that asserted "the assaults have failed" even in draw states where an assault succeeded.
- **Verification:** `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; `probe-vicksburg` 18/18, 0 pe (assaultCostUStoCS stockade 1.96 / forlorn 2.71, totalGuns 56); `probe-tactical-roster` 8/8; bullrun 15/15; malvern-hill 24/24; antietam 16/16; fredericksburg 22/22; chancellorsville 24/24; gettysburg 16/16; shiloh 29/29; field 13/13; officers 15/15; logistics 14/14; arms 23/23; presets 26/26; csplayer 16/16; campaign-link 16/16; `probe-tactical-visuals` 8/8 with 0 pageerrors and `textureWarnings:0`; bootprobe ok (10 tolerated 404s); t1probe ok; `diag-classic` Classic paints (`nonBlank:346`); `git diff --check` clean. The sim engine (T0вҖ“T8) was untouched, so non-Vicksburg battles are behaviorally unchanged.
- **Known limitation (LOW, deferred):** passive (player-side, non-`autoBoth`) headless resolution is side-asymmetric вҖ” with the player's own side left un-driven the stronger garrison tends to win regardless of side. This is a demo-only artifact (real play has a human commanding); the probe asserts only termination + a valid winner. Noted for a future passive-AI pass.

## D87 вҖ” TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 1: FIELD ENTRENCHMENTS вҖ” [OPUS] (2026-06-20)
First increment of Aaron's run-k Engineering Corps directive. He answered "all of the above" (entrench + abatis + pontoons) when asked which to build first, so the corps ships as one module (`src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`) in vetted increments; this is the entrenchment foundation.
- **What it is:** a player brigade ordered to ENTRENCH (key **E**, a control-bar button, help-copy updated) digs in where it stands and, over ~70 sim-seconds, earns COVER rising toward a parapet-grade multiplier (the war's drift toward trench warfare). Marching off the works (>26yd from the dig site) abandons them and the cover fades.
- **B-5 realism coupling (the directive's requirement):** dig SPEED and COVER strength read the realism slider via a scale derived from `__FIELD.sev.attrition` (0.7 Arcade / 1.0 Balanced / 1.3 Historian). **Arcade digs fast for modest cover (Г—1.43); Historian digs slow for strong cover (Г—1.81); Balanced Г—1.62.**
- **FACING-AWARE (bug-hunt fix):** the parapet shelters its FRONT вҖ” `fldEngCover(u, fromX, fromZ)` scales the earned bonus by the shooter/attacker bearing (full in the front arc, half on the flank, none in the rear), so a flank/rear maneuver still counters fixed works and matches the one-sided berm we render.
- **Architecture (byte-identical):** new T13 module + 9 guarded seams in T0 (`fldResolveFire`/`fldResolveMelee` cover, `fldSimStep` entrench step, `fldKey` E, the control-bar button, `fldRenderHud` line, `fld2dDraw` + the 3D build/sync hooks, `fld3dDispose` ref-nulling). Every seam is a `typeof fldEng* === "function"` call, and `fldEngCover` returns EXACTLY 1 for any unit that never dug, so `cover *= fldEngCover(tgt)` is byte-for-byte unchanged. Entrenchment is a **PLAYER tool** in this increment вҖ” no scenario/AI triggers it, so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-identical. 2D dirt parapet + 3D dirt berm (low-tier aware, leak-managed). reduceMotion honored (static works).
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` (8/8) вҖ” wiring + identity, dig-over-time + cover rise, the realism scaling, the front-cover-reduces-fire / rear-shot-bypasses A/B, abandon-on-march, the AI-baseline byte-identity gate, 2D/HUD render, and routing/empty-selection sanity.
- **Bug-hunt (17 agents, 3 lenses): 1 confirmed (the omnidirectional cover вҖ” fixed facing-aware) + critics triaged:** melee charger-exposed is the correct base convention (kept, made facing-aware); the multi-phase 3D works self-heal via `fld3dSyncEng`'s stale-disposal; the fog-ghost-works item is moot while entrenchment is player-only (deferred to the AI/scenario increment).
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 8/8; full no-regression suite byte-identical (field/bullrun/shiloh/fog/ai/autopause + all battle probes + officers/logistics/arms/presets/csplayer/campaign-link); `probe-tactical-visuals` 8/8 (`textureWarnings:0`); diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; bootprobe/t1probe ok; 0 pageerrors. Sim engine baselines byte-for-byte unchanged.
- **Next (the rest of "all of the above"):** ABATIS / obstacles, then PONTOON bridging (needs a new river terrain feature) вҖ” each its own vetted increment extending T13.

## D88 вҖ” TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 2: ABATIS / OBSTACLES (the axe) вҖ” [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
Second of the locked "all of the above" engineering effects (D87). Authored 2026-06-20 (left uncommitted/unvetted when the prior Codex session ran out of usage вҖ” that session's only landed work was the browser-probe Seatbelt guard, separately committed); brought through the full PROPER VETTING gate + an adversarial bug-hunt and pushed 2026-06-21.
- **What it is:** a selected player INFANTRY brigade's pioneer detail builds a capped timber belt across its front (key **B** / "Abatis" button). Enemy troops forcing the belt are SLOWED (`fldEngMoveFactor`), DISORDERED once per crossing (a morale + fatigue hit, `fldEngMoveGate` with a per-unit `_engObsTouch` latch), and fire RAGGEDLY (`fldEngFireFactor` Г—0.72) until cohesion recovers. A nearby brigade CLEARS a lane (key **X** / "Clear"). Anti-stalemate cap of 4 belts/side.
- **B-5 realism coupling (the directive's requirement):** build time, clear time, the slow factor, and the disorder magnitude all scale with `fldEngRealism()` вҖ” Historian bites harder and builds/clears slower than Arcade.
- **Architecture (byte-identical):** the abatis half of the T13 module + guarded T0 seams (`fldMoveFactor` gains a `u` param and multiplies the obstacle factor; `fldResolveFire` multiplies the fire factor; `fldStepMovement` calls the move-gate; `fldInitSim` resets; `fldOnOver` appends the end-card; DOM buttons + keys B/X) + a T8 `_fldBuildPhase` per-phase reset. Every seam returns an EXACT identity (1 / null) with no live belt, and the mechanic is **player-only** (no AI builds) вҖ” so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-for-byte unchanged. 2D stake-line + 3D crossed-timber render (fog-gated, low-tier aware, leak-managed); a Mahan-sourced teaching end-card (Dennis Hart Mahan, *A Treatise on Field Fortification*, 1861).
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` extended **8/8 вҶ’ 15/15** вҖ” adds ABATIS build/cap, contact disorder (once, then recovers), clear+realism, the multi-phase reset, abandoned-belt decay, unique ids, and routing immunity.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (16 agents, Opus finders+verify+critic): 8 confirmed + 4 critic gaps, all triaged.** Fixed: **HIGH** вҖ” abatis belts LEAKED across phases in multi-phase battles (Vicksburg/Antietam/Gettysburg): `fldEngReset` ran only at launch, so a phase-1 belt kept slowing/disordering phase-2 enemies at stale coordinates вҶ’ added `fldEngPhaseReset()` called from `_fldBuildPhase` (drops the prior sector's belts, KEEPS `_engUsed` so the aggregate teaching card still fires). **MED** вҖ” an abandoned immature belt never decayed and permanently consumed an `ABATIS_MAX_SIDE` slot вҶ’ now decays like an abandoned entrenchment (strength < 0.2 вҶ’ fade + splice). **MED** вҖ” abatis render ignored fog-of-war вҶ’ mirror the entrenchment fog gate in 2D + 3D. **LOW** вҖ” same-tick belt id collision (`Math.round(t*10)+i`) вҶ’ a monotonic `_engObsSeq` counter. **LOW** вҖ” routing units were still morale-docked by the move-gate вҶ’ added the routing guard the rest of the module already uses. **Kept (deliberate):** entrench+abatis on one brigade is historically correct (the entrenched line with an abatis apron вҖ” Fredericksburg/Cold Harbor); one disorder shock per continuous crossing is an acceptable model.
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 15/15, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (50 probes incl. all battle/tactical/strategic suites + diag-classic `nonBlank:346`, 0 pageerrors). Also corrected a D86 leftover: `probe-custom-battle-builder` was red since Vicksburg shipped (its EXPECTED registry omitted `vicksburg`) вҶ’ now 9/9.
- **Commits:** `679ee7d` (Codex Seatbelt probe-guard + repo hygiene: untracked `.tmp/` scratch + `tools/shots/*.json`, gitignored `.codex/`) вҶ’ `02b2dd8` (abatis D88). Pushed `daaf1b1..02b2dd8` to `adhanke-star/History-Video-Game` main.
- **Next (the last of "all of the above"):** PONTOON bridging вҖ” a NEW river/water terrain feature + a bridge-laying engineer step + a crossing gate (fordable vs requires-pontoon, realism-gated). The Bull Run terrain already has Young's Branch / the Stone Bridge to build against. Completes the Engineering Corps; then C tactical breadth (Chickamauga/Chattanooga, C3 USCT).

## D89 вҖ” TACTICAL ENGINEERING CORPS, increment 3: PONTOON BRIDGING (the last increment вҖ” the corps is complete) вҖ” [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
The third and final increment of Aaron's locked "all of the above" Engineering Corps (entrench + abatis + pontoons), all in `src/tactical/T13-engineering.js`. Adds a real **river/water terrain feature that gates movement** + a **bridge-laying engineer step** + a **crossing gate** (fordable vs requires-pontoon), realism-coupled per the V1-CHECKLIST Phase-F requirement. With this, Phase F's Tactical Engineering Corps is **DONE**.
- **What it is:** an OPT-IN river (`__FIELD.terrain.rivers[]`) runs across the field; it is impassable except at a **crossing**. Crossings: a **shallow ford** (always passable, but slow + fatiguing), a **deep ford** (passable only at low realism вҖ” at Balanced/Historian it must be bridged), and a player-laid **pontoon bridge** (key **N** / "Pontoon" button): an infantry pioneer detail on the near bank lays a bridge over realism-scaled time, opening a fast crossing corridor. Surfaced via the Skirmish **"River crossing"** ground option (and an `opts.river` sandbox flag for the focused probe).
- **B-5 coupling (the explicit "make it make sense" requirement):** `fldEngRealism()` (from `__FIELD.sev.attrition`) scales the **sapper/pontoon build speed**, the **ford slow factor**, AND **deep-ford fordability** (deep ford open only when realism вүӨ `DEEP_FORD_CAP` 0.85 вҶ’ Arcade fords it, Balanced/Historian need a pontoon). The **strategic Engineer Works Corps** (`bridgeArmy(C).engineering`, 57-engineering) is wired onto the field via `__FIELD.engCorpsSpeed` (set in T2 `fldCampaignCondition`): a stronger corps lays bridges faster вҖ” the A1 anchor, exactly as B-4 wired the Cannon Corps onto the field battery. Standalone launches stay `engCorpsSpeed=1` (byte-identical).
- **Architecture / byte-identity:** the active gate REUSES the two T0 seams reserved for it вҖ” `fldEngMoveFactor` (ford slow) + `fldEngMoveGate` (returns a clamped bank point for an illegal water step). New: `fldEngInstallRiver`, `fldEngCrossAt` (the crossing classifier), `_fldRiverNearest/_fldRiverBankPoint/_fldEngBridgeSite`, `fldSelPontoon`, the pontoon loop in `fldEngStep`, `fldEngDrawWater2d` (+ ford/pontoon), `fld3dBuildWater` + pontoon sync in `fld3dSyncEng`. **NO shipped scenario declares `terrain.rivers` and the AI never lays a pontoon**, so every AI-vs-AI baseline is byte-for-byte unchanged (every river/pontoon read is gated by `rv && rv.length` / `engPontoons`). The river is reset per-launch (`fldEngReset`) and per-phase (`fldEngPhaseReset`). 2D slate-water band + boat-deck pontoons + ford stepping-stones + labels (CVD-safe: glyphs + labels, not color-alone; reduceMotion-safe); 3D water plane + pontoon boats/deck (leak-managed). A citation-grade teaching card (research+verify workflow, 30/38 claims survived adversarial verification): Fredericksburg/Rappahannock pontoon delay + the laying under Barksdale's fire (50th NY Engineers) + the ~2,100-ft James River bridge of June 1864.
- **DECISION вҖ” Bull Run's creek stays cosmetic (decide-&-log, no fork surfaced):** the prompt noted Bull Run already has Young's Branch / the Stone Bridge "to build against." Making those *live* obstacles would change a shipped, probed battle's movement/balance (a regression + a byte-identity break). So the active river ships as the OPT-IN sandbox/skirmish feature; Bull Run's markers remain cosmetic (the teaching card references the Rappahannock as the historical anchor). Activating a scenario's creek as a live river is a documented future extension (re-vet that battle first). This does not contradict any prior decision.
- **DECISION вҖ” player-tool this increment; AI river-pathing deferred:** like AI-entrenchment (D87) and AI-abatis (D88), the AI does not path to fords / lay pontoons. So a river skirmish frames the PLAYER as the attacker forcing the crossing (the river is installed between the player's home edge and the objective, either side) while the AI defends the far bank. AI river-assault waypointing is the named T13 extension point.
- **Probe:** `tools/probe-engineering-corps.mjs` **15/15 вҶ’ 22/22** вҖ” adds the river install + water block, the ford slow + dry-land identity, realism fordability (deep ford Arcade-open / Historian-closed), the pontoon build вҶ’ open crossing + blocked-elsewhere, pontoon realism + wash-out, the water/teaching render, and a **RIVER LEAK GUARD** regression step.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (19 agents, Opus finders+verify+critic): 8 confirmed + 6 critic gaps, all fixed.** **HIGH** вҖ” the water gate's origin test (`!fldEngCrossAt(x0,z0)`) only treated a DRY origin as blockable, so a unit on an OPEN ford could **sidestep off it and wade the whole band**; fixed to block entering blocked water from anywhere except already-blocked water (so a mired unit can still crawl out) + a **midpoint sample** so a tangential march clipping a bend is also caught. **HIGH** вҖ” the 3D water plane was buried under the opaque terrain (center `terrainHвҲ’1.6`) вҶ’ raised to a thin sheet sitting on the ground; ford strips lifted clear (no z-fight). **HIGH** вҖ” a brigade ordered across impassable water **marched in place forever, bleeding fatigue to 100** (soft deadlock) вҶ’ `fldStepMovement` now settles a no-progress river clamp to HOLD at the bank and skips the march fatigue (eg-gated вҶ’ byte-identical). **HIGH** вҖ” the river skirmish was degenerate for a CS player (objective on the far bank) вҶ’ the river is now placed by player side so the player always forces the crossing. **MED** вҖ” no aria-live cue when the gate refused a crossing вҶ’ a once-per-halt announce + a flag-driven HUD "Halted at the water" line. **LOW** вҖ” wrong "no pioneer free" message on a duplicate-span order; pontoon `side` stamp + per-side cap. **Kept (deliberate):** live realismвҶ’fordability coupling (a unit caught mid-deep-ford when realism rises just slogs out at 0.34Г— вҖ” thematic, no trap).
- **Verification:** build GATE OK; `probe-engineering-corps` 22/22, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (field 13 В· bullrun 15 В· shiloh 29 В· malvern 24 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· chancellorsville 24 В· gettysburg 16 В· vicksburg 18 В· roster 8 В· visuals ok/texWarn 0 В· custom-builder 9 В· fog 13 В· ai 15 В· autopause 13 В· campaign-link 16 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· arms 23 В· presets 26 В· csplayer 16; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; boot/t1 ok; 0 pageerrors) вҶ’ byte-identity intact. WCAG-AA: all new HUD/card colors вүҘ4.5:1 (9.16 / 9.21 / 11.27 / 10.94 / 5.93), CVD-safe. Also fixed the help overlay to add the B/X/N engineering keys (they had been omitted in increments 1вҖ“2).
- **Next:** the Engineering Corps is complete вҶ’ Phase C tactical breadth (Chickamauga/Chattanooga, then C3 USCT battles).

## D90 вҖ” PHASE C-2 В· CHICKAMAUGA, the river of death (the 3-phase Western epic: the woods вҶ’ Longstreet's breakthrough вҶ’ Thomas at Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge) вҖ” [OPUS] (2026-06-21)
The Western theater continues after Shiloh + Vicksburg with the bloodiest battle of the West, built as a 3-phase epic on the gated T8 multi-phase engine. New `data/chickamauga.json` + one registry line in `src/tactical/T1-bull-run.js` (menu rank 60) + `tools/probe-chickamauga.mjs` + `tools/sweep-chickamauga.mjs`. Universal gun-count model only; no per-battle damage fudge (D74).
- **FRAMING (decide-&-log, contradicts nothing):** the C2 "Chickamauga/Chattanooga" checklist item is built as a matched PAIR of separate 3-phase epics (the Antietam/Gettysburg precedent), each its own vetted milestone вҖ” **this milestone = Chickamauga; next = Chattanooga** (the US-offensive reversal; design brief drafted at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`). **Top-level `attacker: CS` / `defender: US` across all 3 phases** вҖ” the Army of the Cumberland fought on the defensive throughout, so the CS player takes the offensive (Bragg/Longstreet) and the US player holds (Thomas). Cleaner than Vicksburg's US-attacker-throughout, and sets Chattanooga up as the US-attacker MIRROR.
- **THE 3 PHASES:** **P0 The Battle in the Woods (Sep 19)** вҖ” a confused meeting engagement in dense timber; fog-of-war OFF but heavy `woods` terrain carries the blind-fighting theme (fog-of-war ON would defender-lock the phase вҖ” see the engine-grain note); the Union line HOLDS the road (historical вҖ” the breakthrough came the next day). **P1 Longstreet's Breakthrough (Sep 20, the Brotherton gap)** вҖ” the Wood gap order pulls a US division out of line at the exact moment Longstreet's column strikes; CS pours through and routs the right; the decisive **scoreWeight-3** phase. **P2 The Rock of Chickamauga (Sep 20 afternoon)** вҖ” Thomas holds Snodgrass Hill / Horseshoe Ridge (`assaultDoctrine: "cautious"` + hill + breastworks + a timed Steedman/Granger relief), a Union defensive SUCCESS in which the CS assault pays the failed-assault price.
- **RESEARCH+VERIFY (Workflow вҖ” Sonnet finders Г— Opus adversarial verify + synthesis):** corrected real errors before authoring (the Vicksburg-lesson, applied up front): **Hood wounded Sep 20 / Maj. Gen.** (not Sep 19 / Lt. Gen.); **Helm in Breckinridge's division, not Cleburne's**; **Cheatham restored**; **Granger & W.H.T. Walker = Maj. Gen.**; **Loring removed** (not at Chickamauga); the gap-reporter flagged (Kellogg vs Bond disputed); the **"River of Death"** Cherokee gloss shipped ONLY as disputed folk etymology, never as fact.
- **BALANCE (AI-vs-AI, 32 seeds, deterministic вҖ” D74, no fudge):** P0 US-holds 32/32 (mutual bloodbath ~2,400 each); P1 **CS breakthrough 32/32** (US routed cheaply, US:CS ~5.1; weight 3); P2 **US-holds 32/32** with the CS attacker paying **CS:US ~3.0**; **aggregate CS 32/32** (CS 3 / US 2). A human US player who wins P1 (closes the Wood gap) OVERTURNS the aggregate (the alt-history hinge). The CS, who won the field, **bled MORE in aggregate** (~70k vs ~63k / 8 seeds) вҖ” the costly-victory teaching, now asserted by the probe.
- **ENGINE-GRAIN LESSONS (logged for the Chattanooga build + future battles):** (1) the objective-hold mechanic favors whoever has more bodies ON the objective + cover + fog, **largely independent of `assaultDoctrine`** вҖ” to make an ATTACKER seize, give it a strength edge + open approach + few defender bodies; to make a DEFENDER hold, give it 3+ divisions + hill + breastworks + a timed reinforcement + cautious doctrine. (2) **The phases share ONE RNG seed stream** вҖ” tuning an earlier phase shifts later phases' outcomes; tune in order, re-sweep the whole battle, and expect a "true 50/50" phase to be bistable (prefer a clear historical lean). (3) Weight the decisive historical phase 3, others 1 (total 5). (4) **fog-of-war ON strongly aids the defender** вҖ” model a historically-foggy attacker-must-win phase via dense woods + fog-OFF. (5) **Write the casualty-DIRECTION + winner guards into the probe from the start** вҖ” every confirmed bug-hunt finding here was a missing casualty-direction/winner guard.
- **ADVERSARIAL BUG-HUNT (Workflow, 10 Opus agents вҖ” 6 diverse-lens finders Г— default-refute verify + a completeness critic): 2 confirmed + 3 critic gaps, ALL fixed.** HIGH (critic вҖ” the Vicksburg wrong-rank-under-Verified class): **Charles Harker mis-ranked "Brig. Gen." вҖ” he was a COLONEL at the battle** (like Hans Heg; his brigadier-generalcy dated to Sep 20 but came afterward) вҶ’ corrected to **Col. Charles Harker** + an anti-"Brig. Gen. Harker" fact-check guard. Plus 4 probe-rigor guards: P1 breakthrough casualty-direction (US:CS вүҘ2.5), P0 winner gate (вүҘ7/8), P1 win-by-SEIZE (winBy "hold"), and the aggregate "winner bled more" guard. (The 2 confirmed were both probe-coverage gaps; the Harker error was the one real content defect.)
- **VERIFICATION (PROPER VETTING, D53-OPS):** GATE OK; `probe-chickamauga` **18/18**, 0 pe; full no-regression GREEN (bullrun 15 В· malvern 24 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· chancellorsville 24 В· gettysburg 16 В· shiloh 29 В· vicksburg 18 В· roster 8 В· field 13 В· officers 15 В· logistics 14 В· arms 23 В· presets 26 В· csplayer 16 В· campaign-link 16 В· fog 13 В· ai 15 В· autopause 13 В· **custom-builder 9** [its EXPECTED registry baseline updated to include `chickamauga` вҖ” the recurring D86/D88 gotcha] В· engineering-corps 22 В· **tactical-visuals** 10 scenes incl. live Chickamauga 2D/3D, textureWarnings:0); diag-classic nonBlank 346; boot/t1 ok; **0 pageerrors**. WCAG: no new color CSS (content flows into the already-AA shared T1/T8 components). Committed + pushed. **NEXT: Chattanooga (the US-offensive reversal вҖ” Orchard Knob вҶ’ Lookout Mountain вҶ’ Missionary Ridge; brief at `.tmp/chattanooga-design.md`), then C3 USCT battles (the Crater В· New Market Heights В· Olustee В· Nashville).**

## D92 вҖ” ROSTER HISTORY-ACCURACY HARDENING (all 9 shipped battles) + the accurate-inputs principle вҖ” [OPUS, Aaron-directed] (2026-06-21)
Aaron asked whether the full Chattanooga-grade rigor (citation-grade research + adversarial verify, casualty-direction guards, balance sweep) had been applied to the battles already built. It had NOT for the 7 pre-Opus battles (the Codex/early-built C1 Eastern marquee + Shiloh + Bull Run); only Vicksburg + Chickamauga (Opus, bug-hunted) had the adversarial history pass.
- **Adversarial audit (Workflow, 9 Opus historians + critic + a consolidated casualty-direction sweep `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs`):** found **15 HIGH-severity wrong facts shipped under "Verified" stamps** вҖ” overwhelmingly the **rank-at-the-battle** class (a later/posthumous/backdated promotion applied to the battle date), plus wrong-division (the Vicksburg "Hebert" class) and a **dead officer commanding a battery**. ALL FIXED, each annotated in-file:
  - **Malvern Hill (4):** Hunt Brig.Gen.вҶ’**Col.** (file self-contradicted, calling him Col. elsewhere); Jackson Lt.Gen.вҶ’**Maj.Gen.** (no CSA Lt.Gen. grade until Oct 1862 вҖ” the Hood-at-Chickamauga anachronism); Porter Maj.Gen.вҶ’**Brig.Gen.** (MG dated Jul 4, 3 days after); Hooker Brig.Gen.вҶ’**Maj.Gen.** (under-ranked).
  - **Chancellorsville (4):** Rodes Maj.Gen.вҶ’**Brig.Gen.** (MG conferred after, for this flank attack); Berry **III Corps** not II; Paxton's Stonewall Brigade re-attached to **Colston's division** not A.P. Hill's (Hebert-class); Fairview battery **Capt. Hazzard (DEAD, d. Aug 1862) вҶ’ Capt. Clermont L. Best**.
  - **Shiloh (3):** Breckinridge Maj.Gen.вҶ’**Brig.Gen.** (MG Apr 14, 8 days after); Bragg led the **RIGHT** wing not the left (contradicted its own teaching card); W.H.L. Wallace died **Apr 10** not May 10.
  - **Gettysburg (3):** Doubleday & Early Brig.Gen.вҶ’**Maj.Gen.** (both under-ranked); Stannard's Vermont Bde **I Corps** not III.
  - **Vicksburg (1):** Martin L. Smith Maj.Gen.вҶ’**Brig.Gen.** (Г—3 fields; MG dated Nov 1863, 4 months AFTER the surrender).
  - Plus ~12 medium/low (Antietam Benjamin 1st-Lt + **4 not 6 guns** + Graham Capt; Shiloh Wood-as-reserveвҶ’**Chalmers's evening assault** / Taylor-on-Battery-AвҶ’**Peter P. Wood** / TrabueвҶ’Robert P., infantry not artillery; Bull Run Pelham's-batteryвҶ’**Alburtis's** / Elzey 13th VA + 1st Md Infantry; Fredericksburg Ransom echelon reframe; Gettysburg Archer captured at **Willoughby Run** not the Railroad Cut; Chickamauga Negley **court of inquiry** not court-martial + Cheatham's Preston Smith brigade added).
  - **SURFACED, deliberately NOT auto-fixed (genuine source conflict, per Aaron's rule):** Bull Run **Heintzelman** (Col. vs Brig. Gen. вҖ” regular-vs-volunteer commission conflict) and Antietam **Mansfield** (his Maj.Gen.-of-volunteers dated Jul 18 1862 predates the battle вҖ” the data's "Maj. Gen." is defensible; the auditor's downgrade is contestable). Left as-is for a future editor.
- **THE LOCKED PRINCIPLE (Aaron, verbatim during the pass):** "I want skill and gameplay and weapon type etc to impact outcomes вҖ” that's the priority over staying absolutely accurate to history. I don't want the no-lost-cause to be over-interpreted." Outcomes EMERGE from skill + weapon type + terrain + tactics via the D74 universal model. History enters ONLY as the **default equipment** (accurate soldier/gun counts, weapons, terrain, doctrine) so the **probable** result lands near the historical one *because the inputs are true* вҖ” **NEVER an output gate forcing a casualty direction or winner.** So we **DROPPED** the planned "fix Antietam so the CS doesn't out-bleed the Union" balance refight and the hard historical-direction probe gates; `sweep-all-battles.mjs` stays a DIAGNOSTIC. The only casualty guards kept/added are **system validations** (cover reduces casualties, rifled out-ranges smoothbore, more guns = more fire) that keep the game LEGIBLE (a player can read the visible OOB and forecast probable odds + casualty %). A teaching-text-vs-sim divergence is the intended "your war vs history," not a defect. (Full principle: memory `civilwar-roster-accuracy-principle`.)
- **Verification:** ALL edits are labels/notes only EXCEPT one accurate gun-count (Antietam Benjamin 6вҶ’4) + one unit re-identification keeping stats (Shiloh WoodвҶ’Chalmers). `node tools/build.mjs` GATE OK; full re-vet GREEN вҖ” all 9 battle probes (bullrun 15 В· malvern 24 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· chancellorsville 24 В· gettysburg 16 В· shiloh 29 В· vicksburg 18 В· chickamauga 18) + roster 8 + custom-builder 9, **each battle's own balance assertions still green** (outcomes byte-preserved), diag-classic `nonBlank:346`, 0 pageerrors; broad tactical-systems suite + boot/t1 green. New `tools/sweep-all-battles.mjs` consolidated casualty-direction diagnostic.
- **D92-verify (2026-06-21, resumed session after an API-error hang):** the D92 work was on disk but uncommitted when the prior session died on a 529. Before committing, an **independent adversarial re-verification** (Workflow: 1 Opus historian per battle + critic, re-run for the 2 that 529'd) checked every asserted correction against 2+ sources to catch a "fix" that was itself wrong. The 6/9 + 2 re-run + chancellorsville came back GO; it found **4 more items, ALL FIXED before commit:** (1) **Bull Run** вҖ” the D92 `cs_elzey` gloss "(Elzey's own regiment)" was attached to the 10th/13th Virginia, but Elzey's own regiment was the **1st Maryland** (he had colonel'd it); the 13th Va. was A. P. Hill's, the 10th Gibbons's вҖ” gloss moved to the 1st Maryland (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). (2) **Shiloh** вҖ” `us_buell_ammen` was "Brig. Gen." but Jacob **Ammen was a COLONEL** (24th Ohio) at Shiloh; his BG dated Jul 16 1862, after the battle (the anachronistic-rank class, *missed* by D92) вҶ’ Col. (3) **Antietam** вҖ” `us_battery_b` (Gibbon's Battery B, 4th U.S.) was tagged `rifled` but was **six 12-pdr Napoleons (smoothbore)** вҖ” its own note already said "double canister," the smoothbore signature; corrected `rifledвҶ’smooth` (an accurate-weapon input per the D92-locked principle; the antietam probe stayed 16/16 so the Cornfield outcome is byte-preserved вҖ” outcome-neutral). (4) **Malvern Hill** вҖ” D92 had *over-promoted* `us_hooker` BGвҶ’Maj. Gen. by his May-5-1862 date-of-rank, but Hooker's MG commission was **issued Jul 26 1862 (after the battle) and backdated**; the canonical Seven Days OOB lists him **BG**, exactly as the file (correctly) keeps Porter/Couch/Kearny вҖ” reverted to Brig. Gen. for internal consistency (a wrong fact D92 *introduced*). Net beyond the original D92: 3 label fixes + 1 outcome-neutral weapon-tag fix. Re-vet GREEN (full battle + roster + custom + systems suite + diag-classic `nonBlank:346` + boot/t1, 0 pageerrors). THEN committed + pushed.

## D93 вҖ” "THE SOLDIER'S STORY" character/narrative pillar вҖ” captured + scheduled вҖ” [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + directive, 2026-06-21)
Aaron's vision for an individual character/narrative layer, modeled on EA-Sports rosters. Captured here + memory `civilwar-soldiers-story-pillar`; **scheduled AFTER the C+E roadmap** (his choice) вҖ” NOT built now.

- **Aaron's 3 scoping answers (AskUserQuestion):** (1) granularity = **"every named individual found"** (exhaustive); (2) sequencing = **AFTER C+E** (finish Chattanooga + C3 USCT + the E strategic arc first); (3) shape = **unified journey-mode pillar** (merge with the D91 loot/survival journey mode; design the playthrough + interpersonal/**romance** threads as one deliberate pillar).

The real SYSTEM work is the **career/trajectory model** (each person's whole-war path) + the **start-anywhere engine**; the roster is large-but-bounded content.
- **Hard dependency:** accurate rank+position+unit per person вҖ” **the D92 roster hardening is the first roster data** and a prerequisite for "start from real rank."

## D94 вҖ” THE RATING SYSTEM (the OVR / "Madden layer") вҖ” designed + build authorized вҖ” [AARON] (AskUserQuestion + 3 directives, 2026-06-21)
A Madden-style **1вҖ“100 OVR + badges/abilities** for soldiers, officers, and brigades, the substrate for the D93 Soldier's Story. Full design law in **`RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`** (a 3-lens design Workflow: B sim-accurate-input spine + C prosopography data substrate + A Madden Star/Superstar/X-Factor feel, judged + synthesized; verified against the live engine).
- **The keystone (honors D74/D92):** ratings FULLY decide casualties + winners вҖ” but *through the inputs, not by editing the scoreboard*. A documented persona is *derived* into true attributes that *seed* the levers the engine already reads (`xp`, `quality`вҶ’`cmdBonus`, `weapon`, `radius`, `fate`, `cohesion`, bounded `sev.*`) ONCE at build/preset-apply, then the normal combat model runs on them вҶ’ the strong unit dominates *emergently* (and can still be out-played). The ONLY forbidden act (the "output wall", build-gate-asserted) is a handler writing `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/victory/`tgt.men` or out-of-band `sev.*` **directly** at resolution time (the scripted "higher rating вҮ’ auto-win" hack вҖ” it would make the sim a cutscene and kill the teaching). One spine, anchored at 64 вҶ’ a neutral unit is byte-identical to Classic.
- **Unifies, does not duplicate:** the officer OVR **is** `_cmdGenRating` (`0.55*skill+0.45*reputation`); reuses `commandLeadership` (the 42вҖ“88 bridge), `_cmdLeadWord`, `_cmdTraitBar`; persona inserts only at the FRONT (personaвҶ’`gen.skill`). No parallel rating, no second bridge.
- **Aaron's 4 locked directives (AskUserQuestion + follow-ups):** (1) **BUILD THE FULL SYSTEM NOW** вҖ” R-0вҶ’R-4 reprioritized *ahead of* Chattanooga (pulls D93 forward); (2) **X-Factor feel = DRAMATIC Madden surge** (visible glow + announce + strong swing, still hard-capped under `CMD_BONUS_CAP 0.9` вҖ” the cap, not the feel, is the wall); (3) **negatives = VERIFIED + plainly named** (Bragg "Piecemeal", McClellan "The Slows" вҖ” anti-Lost-Cause rigor applies to flaws too, вүҘ2 sources); (4) **tier scale = AвҖ“F report-card** (A+ вүҘ90 "Legendary" club, then A/B/C/D/F вҖ” NO gaming "S"; neutral 64 = C).
- **"Integrated in ALL layers" (Aaron directive):** the OVR surfaces + bites in the strategic President's Desk (appointment pool/cabinet/command OVR+grade+badges), the War-Effort army-quality readouts, **auto-resolve** (a capped `_cmdBadgeEdge` on the margin), **Classic hex** (OVR-derived quality via the `86-battle-conditioning` Вұ12% anchor, base unedited), the **real-time tactical** field (the full badge/X-Factor seams), **campaign progression** (reputationвҶ’OVR dev-traits), the Custom Battle Builder, and the D93 journey mode вҖ” all three battle modes read the SAME rating-derived inputs so they stay substitutable (the D62 bridge property). The rating never forces an outcome in any layer.
- **Build increments (each byte-identical-when-inactive, fully vetted + pushed):** R-0 data spine (`data/ratings.json` + `src/tactical/T14-ratings.js` pure fns + `tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, no combat seam) В· R-1 officer derivationвҶ’pipe В· R-2 OVR read-out UI (AвҖ“F, WCAG/CVD triple-encode) В· R-3 badge engine + global per-lever stacking cap + all-layers wiring В· R-4 X-Factors (deterministic seed-replay no-fudge gate) В· R-5 D93 scale-out (lazy per-person materialization) В· R-6 negative-badge sweep + dev-traits. Calibration oracle: the derivation table is regression-locked against the 9 shipped scenarios' authored `quality`/`xp` before any mass generation. (Reversible; design law in `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md`.)
- **D94-elicitation (Aaron, 10 rounds Г— 3 AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-21) вҖ” `RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN.md` В§15 has the full 30 answers.** The system grew substantially (Aaron chose comprehensively, mostly all-of-the-above): **~15 attributes** (the 10 + initiative/logistics/engineering/cavalry/artillery), shared-set/weighted-by-level, **own-visible/enemy-fuzzy**; badge kinds span ALL types at every rung (Star drill/terrain/arm/veteran В· Superstar auras/tactics/reputation/logistics В· X-Factor historical/surge/heroic/doomed); negatives ALL kinds (command/vice/unit/political); general strategic skills (maneuver/logistics/political/coordination); brigade identity (legend/ethnic/veteran/hard-luck). **NEW subsystems:** a between-battle **camp loop** вҖ” drilling-as-practice (focus-or-delegate, concordant battlefield bonuses) + **simmable scouting** (tiered by cavalry/recon) + **progression** (combat-XP + drilling + hidden potential ceiling + attrition decline). The **Army GM franchise layer** вҖ” a **war-wide free-agency pool** (alt-history dream-teams, balanced by a **symmetric AI GM** + difficulty scaling + clout cost + historical anchors), **all promotion paths** (merit/capital/seniority/field-brevet), killed-officer permadeath, and a **FULL multi-currency economy** (political capital + seniority/manpower + supply) earned from all sources, pressured by factional demands + event shocks. **Matchups:** dual **Attack/Defend OVR** + a full pre-battle matchup screen; emergent counters surfaced as advice. **UI:** period "Army Register" broadsheet roster; in-battle badges via HUD chips + X-Factor banner/glow + floating proc text + marker glyph; initials/rank portraits now. **Data:** full prosopography target, strict 2+ source provenance. **Ship order:** OVR+badges-in-battle first.
