## D95 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-1**: officer derivation into the existing command + field pipes (the persona becomes the source of truth) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first wiring increment of the D94 rating system (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9 R-1). The documented persona now SEEDS the levers the two pipes already read вҖ” **strategic** `gen.skill` and **tactical** officer `quality`/`radius`/`fate` вҖ” with the no-fudge keystone intact (the persona only sets inputs at build/make time; nothing is read at casualty/winner/rout time) and every unrated/un-opted entity **byte-identical**.
- **Strategic leg (`src/35-command.js`):** new `_cmdGenPersona(gen)` + `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen)`; `_cmdGenRating` now derives `skill` from the linked persona (`command/tactical/discipline` вҶ’ `fldOfficerSkillSeed`) instead of reading the static `gen.skill`. **Calibration oracle (strategic):** the 9 personas are authored so `round(0.45*command+0.35*tactical+0.20*discipline) === the Verified gen.skill EXACTLY` (FP-boundary-safe; min distance from the round-half boundary 0.2) вҶ’ `commandLeadership`/auto-resolve/conditioning stay **byte-identical** and the appoint-pool words still match history, while the persona is now the source. `cmdActiveTraits.skill` + the Command-desk Skill bar also route through `_cmdEffectiveSkill` (one source of truth; the bug-hunt critic's single-source-of-truth fix вҖ” byte-identical today, closes the future-drift footgun). Unrated generals keep authored `gen.skill`.
- **Tactical leg (`src/tactical/T3-officers.js`):** new `fldOfficerPersona(o)` + `fldMakeOfficer` derives `quality` (`fldPersonaQuality`, calibrated to reproduce the authored field quality within вүӨ0.005 вҖ” the R-0 oracle, so a rated aura shifts only slightly), `radius` (authored echelon range + a small charisma nudge, clamped 160вҖ“290), and `fate` (the persona's durability multiplier, which matches the authored scenario fate for the Bull Run cast). **EXPLICIT `pid` opt-in, NO `id` fallback** вҖ” the bug-hunt-class fix for a real **cross-scenario id collision**: leader ids are reused across battles (`ld_jackson` is the 1861 brigadier at Bull Run but a corps commander at Antietam/Chancellorsville), so an `id`-match would leak the wrong persona; a leader derives ONLY when it names a persona via `pid`. The 7 Bull Run leaders are opted in (`data/bullrun.json`); every other scenario's leaders have no `pid` вҶ’ byte-identical until their personas are authored.
- **`data/ratings.json` вҖ” NEW `generalPersonas` map** (9 strategic army-commander personas keyed by the `data/generals.json` id): **CS** Lee, Jackson, A.S. Johnston, Bragg, Longstreet В· **US** McClellan, Grant, Burnside, Meade вҖ” the principal commanders of the 9 D92-hardened battles (Bull Run is covered by the field cast). A SEPARATE record from the Bull Run FIELD cast (war-long army commander vs the 1861 brigade officer); R-5 unifies them into one prosopography person. The documented character + the named negatives (McClellan `the_slows`, Burnside `rigid_plan`, Bragg `piecemeal`) are Verified with real sources (Sears 1988, Marvel 1991, Robertson 1997, Hess 2016, Wert 1993, Chernow 2017, McPherson 1988, вҖҰ); the attribute VECTOR is Inferred designer calibration anchored to each Verified `gen.skill`; `aggression` tracks the documented temperament and is EXCLUDED from the headline OVR (anti-Lost-Cause).
- **Vetting:** GATE OK; `probe-ratings` **13/13** (3 new R-1 steps: strategic exact + unrated byte-identical + tactical derive + cross-scenario collision guard), `probe-command` **15/15** (incl. the new source-of-truth guard); FULL no-regression GREEN вҖ” all 9 battle baselines byte-identical (incl. **chancellorsville 24/24**, proving the `ld_jackson` collision fix) + roster/custom-builder/fog/ai/autopause/campaign-link/logistics/arms/presets/csplayer/officers/field/engineering-corps/tactical-visuals; diag-classic `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 Opus lenses Г— default-refute verify + a completeness critic): 0 confirmed finder findings; 1 LOW critic finding (the single-source-of-truth read) FIXED. ## D96 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-2**: the OVR read-out UI (Command desk grades + tactical HUD brigade OVR) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)

## D97 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-3**: the badge engine (the first ratingвҶ’combat seam) + the no-fudge build-gate вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first place a rating actually TOUCHES combat (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§4/В§6/В§9 R-3). A guarded one-token factor seeds the levers the engine already reads; the no-fudge OUTPUT wall is now enforced **structurally** by the build. **Byte-identical when off** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles produce identical deterministic results on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build).
- **`fldBadgeFactor(u, lever)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** the guarded MULTIPLICATIVE one-token factor вҖ” IDENTITY 1.0 when `__FIELD.badges` is off OR the unit carries no matching badge (mirrors the `(u.cmdBonus||0)` no-op). It sums the unit's badges' signed `mag`s for a lever, gates each by its trigger (`_fldBadgeTrig`: always/march/in_woods/arm_cav/arm_art; others default on, an R-4 refinement), then CLAMPS the summed delta to the realism-scaled per-unit per-lever cap (`fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"badgeLever")` вҖ” arcade .16 / balanced .10 / historian .06, D94-softcap). Negatives are DAMPERS (factor<1, вүҘ1вҲ’cap), never enemy buffs. Pure read; returns a factor, never writes state. Plus `fldUnitCohesion(u)` ((cohesionвҲ’50)/50, clamped [вҲ’1,1]; **0 when cohesion unauthored** вҶ’ byte-identical вҖ” the rally term defaults neutral, NOT xp-derived, since an xp-derived default would shift the rally of every xpвү 2 unit).
- **Four guarded seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** fire (`fldResolveFire` `power *= fldBadgeFactor(u,"fire")`), rally (`fldMoraleStep` `rally = (1 + xp*.12*vet + .06*cohesion*vet) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"rally")`), melee (`fldResolveMelee` atk/def), speed (`fldMoveFactor` `(u._spdMul||1) * fldBadgeFactor(u,"speed")` вҖ” `_spdMul` reserved for the R-4 X-Factor surge). All identity when off. The `__FIELD.badges` gate (default ON, `_badgesOff` hook) + `__FIELD.realismTier` (set in `fldPresetsApply`, default balanced) added.
- **Badge data (`data/ratings.json`):** each of the 25 badgeDefs now carries `fldLever` (fire/rally/speed/melee, or `none` for officer-aura / auto-resolve-edge / canister / sight effects deferred to R-4/В§7.5) + a signed `mag`. Ships the Star/Superstar positives + the Verified named negatives with real tactical bite: McClellan **The Slows** (speed вҲ’0.08), Bragg **Piecemeal** (rally вҲ’0.05), Burnside **Rigid Plan** (fire вҲ’0.05), **Green Levies** (rally вҲ’0.08), **Powder-Shy** (rally вҲ’0.05); positives marksman/woods_fighter (fire), disciplined/blooded/beloved/stonewall (rally), hardy_marcher/horseman (speed). Badges are NOT yet assigned to shipped scenario rosters (that is the R-6 sweep) вҶ’ every battle stays byte-identical.
- **The NO-FUDGE OUTPUT WALL, build-gate-asserted (`tools/build.mjs` gate 4d):** the rating module (`tactical/T14-ratings.js`) is scanned at build for any write to `cas`/`aCas`/`bCas`/`.victory`/`.men`/`sev.*` вҖ” dot AND bracket notation (the bracket variants close the bug-hunt's computed-member bypass) вҖ” and the build FAILS (exit 5) if found. Verified firing on planted `u.men=0`, `u["men"]=0`, and `F.sev["attrition"]=2` writes; clean build prints `GATE OK В· вҖҰ В· no-fudge вң“`. The combat modules legitimately write these; the wall scopes to the rating/badge module, which may only seed inputs + return factors.
- **Vetting вҖ” NOTE the environmental deviation:** GATE OK (incl. the new no-fudge gate). The standard `load`-based probe suite was **environmentally BLOCKED** this session: headless Chrome's `load` event never fires for the game page (the THREE-CDN `<script>` stalls in headless intermittently; it broke the committed-green R-2 build identically; a trivial page fires `load` in 73ms; `domcontentloaded` loads everything incl. THREE in ~1.5s). Root contributors: (a) the single-threaded `python -m http.server` chokes on the page's ~170 local asset requests (fixed by a **ThreadingHTTPServer**); (b) the THREE-CDN `load` stall (the documented gotcha). So R-3 was vetted via a **`domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness** (`.tmp/r3-verify.mjs`): it ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically (same seed) on the R-3 build vs the committed R-2 build and confirmed **IDENTICAL** casualties/winner/steps for all 10, plus the full badge-logic assertions (off=1, single=1.06, stack clamps to 1.10=1+cap, realism arc 1.16 > bal 1.10 > his 1.06, negatives 0.92, cohesion math), 0 pageerrors. This cross-build diff is a *stronger* byte-identity check than the standard probes. **Adversarial bug-hunt** (4 Opus lenses Г— refute-verify + critic): 2 confirmed (the gate-4d bracket bypass вҖ” FIXED by adding bracket regexes; a phantom `'sharpshooters'` key in the probe/T0 comment вҖ” FIXED) + 0 critic. Committed + pushed.

## D98 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-4**: the X-FACTORS (the dramatic "in the zone" Madden surge, inside the no-fudge wall) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The dramatic increment (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§4/В§6/В§9 R-4, D94 fork-1 "DRAMATIC surge"). An X-Factor badge enters "in the zone" when its situational trigger fires and SURGES on ONE channel, hard-capped вҖ” a visible, announced swing that provably can never breach the no-fudge wall. **Byte-identical when off / unassigned** (proven: a `domcontentloaded` byte-identity harness ran sandbox + all 9 battles deterministically on the R-4 build vs the committed R-3 build (HEAD dc9ba61) вҶ’ **IDENTICAL** winner/US-cas/CS-cas/steps for all 10, 0 pageerrors).
- **`fldXFactorStep(dt)` (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** gated on `__FIELD.badges`; for each unit carrying an `rung:"xfactor"` badge (`_fldUnitXFactors`), tests its activation (`_fldXFactorInZone`: march_vigor=moving В· his_offensive=moving/charging В· ammo_low_defend=ammo<12 & not charging В· last_stand_defend=holding & (low morale or a friendly routing within 220yd) В· usct_assault/mass_assault=charging В· flanking=cav & charging) and, when in the zone, sets the surge on EXACTLY ONE channel (its declared lever): a **NON-speed** X-Factor (rally/melee/none) sets `u._xfActive = fldRatingRealismCap(tier,"xfactor")` (arcade 1.45 / balanced 1.20 / historian 1.08); a **SPEED** X-Factor (Foot Cavalry / The Slows) sets `u._spdMul` only (capped [0.85,1.15]) and does NOT surge the command aura. One-shot вҡЎ `fldAnnounce` + `fldScenarioBanner` on the rising edge (`_xfOn`); a marker glow (`_xfGlow`); deterministic decay (`_fldXfDecay`) toward identity out of zone. **NO RNG** вҶ’ seed-replayable. A unit carrying no X-Factor is left wholly untouched (`_xf*`/`_spdMul` stay undefined) вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **`fldXFactorApplyCmd(u)`:** scales the unit's ALREADY-SUMMED command aura `u.cmdBonus = min(FLDO.CMD_BONUS_CAP, (cmdBonus||0)*_xfActive)` вҖ” pushes the aura toward the **hard 0.9 wall, NEVER beyond**. A strict no-op unless an X-Factor is active (`_xfActive` undefined/вүӨ1) вҶ’ byte-identical. Called in `fldSimStep` AFTER `fldOfficersStep` (so the aura is summed first), gated on `__FIELD.badges` (NOT officers) so the cmdBonus surge and the `_spdMul` surge share ONE gate.
- **Seams (`src/tactical/T0-field-sandbox.js`):** `fldSimStep` calls `fldXFactorStep(dt)` just before `fldOfficersStep` + the apply loop just after; `fldMoveFactor` clamps the **COMBINED** speed factor (the `_spdMul` surge Г— the R-3 static speed-badge factor) to ONE documented band **[0.75,1.30]** so no stack can breach it (exactly 1 when no rating speed input вҶ’ byte-identical); `fld2dDraw` draws a guarded `_xfGlow` pulse вҖ” a CVD-safe amber burst RING (the shape carries the meaning) + a **vector-drawn** lightning bolt (no emoji-font/tofu dependency), `reduceMotion`-honored, drawn for no shipped unit вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **Data (`data/ratings.json`):** ADDED `first_with_the_most` (Forrest, cav, flanking trigger, fldLever none вҶ’ surges via the capped cmdBonus only; 2 sources вҶ’ Verified). The 7 X-Factors: foot_cavalry, rock_of_chickamauga, bayonet, earned_in_blood, grand_charge, first_with_the_most, the_slows. NOT assigned to any shipped scenario (the R-6 sweep) вҶ’ byte-identical.
- **NO-FUDGE REPLAY GATE (`tools/probe-ratings.mjs`, +2 steps вҶ’ 17/17):** a deterministic seed-replay tags one CS sandbox brigade with foot_cavalry and runs it vs the untagged baseline (same seed): the surge **BITES** (it flipped a US win into a CS win) yet stays **bounded** (17.2% total-casualty delta вҖ” an input nudge, not a scripted result) and the **wall holds** (`maxCmd 0.47 < 0.9`). Plus synthetic asserts: speed X-Factor surges only `_spdMul` (no cmdBonus), non-speed surges cmdBonus capped at the wall, the combined-speed clamp binds at 1.30, negatives drag, realism-monotone amp, decayвҶ’1.

## D100 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q8**: the between-battle CAMP LOOP (drilling + progression) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The agency that GROWS your rating over a campaign (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§15 / В§14.6). A new "Camp" desk tab where, between battles, the President DRILLS the army; the drilled training raises the army he fields via a guarded, bounded conditioning seam вҖ” PURE INPUT-SEEDING, never the scoreboard, and **byte-identical until the player engages the camp**.
- **`src/36-camp.js` (new module):** `campInit` (idempotent; seeds `C.president.camp` = drill{musketry/maneuver/entrenching/endurance}, fatigue, delegate, **engaged**); `campDrill(C,focus)` (raises a focus toward CEIL 90, +fatigue, sets engaged); `campSetDelegate`; `campTrainingBonus(C)` (THE BRIDGE SEAM вҖ” per-facet deltas, ALL ZERO when no focus is drilled); `campOnResolve` (rest sheds fatigue, a delegated army auto-drills, a clean win SEASONS / a battle this side bled the lion's share ERODES вҖ” gated on `engaged`); `campRenderTab`/`campWireTab`; `_campGrade`/`_campBar`. **Drilling/progression only** вҖ” SCOUTING deferred to Q8b (it needs the strategic-next-battle вҶ” tactical-OOB mapping).
- **The bridge seam (`src/85-battle-bridge.js`):** `bridgeArmy` applies a guarded camp term вҖ” drilling lifts firepower (musketry) / morale (maneuver) / supply (entrenching) + relieves fatigue (endurance) + a small overall "sharpness," **bounded** (full-drill вүҲ +8 overall over base, вүӨ14; fatigue DRAGS the gain Г—(1вҲ’0.6В·fat/100)). EXACTLY 0 when undrilled вҶ’ byte-identical. Computed once, reused.
- **Wiring:** `campInit` in `_t1InitAll` (after cmdInit); `campOnResolve` in `_t1Resolve` (after cmdOnResolve); a "Camp" tab in `30-president-shell.js` (dispatch + tab arrays + button + wiring); `"36-camp.js"` in the manifest. `C.president.camp` rides `serializeSave` wholesale + lazy-migrates via idempotent campInit вҖ” **no `_SAVE_VER` bump** (additive, D7).
- **THE KEYSTONE (byte-identity):** an `engaged` flag (false until the first drill/delegate) makes the WHOLE loop INERT until the player opens the camp вҖ” `campOnResolve` early-returns and `campTrainingBonus` is all-zero at zero drill вҖ” so a campaign that never camps conditions byte-for-byte as the pre-Q8 build (proven: probe-camp's keystone step + probe-bridge 6/6 + probe-conditioning 6/6 UNCHANGED). NO RNG (deterministic).

ALL fixed: **(MED + a critic-MED, the real one)** the "bloody" attrition test divided a raw men-count by `C.manpower.strength` вҖ” a 0-100 INDEX (and one decremented upstream the same turn by manpowerOnResolve), so nearly every real battle read "bloody" вҶ’ the **win-seasons branch was effectively DEAD** (drilled training only ever decayed, inverting the headline progression). ## D101 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-5**: the PROSOPOGRAPHY SCALE-OUT (bulk per-person derivation + LAZY materialization + the play-as-anyone hook) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The D93 "Soldier's Story" substrate the whole rating spine was built for: a brigade can now be *inspected down to its men*, and any person can be *materialized + promoted* вҖ” all PURE DATA + DISPLAY, **byte-identical** (no shipped scenario assigns bulk persons; the deterministic sim вҖ” sandbox + all 9 battles вҖ” is proven identical to committed HEAD `84c5e95`). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§5/В§8/В§9 R-5/В§15 (R9).
- **The LAZY-MATERIALIZATION keystone (В§8):** a brigade TOKEN carries ONE aggregate `fldMenMeanOVR(u,year)` вҖ” its men's mean OVR, derived O(1) from xp + arm-branch + year + a deterministic per-brigade-id jitter, clamped [20,88] (a brigade AVERAGE never reaches the Legendary individual ceiling). Per-person rows are NEVER instantiated en masse: `fldMaterializePerson(spec,year)` builds exactly ONE row on demand (inspect / play-as), and `fldBrigadeMuster(u,n,year)` builds a HARD-CAPPED (вүӨ6) representative sample (captain/sergeant/private from a data-driven `musterTemplate`), **never `u.men` rows** вҖ” proven: a 100,000-man brigade still materializes 3. The mean is always recomputable, never the source of truth.
- **New pure functions (`src/tactical/T14-ratings.js`):** `fldMenMeanOVR` В· `fldMaterializePerson` (reuses the R-0 `fldDerivePerson` вҶ’ headline + dual OVR + grade; a generated row gets a deterministic synthesized period name [`_fldSynthName` + `_FLD_FIRST`/`_FLD_LAST`, NO RNG] + Inferred provenance + a `latentCommand` seed) В· `fldPromotePerson(person,toRank)` (the **latent-command promotion** = play-as-anyone: lifts command/tactical/discipline/charisma by the rank-base delta; returns a NEW person, pure) В· `fldPersonTeam` (the EA-style {side,army,corps} journey hook) В· `fldProvenanceStyle` (the **Inferred-vs-Verified visual distinction** В§10 вҖ” Verified solid / Inferred HATCHED `repeating-linear-gradient` / Disputed dashed; meaning rides pattern + glyph [вң“/~/?] + word, NOT colour вҶ’ CVD-safe) В· `fldMusterHudLine` (the compact in-battle inspect line) В· `fldMusterRollHtml` (the full "Muster Roll" panel, ready for the journey-mode character sheet). **Data:** `musterTemplate` + `_r5Note` added to `data/ratings.json`.

Pure display; "" when ratings data absent вҶ’ byte-identical. NO new combat path; NO RNG.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (11 agents: 4 diverse-lens Opus finders Г— default-refute verify + a completeness critic; 6 raw вҶ’ **2 confirmed + 2 critic, ALL LOW, ALL latent**; 0 HIGH/MED; completeness verdict: no no-fudge-wall write, no determinism leak, no lazy-materialization breach, no escaping gap). ALL 4 fixed (defensive-copy hardening so a FUTURE bulk-person/career path can't corrupt canonical `GAME_DATA`): **(1)** `fldMaterializePerson` returned the AUTHORED persona BY REFERENCE (via `fldDerivePerson`'s authored branch) вҶ’ now shallow-copies persona at the materialization boundary; **(2)** `fldPromotePerson` with an unmapped/typo'd `toRank` silently mapped to the 64 anchor (a +16 unearned lift + false officerTier) вҶ’ now requires a real `rankBase` key, else a clean no-op clone; **(3)** the `sources` ARRAY was a second shared reference (and `fldPromotePerson` propagated it) вҶ’ now `.slice()`'d on both paths; **(4)** `fldPromotePerson`'s persona-less guard returned the input ref, breaking its "returns a NEW person" contract вҶ’ added `_fldClonePerson` (copies persona + sources) for every no-op path. ## D102 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q9**: the GM PROMOTION economy (the first depth-chart MOVE вҖ” promote В· multi-currency В· merit gate) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The first real GM *move* beyond appoint/relieve, built on the existing `cmdAppoint`/political-capital spine + the R-5 person spine (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.2/В§14.3/В§15). The President promotes a general one grade up a clean strategic ladder, spending a **multi-currency** budget, **merit-gated** by reputation. PURE INPUT-SEEDING + display вҖ” **byte-identical until the player promotes** (proven: sandbox + all 9 battles byte-for-byte identical to committed HEAD `fc1d251`). Design law: В§12.
- **The ladder + the move (`src/35-command.js`, the "Q9 (D102)" block):** `_cmdBaseGrade` parses each general's VERBOSE `generals.json` rank deterministically down to one of **Brig. Gen. вҶ’ Maj. Gen. вҶ’ Lt. Gen. вҶ’ General** (the multi-word grades are checked before the bare "General"; an unrecognized rank defaults to the LOWEST grade вҖ” never invents a man up). `cmdPromote(C,id)` raises him one grade, spending BOTH currencies (gated on both): **political capital** (`C.clock.capital`, the primary вҖ” `capitalCost` by target grade, Г—`aboveMeritMul` if above merit) + a NEW **seniority** pool (`cmd.seniority` вҖ” `seniorityCostBase` + a `seniorityLeapfrog` surcharge when he leapfrogs a passed-over senior). Bounded, clamped, logged.
- **The merit gate (the honest history):** each target grade carries a reputation **meritBar**. EARNED (rep вүҘ bar) вҶ’ a confidence bump (+`earnedRepBonus`); ABOVE merit (rep < bar) вҶ’ the capital surcharge **+ a jealousy reputation hit** (вҲ’`aboveMeritRepHit`). Because OVR = 0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation, **over-promoting a favorite past his record can LOWER his OVR** вҖ” rank without merit doesn't make a good commander. (Teaches the real command politics Lincoln navigated; anti-Lost-Cause: merit, not grade, is competence.)
- **How it reaches the fight (no new combat path):** a promotion lifts the general's effective skill by a small BOUNDED amount вҖ” `_cmdPromoteSkillLift` = (rankBase delta Г— `skillLiftWeight` 0.92), clamped to `skillLiftCap` 6 вҖ” added inside the EDITED `_cmdEffectiveSkill(gen, C)`, which flows ONLY through the existing `_cmdGenRating вҶ’ commandLeadership вҶ’` the bridge LEADERSHIP facet (an INPUT the sim already reads; `commandMarginEdge` reads aggression/caution, untouched). NEVER the scoreboard (D74/D94 no-fudge wall вҖ” `cmdPromote` mutates only `clk.capital`/`cmd.seniority`/`cmd.promotions`/`cmd.reputation`). **0 lift when un-promoted вҶ’ every pre-Q9 reading byte-identical.**

## D103 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **R-6 (citation-provenance portion)**: the CATALOG-WIDE citation hardening + a permanent build-gate вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The R-6 increment's **negative-badge ASSIGNMENT to rosters + live dev-traits remain**; this milestone shipped the **citation-grade prerequisite** that gates them: every `Verified`-stamped claim in the data catalog now carries **вүҘ2 independent real sources**, the non-negotiable made un-erodable by the build. **A live violation was found and closed:** an audit revealed the debt was NOT confined to badges (the logged D98вҖ“D101 framing) вҖ” **47 records across SIX data files** were stamped `Verified` with <2 sources (badges 13 В· personas 2 В· weapons 9 В· artillery 9 В· engineering 8 В· terrain 1 В· cabinet 5). Outcome: **0 fabrication** (critic-confirmed), all citations real/on-claim/independent. The long descriptive forms ("Verified specs (вҖҰ)", "Verified (high) вҖ” вҖҰ", ~72 of them) cite inline in prose and trim-lowercase to вү  "verified", so they stay out of the structured gate **by design**. Mirrors the 4d no-fudge wall: a non-negotiable made structural.

## D105 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **LIVE DEV-TRAITS (the Madden development arc)**: a general's OVR now develops over the campaign, shaped by a hidden potential ceiling вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The last open item on the R-6 rating track (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9-R-6: "reputation level-up вҶ’ OVR still TODO") + the D94-fork-#5 lock ("ReputationвҶ’OVR dev-traits = LIVE in-campaign now"). `cmdOnResolve` already evolved a general's reputation by battle outcome (decisive win +6 / win +3 / draw вҲ’1 / loss вҲ’4 / decisive loss вҲ’8), and `_cmdGenRating` (0.55В·skill + 0.45В·reputation) вҶ’ `commandLeadership` already read it вҖ” so winning a campaign already nudged his OVR. D105 adds the **Madden DEV-TRAIT** that SHAPES that arc: a hidden potential **ceiling** (how high he can climb), a **floor** (how far he can fall), a development **rate** (rise vs fall), and an **attritionDrag** (the В§15-R3 decline-with-heavy-attrition). **ACCURATE INPUTS, never an output gate (D74/D92)** вҖ” a dev-trait only shapes the general's REPUTATION (an INPUT the existing pipe consumes), it NEVER writes a casualty/winner. Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§9-R-6 / В§14.6 / В§15-R3.
- **The keystone (byte-identical-when-off, the R-6/D104 pattern):** the engine seam in `cmdOnResolve` is **byte-identical for an UNASSIGNED general (or absent devTraits data)** вҖ” it takes the LITERAL pre-D105 path `clamp(cur+delta, 5, 98)`, rate 1, no drag (proven across ALL five outcome quadrants + both clamp rails). The deliberate, citation-grade, historically-directed change is the AUTHORED `data/ratings.json` `devTraits.assign` map (20 generals вҶ’ one of 12 archetypes). The ceiling/floor are RELATIVE to the general's SEEDED start reputation (`devTrack.start`, fixed), every archetype keeps `ceilingAboveвүҘ5 & floorBelowвүҘ5`, so the pre-D105 "a winning general gains reputation / a losing one loses it" invariant holds for all.
- **The arc (in `cmdOnResolve`):** an assigned general's base delta is scaled by his `riseRate`/`fallRate`, plus a bounded extra `attritionDrag` when his side bled the lion's share (casualty SHARE > pivot вҖ” the D100 unit-correct measure), then clamped to HIS `[floor,ceiling]` band. New pure fns (`src/35-command.js`): `_cmdDevCfg`/`_cmdDevStart`/`_cmdDevTrait` (resolves the absolute band) / `_cmdAttritionDrag` (bounded вүӨ attritionDragMax) / `_cmdDevTrackUpdate` (pure observation) / `_cmdDevTrend` / `_cmdCareerArcHTML`. `cmdInit` seeds + sanitizes `cmd.devTrack[id]={start,peak,low,battles}` (rides the save, no `_SAVE_VER` bump). NO RNG.
- **The 12 archetypes + anti-Lost-Cause balance:** rising_star (Grant/Sherman/Sheridan) В· steady_rock (Thomas) В· established_legend (Lee/Jackson) В· natural_genius (Forrest) В· steady_professional (Meade/ScottвҶ’administrator/Longstreet/A.S.Johnston) В· cautious_fabian (J.E.Johnston) В· mercurial_cavalier (Stuart/Beauregard) В· administrator (Scott/Halleck) В· plateau (McClellan) В· overpromoted (Burnside/Hooker) В· volatile_aggressor (Hood) В· quarrelsome (Bragg). **The thesis is anti-Lost-Cause:** the Union's elite are RISERS (4 high-ceiling developers rated as high as Lee/Jackson вҖ” the honest claim that the Union found and elevated its best command) while command failures are named plainly on BOTH sides (US McClellan plateau / Burnside-Hooker overpromoted; CS Bragg quarrelsome / Hood volatile-disaster). All 20 assignments are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading of a documented arc вҖ” gate-4e-exempt) with 1-2 real sources each; nothing laundered (Forrest's Klan + Longstreet's Lost-Cause slander named in the notes).
- **The read-out (`_cmdCareerArcHTML`, a new Command-desk "Career Arc" section):** the sitting general's dev-trait tier (label + glyph + polarity sign + desc), his OVR arc (startвҶ’nowвҶ’peak on a floor..ceiling band with start/peak ticks), a trend verdict (Rising/Holding/Fading/Untested) + the net delta, and a soft potential-room note. Triple-encoded (word + sign + number; glyph + colour decorative) вҶ’ CVD-safe; `wcag-auditor` AA (one nested-opacity spot 3.93вҶ’4.57:1 fixed).
- **The no-fudge wall extended (bug-hunt):** build-gate 4d (the no-fudge OUTPUT WALL) now also scans `src/35-command.js` (confirmed it writes ONLY command state вҖ” reputation/seniority/capital/devTrack, none in the forbidden set) вҖ” closing the coverage gap so the strategic rating code's no-fudge invariant is STRUCTURAL too (mirrors how D103's gate 4e made citations un-erodable).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (the ultracode pattern вҖ” 5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge В· byte-identity В· bounding/determinism В· citation/balance В· UI/probe] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 29 agents; **8 confirmed + 3 critic-missed; 1 HIGH, 3 MED, 7 LOW; critic: "SAFE TO COMMIT вҖ” both hard invariants [no output gate, byte-identical-when-off] CONFIRMED HOLD"** via independent grep corroboration that `devTrack`/`reputation` are read by no combat code). ALL 11 fixed: **(HIGH, the only blocker)** a fabricated-by-misattribution Thomas citation ("Conquered into Liberty" is Eliot Cohen's, not Larry Daniel's) вҶ’ corrected to Daniel's actual *Days of Glory: The Army of the Cumberland* (CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #4); **(MED)** the Burnside note "proved right at Fredericksburg" laundered a Union command failure вҶ’ rewritten to name the futile Marye's-Heights assaults plainly (anti-Lost-Cause); **(MED, the keystone hardening)** `_cmdDevTrait`/`_cmdDevStart` consumed `devTrack.start` RAW вҶ’ a tampered/stale save (start NaN / 500) poisoned the reputation clamp вҶ’ now coerced through `_cmdNum` + clamped [0,100] at the read site, `cmdInit` SANITIZES the whole record on LOAD (the Q9 re-clamp pattern), and `_cmdCareerArcHTML` coerces the whole `tr` record (no "NaN" can render); **(MEDвҶ’the gate gap above);** **(LOW Г—7)** byte-identical-off probe now covers all 5 quadrants + both clamp rails; the off-test asserts `devTraits.assign` is restored (no global-state leak); floor/drag steps assert the locked general's trait; the render step covers all 4 `_cmdDevTrend` branches + the battles=0 edge; the new SAVE-TAMPER probe step (start NaN/500/вҲ’99 вҶ’ finite + in-band + no NaN render); the balance check counts named-failures as (вҲ’,~) so it doesn't rest on the single cs-bragg record.
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“` (4d now scans 35-command.js) `В· citations вң“` (the Thomas fix); `probe-command` **34/34** (9 D105 steps: data+balance В· byte-identical-off all-quadrants+rails В· assign-restored В· rising-star-vs-plateau+ceiling В· floor cap В· attrition drag bounded В· no-output-gate+devTrack-purity В· save-tamper В· render+4 trend branches); `probe-ratings` **21/21** (the tactical rating engine + the 9-battle badge resolution intact вҖ” D105 touches NO tactical code, byte-identical by construction, confirmed by `git diff`), `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA. **ENV:** the 8 GB Mac had a healthy memory window this session; probes ran foreground via a threaded server (the documented load-stall gotcha did not bite). ## D118 вҖ” E1 deepening increment 5: **INTERACTIVE HINGE-FORK DECISION CARDS** вҖ” 4 citation-grade strategic forks that STEER the war toward the endings вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)

- **CONFEDERATE end-states (12):** (groundedвҶ’longshot) Recognized independence (the 1862 window won) В· Negotiated peace 1864 (break Northern will to the election) В· Emancipated Confederacy (Cleburne's path fully вҖ” independence but the founding creed gutted; anti-Lost-Cause, named honestly) В· Stalemate / two Americas (an exhausted armistice) В· Fabian survival (Johnston's pure-defensive attrition outlasts Northern patience) В· Trans-Mississippi redoubt (Kirby-Smithdom survives west of the river) В· King Cotton coerces Europe (the embargo finally pays) В· The Northwest secedes (Copperhead success fractures the Union three ways). (fantastical) A British war (Trent escalates; the Royal Navy breaks the blockade) В· Foreign legions land (Maximilian's army crosses the Rio Grande) В· Stonewall lives (Jackson survives Chancellorsville) В· The Golden Circle (a slave-power Caribbean/Latin-American empire).
- **UNION end-states (12):** (groundedвҶ’longshot) Reconstruction that HOLDS (the 14th/15th enforced past 1877 вҖ” no Jim Crow) В· Early abolition war (1862) В· Hard-war quick collapse (Sherman's doctrine early) В· Reunion WITHOUT emancipation (the dark path вҖ” the war's purpose abandoned, named as the moral failure it is) В· The 1862 knockout (Richmond falls early) В· Forty acres enforced (emancipation + land redistribution carried through) В· Compensated, bloodless end (Lincoln's road not taken вҖ” slavery ends by purchase) В· The general strike triumphant (Du Bois's mass self-emancipation collapses the labor base). (fantastical/poignant) Lincoln lives Reconstruction (never assassinated; leads it himself) В· The repeater/Gatling war (rapid-fire a year early) В· A Russo-American century (the Tsar's fleet stays and fights) В· The 13th early (abolition by amendment from the start).
- **REWARD AXES (7) вҖ” what "done right" unlocks the biggest divergences:** battlefield dominance В· the economy/blockade game В· the political/home-front game В· the emancipation/manpower game В· the command game (the GM depth-chart/rating system) В· engineering & technology В· intelligence & cavalry.
- **Wildness ceiling:** a LABELED SPECTRUM вҖ” grounded/plausible endings by default; fantastical endings unlocked by fantastical play and explicitly tagged "fantastical" (so the teaching line вҖ” what really happened вҖ” always stays clear). Honors the tiered wild-card design (D28) + the no-thumb-on-the-scale law (D54).
- **BUILD ORDER (Aaron):** **the FANTASTICAL tier FIRST** (the most fun/"video-game" payoffs), then backfill the grounded teaching forks. The end-state DETECTION + the ledger/report surfacing build on `divScan` (81-divergence.js) + the wild-card catalog (80-victory.js) + the `decResolve`/`_decApply` hinge-fork engine (32-decisions.js); each end-state carries a citation-grade counterfactual (the D111 inline-prose trust model; failures named both sides). Implement as vetted increments under E1; the actual war-END screens for these land with E4-i2.

## D113 вҖ” В§12.3 THE ELECTION-SUPPORT RELIEF-BIND вҖ” a commissioned political general costs more capital to relieve before the 1864 vote (the bind Lincoln lived) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
- **What shipped (the GM В§12.3 keystone the Commission move D109 was built around, now unblocked by the 1864-election state E4/D112):** a commissioned POLITICAL general (Banks/Butler/Sigel/McClernand вҖ” `commission.kind:"political"` + a `politicalValue`) delivers his constituency's votes to the war effort while he serves, so relieving him in the run-up to the 1864 election forfeits that support вҖ” an ADDITIVE surcharge on his relief cost (`_cmdReliefCost`) that rises year over year toward the vote (1862<1863<1864) and FALLS to zero the moment `clock.resolved1864` is set (the bind is spent). `surcharge = round((politicalValue/100) * windowByYear[year] * surchargeMax)`, bounded [0, surchargeMax=14]. A new teaching tell on the active-general card names the constituency + the `+N capital` cost ("Lincoln lived this bind"). Teaches the В§12.3 command-politics lesson concretely: Banks in command costs commandLeadership 49 vs Grant's 87 (D109) AND can't be cheaply dumped before November 1864.
- **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log; the kickoff named it "pair with E4"):** chose the relief-bind over the frozen-loop negotiated-peace war-end (E4-i2) for an autonomous tick because it is a contained, well-authorized command-economy extension (the code already flagged it "the follow-on" at 35-command.js:985) with no frozen-loop touch and no design fork. Aaron then reordered the queue (E1 hinge-forks ahead of E4-i2); this D113 was already mid-vet so it lands first.

The surcharge is EXACTLY 0 for every starting-roster general (none is `commission.kind:"political"`), the entire CS side, and outside the window вҶ’ `_cmdReliefCost` is byte-identical for the whole roster in every year; the only behavioral change is a UNION political general the player chose to commission AND field in the 1862-64 pre-election window. No new save state; no `_SAVE_VER` bump; NO RNG. ## D110 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q12: THE DIVISION SUB-TIER** (seat pool generals into division billets nested under a seated corps вҖ” the next rung of the GM depth-chart over the OOB tree) вҖ” [CODEX code + CLAUDE close-out] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The next rung of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1's billet tree (Army вҶ’ Corps вҶ’ **DIVISION** вҶ’ Brigade), built HIERARCHICALLY on the Q10 corps depth-chart (D108). Beyond seating the army's IвҖ“IV Corps, the President now SEATS pool generals into each seated corps's **DIVISION** billets (3 per corps), spending `seatCost` (2) political capital (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, no new resource per В§12). A division is staffable ONLY UNDER a SEATED corps (the real chain of command вҖ” a division belonged to a corps), so the depth chart becomes a TREE the President builds top-down.
- **PROVENANCE / CLOSE-OUT (the [AARON] hand-off):** the Q12 CODE + DATA + PROBE were authored in an interrupted Claude-Code session, finished + committed (`7b64d2e`) + pushed by **Codex** on this machine. Codex shipped a sound, builds-GATE-OK, byte-identical-to-source feature **but did NOT run the adversarial bug-hunt or write any doc trail** (a PROPER-VETTING gap vs CLAUDE.md #3 + a record-in-repo gap vs #5). This entry + the bug-hunt below are the **CLAUDE close-out** that brings D110 to the project's "done" bar. (No code was reverted вҖ” the commit is sound; this adds the missing vetting + documentation, plus the one bug-hunt fix.)
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated division commanders only shape the army's LEADERSHIP facet вҖ” an INPUT the bridge already reads вҖ” via a small BOUNDED lift folded into `commandLeadership`, summed exactly like the corps lift: `_cmdDivLift` = clamp(ОЈ over seated divisions of (`effDivRating`вҲ’64)Г—`perSlotWeight`, Вұ`liftCap`) = clamp(ОЈГ—0.03, Вұ2). `effDivRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (4) when his current grade is below `preferredGrade`. The lift is DELIBERATELY SMALLER than the corps lift (cap 2 vs 4, weight 0.03 vs 0.05) so the influence hierarchy holds вҖ” **army (~Вұ17, В§27) > corps (Вұ4) > divisions (Вұ2):** a lower tier is a smaller modifier, never dominant. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership вҶ’ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe, NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). NO RNG.
- **THE GRADE-FIT (a division was a Maj. Gen.'s billet in BOTH armies):** `preferredGrade` is a bare Maj. Gen. for US and CS alike вҖ” distinct from the corps tier (a US corps a Maj. Gen.'s, a CS corps a Lt. Gen.'s). Many divisions were in fact led by Brigadier Generals early in the war, so any Brig. Gen. seated over a division leads `belowGrade` until promoted (the Q9 synergy, biting on both sides here). `data/ratings.json` `divisionCommand`: perCorps 3 В· seatCost 2 В· preferredGrade {US,CS: "Maj. Gen."} В· perSlotWeight 0.03 В· liftCap 2 В· belowGradePenalty 4 В· **Inferred** В· 2 real sources (Glatthaar, *General Lee's Army*; Weigley, *A Great Civil War*).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until you seat a division:** no division seated вҶ’ the ОЈ is over zero slots вҶ’ lift 0 вҶ’ `commandLeadership` unchanged вҶ’ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `7d86fcf` (a vacant division contributes 0, NOT a penalty; `_cmdDivLift` has a fast-path returning 0 without walking the roster when `cmd.divisions` is empty/absent вҖ” so a pre-Q12 save with no record reads identically). **ONE BILLET PER MAN:** a general holds at most one of {army command, a corps, a division}; seating him in a division clears any corps/other division he held, and appointing/seating him HIGHER clears his division. **Vacating a corps CASCADES** вҖ” its orphaned divisions stop contributing lift, enforced at the READ layer (`cmdDivSeated`/`_cmdDivLift` filter divisions whose parent corps is no longer seated; `_cmdDivClean`:795 requires the parent corps seated) and cleaned on the next load-sanitize. `cmd.divisions = {corpsIdx:{divIdx:generalId}}` (nested) rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` sanitizes a tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop array/non-object/out-of-range/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/dupes вҖ” the Q9/Q10/Q11 idiom). Writes ONLY `cmd.divisions` + `C.clock.capital`. Carries the Q9/Q10/Q11 hardening verbatim: the `isFinite` capital guard, the commission gate (`_cmdByIdRoster`+`cmdCommissioned`), and debit-the-rounded-gate-value.
- **THE TEACHING (anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** a corps was only as good as its divisions вҖ” A. P. Hill's hard-hitting "Light Division" and Hood's and Pickett's divisions were the cutting edge of Lee's corps, **as were the Union's hard-fighting divisions under Hancock's II Corps (Gibbon, Barlow)** вҖ” while a corps with weak divisions underdelivered. New UI: division sub-rows nested under each seated corps in the "The Corps Command вҖ” Depth Chart" section + a combined corps+division lift read-out; every new colour annotated вүҘ4.5:1 (WCAG-AA), every dynamic value `_cmdEsc`-escaped.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt (the close-out Codex skipped вҖ” run NOW on the shipped diff):** a Workflow of **5 diverse-lens Opus finders** (no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/edge/save-tamper) Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic. **4 lenses CLEAN; 1 confirmed LOW, FIXED:** the division teaching exemplars (A. P. Hill's Light Division, Hood's, Pickett's) were **all-Confederate** while the rating mechanism is genuinely side-neutral and the sibling corps tier deliberately named both sides (the rout of Howard's XI Corps) вҖ” the exact Lost-Cause over-celebration pattern CLAUDE.md #4 guards against. FIXED (copy-only, byte-identical): added the Union counterpart (Hancock's II Corps divisions, Gibbon/Barlow вҖ” accurate at Gettysburg/Wilderness/Spotsylvania) to both the player-facing `divFoot` string and the `divisionCommand` `_note`. The save-tamper lens independently executed an 18-vector battery against `_cmdDivClean` (Array/null/non-object/out-of-range/float-key/bogus/dead/army-commander/corps-holder/orphaned-corps/cross-corps-dupe) вҖ” all sanitize correctly; the no-fudge lens grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.divisions`; escaping confirmed safe (`htmlEsc` at render + `_cmdEsc` in the UI).
- **Vetting (the offline gates GREEN; the headless `load` suite ENV-BLOCKED):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“`; the committed `civil_war_generals.html` is **byte-identical to the source build** (empty post-build diff); `probe-command` **69/69** (+11 Q12 steps: config + hierarchy [div liftCap < corps liftCap], byte-identical-when-empty + absent-record, the hierarchy gate [division only under a seated corps], spend/gate/re-seat/vacate, the read-layer cascade, one-billet-per-man, render) with **0 pageerrors**; `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346` (Classic paints); `t1probe` + `bootprobe` ok. **No tactical/combat file is in the D110 diff** (`src/35-command.js` + `data/ratings.json` + `tools/probe-command.mjs` + the generated HTML only) вҶ’ the 9 battles are byte-identical to Q11 **by construction**. **ENV:** the strategic no-regression `load` battery (`probe-desk/ratings/camp/officers/field/oob` + the 9 battle probes) was blocked by the documented **THREE-CDN headless `load`-stall** вҖ” jsdelivr rate-limited this machine's headless client after the first clean load, so only the first chromium launch per session loads (re-running the known-good `probe-command` reproduced the stall on demand); these probes share NO Q12 code path and were all GREEN in the Q11 vetting hours earlier. ## D109 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q11: THE COMMISSION MOVE** (bring documented POLITICAL GENERALS into the officer pool for political capital; the GM "Commission" move) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart move of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.2/В§12.3 ("Commission вҖ” bring a new officer into the pool"). Beyond the generals the war hands you, the President may now **COMMISSION the documented POLITICAL GENERALS** вҖ” US **Banks**, **Butler**, **Sigel**, **McClernand**; CS **Floyd**, **Pillow** вҖ” into his officer pool for **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the existing GM currency, no new resource per В§12), after which they are appointable / promotable / seatable like any general. A new Command-desk **"Commission an officer вҖ” the political generals"** section lists each with his (LOW) combat OVR beside his (HIGH) political value, his constituency, an honest one-line record, and a Commission control (gated on capital + the `maxCommissions` slate). Teaches the GM layer's central command-politics lesson (В§12.3, the keystone): political generals were **cheap to commission and weak in the field** вҖ” Lincoln and Davis took them for the factions, votes, and immigrant regiments they delivered, not their generalship вҖ” so once you appoint or seat one, his low OVR drags the army's leadership, the bind Lincoln lived. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose Commission (option C) over the symmetric AI-GM (B, [hard]) and the DIVISION sub-tier (B-alt, lower-risk-but-thinner) because it fills the GM layer's missing teaching keystone (the political-general bind the В§12.3 anti-gamey constraints are built around), uses the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` byte-identical-until-used spine + the В§8 person concept, and adds 6 new citation-grade historical figures. Scoped to a **pure pool-addition move** (no economy/election fork); the full В§12.3 election-support relief-bind is logged as the explicit next increment (it needs the 1864-election state вҖ” here the relief COST is already taught via each officer's `relief` class through `_cmdReliefCost`).
- **ARCHITECTURE (byte-identical until the player commissions):** the commissionable officers live in a SEPARATE data array (`data/generals.json` вҶ’ `sides[side].commissionPool`), so `_cmdSideGenerals` (the starting roster) and every byte-identity-critical path are UNTOUCHED. `cmdCommission` writes ONLY `cmd.commissioned` (an id list) + `C.clock.capital` + a reputation seed вҖ” NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js`). With nobody commissioned, `_cmdRosterPlusCommissioned` === the bare roster (`roster.concat([])`), so the appoint/promote/corps pools, `commandLeadership`, and the 9 battles are identical to HEAD `8eb913a`. A commissioned officer reaches the fight ONLY by being appointed/seated like any general вҖ” no new combat read. `_cmdById` was widened to also resolve the commission pool (so a commissioned-then-appointed officer resolves everywhere); `_cmdByIdRoster` keeps the roster-only lookup for the byte-identity-critical seeds + the commission "not-a-roster-id" guard. `cmd.commissioned` rides the save; `cmdInit` seeds `[]` once + SANITIZES on load (drop dupes / bogus ids / roster ids / over-cap; non-array вҶ’ array вҖ” the Q9/Q8b/Q10 idiom). NO `_SAVE_VER` bump. NO RNG.
- **THE TEACHING (rank вү  competence; anti-Lost-Cause, both sides):** the 6 are authored with LOW combat OVR / HIGH political value вҖ” appointing a commissioned Banks fields commandLeadership **49** vs Grant's **87** (probe-verified). Honest records name the failures plainly on BOTH sides (Banks/Red River, Butler/Fort Fisher, Sigel/New Market, McClernand/Vicksburg insubordination; Floyd & Pillow/the Fort Donelson flight) AND credit the genuine contributions (Butler's 1861 "contraband" decision; Banks's Louisiana free-labor/emancipation work). The combat ratings are stamped **Inferred** (a calibrated reading); the biographies carry вүҘ2 real published sources each (gate-4e-clean). Persona command/tactical/discipline are calibrated so `fldOfficerSkillSeed` rounds EXACTLY to the entry skill (the existing oracle; verified for all 6). Data authored via a 12-agent **research+verify Workflow** (6 Opus historians + adversarial source-check + a completeness critic); the verifier's one HARD correction applied вҖ” **Pillow's rank вҶ’ Brig. Gen.** (his "Maj. Gen." was a Mexican-War US-volunteer / Tennessee-state-militia title; in CSA service he rose only to brigadier вҖ” CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #4); plus Banks's Black-officer purge folded into his bio and Sigel's unconfirmed reprint year dropped.
- **DATA:** `data/generals.json` `sides.US.commissionPool` (us-banks/us-butler/us-sigel/us-mcclernand) + `sides.CS.commissionPool` (cs-floyd/cs-pillow); `data/ratings.json` `commission` config (costPolitical 2 В· costProfessional 8 В· maxCommissions 3 В· Inferred В· 2 src) + 6 new `generalPersonas`. - **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding/cap В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/WCAG/edge] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; **12 agents; invariantsHold = TRUE** вҖ” the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.commissioned`, `cmdCommission` writes EXACTLY `cmd.commissioned`+capital+reputation, the byte-identity-when-empty property, Pillow correctly Brig. Gen., every rendered string escaped, zero id-collision roster-vs-pool). **5 confirmed (2 MED + 3 LOW), ALL FIXED + the behavior-affecting ones probe-locked:** **(MED, the key one)** `cmdAppoint`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdPromote` resolved their target via the widened `_cmdById` with no commissioned-state check вҶ’ an UN-commissioned commission-pool officer could be appointed/seated/promoted at the function level (the gated UI never exposes it, but a direct call / stale corps-`<select>` value bypassed the commission economy) вҶ’ added `if (!_cmdByIdRoster(side,id) && cmdCommissioned(C).indexOf(id)<0) return;` to all three (byte-identical for roster ids вҖ” the clause is always false for them; probe-locked). **(MED, UI)** a commissioned officer seated in a corps always rendered "I Corps" вҖ” the string for-in key was fed to `_cmdNum(kk,0)` (вҶ’ 0) вҶ’ now `parseInt(kk,10)` (probe-locked). **(LOW)** the shared `cap` gate idiom passed a NaN balance (`typeof NaN==='number'`) at all 6 capital-gate sites (tampered-save only, pre-existing, not a Q11 regression) вҶ’ hardened with `&& isFinite(clk.capital)` uniformly + cmdAppoint now debits the rounded `cap`. **(LOW)** the `maxCommissions` fallback default was 4 (copied from `_cmdCorpsSlots`) vs the shipped cap 3 вҶ’ 3. **(LOW)** a commissioned officer past his service window still showed green "Commissioned / in your pool" while the pools dropped him вҶ’ the row now reads muted "Commissioned В· no longer in service". ## D108 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q10: THE CORPS DEPTH-CHART** (seat pool generals into corps billets over the D106 OOB tree; the GM depth-chart MOVE) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The GM depth-chart MOVE of RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1/В§12.2/В§12.4 ("an army version of waiver/trading/transfer"). Beyond appointing the ARMY commander (the existing `cmdAppoint` billet), the President now SEATS pool generals into the army's CORPS billets (IвҖ“IV Corps) over the D106 OOB tree, spending **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by appoint/promote; no new resource per В§12). A new Command-desk **"The Corps Command вҖ” Depth Chart"** section lists the 4 billets, each showing its seated commander (name + grade + OVR + a below-grade tell) with a Vacate control, or "Vacant" + a pool `<select>` + a Seat control (gated on capital); a live read-out shows the net leadership the staffed corps add. Teaches real command organization вҖ” Lee's First (Longstreet) and Second (Jackson) Corps against the Army of the Potomac's churning corps commands; the rout of Howard's XI Corps at Chancellorsville. **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** chose the depth-chart MOVES (option A) over the symmetric AI-GM (option B, flagged [hard] вҖ” an enemy-command shadow wired to combat risks byte-identity/no-fudge) because A extends the proven `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote` spine over the D106 substrate and is byte-identical-until-moved like Q9; the new officer-slot/vacancy concept the derived T15 corps lacked is the `cmd.corps` slot map + the side-aware grade-fit.
- **HOW IT REACHES THE FIGHT (no new combat path; D74/D94 no-fudge):** seated corps commanders only add a small BOUNDED lift to `commandLeadership(C)` вҖ” an INPUT the bridge already reads вҖ” via `_cmdCorpsLift(C)` = `clamp( SUM over seated slots of (effectiveCorpsRating вҲ’ 64) Г— perSlotWeight, вҲ’liftCap, +liftCap )` (perSlotWeight 0.05, liftCap 4). `effectiveCorpsRating` = the general's GM OVR (`_cmdGenRating`, which already carries the Q9 promotion lift) minus `belowGradePenalty` (6) when his CURRENT grade is below the **SIDE-AWARE** `preferredGrade`. It reaches combat ONLY through the existing `commandLeadership вҶ’ bridge LEADERSHIP facet` pipe вҖ” NEVER the scoreboard (build-gate 4d scans `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`). The army commander still weighs most (`(ratingвҲ’64)Г—0.7`, swing ~Вұ17); the corps lift (Вұ4) is a secondary modifier (В§27: small, never dominant).
- **THE SIDE-AWARE GRADE-FIT (historically precise, the Q9 synergy):** a US corps was a **Major General's** command; a CS corps a **Lieutenant General's** вҖ” the CS authorized the Lt. Gen. grade by Act of Sept. 18, 1862 and promoted Longstreet/Jackson that October to command the ANV's new corps (formally organized GO No. 6, Nov. 6, 1862). So on the shipped roster only CS **Stuart** (a Maj. Gen.) seats below grade over a corps (he leads stretched); promoting him to Lt. Gen. (Q9) removes the penalty. On the US roster every named general already meets the Maj. Gen. floor (a correct latent guard for any future junior/commissioned officer). `data/ratings.json` `corpsCommand` block: `slots 4 В· labels [I..IV Corps] В· seatCost 3 В· preferredGrade {US:"Maj. Gen.", CS:"Lt. Gen."} В· perSlotWeight 0.05 В· liftCap 4 В· belowGradePenalty 6 В· prov Inferred В· 2 real sources` (Sears 1988 on AoP corps creation; Glatthaar 2008 on ANV corps).
- **BYTE-IDENTICAL until the player seats a corps:** no corps seated вҶ’ the SUM is over zero slots вҶ’ lift 0 вҶ’ `commandLeadership` unchanged вҶ’ the sandbox + all 9 battles identical to HEAD `2d11bd7`. A vacant billet contributes 0 (NOT a baseline penalty вҖ” that would break byte-identity). `cmd.corps` rides the save (no `_SAVE_VER` bump); `cmdInit` SANITIZES a stale/tampered/imported record on LOAD (drop invalid slots/ids/dead generals/the army commander; one corps per general; arrayвҶ’{}). Constraints: one corps per general (reassign clears the old slot); the army commander cannot also hold a corps (excluded from the pool; `cmdAppoint` clears the appointee's corps); seating gates on capital and debits the SAME rounded value the gate compared (the Q9/Q8b hardened idiom); vacate is free; re-seating the same slot+general is a no-op (no re-charge). New fns (`src/35-command.js` Q10 block): `_cmdCorpsCfg`/`_cmdCorpsSlots`/`_cmdCorpsLabel`/`_cmdCorpsPreferredGrade`/`_cmdCorpsClean`/`cmdCorpsSeated`/`_cmdCorpsBelowGrade`/`_cmdCorpsEffRating`/`_cmdCorpsLift`/`cmdCorpsCommanderFor`/`_cmdCorpsPoolFor`/`cmdSeatCorps`/`cmdVacateCorps`/`_cmdCorpsSelect`/`_cmdCorpsSlotRow`/`_cmdCorpsDepthHTML`; edits to `commandLeadership` (+the lift term), `cmdInit` (seed+sanitize), `cmdAppoint` (clear billet), `cmdRenderTab`/`cmdWireTab`. NO RNG.
- **THE OOB-BOARD DISPLAY JOIN (T15, pure display):** seated commanders NAME the player's DERIVED corps on the D106 board (`fldCampaignOOB` attaches `co.commander` when `player.source==='derived'`; `_fldOOBSideExact` renders it). The predicted EDGE is UNCHANGED by seating (leadership is captured in the actual fight, never double-counted on the board). Authored battles show the historical brigades (no corps-slot naming); the enemy is NEVER named by the player's depth chart.
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/WCAG/edge] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; **11 agents; 5 raw вҶ’ 3 confirmed (1 MED + 2 LOW); invariantsHold = TRUE** вҖ” the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.corps`, seat/vacate write only `cmd.corps`+capital, byte-identity airtight, no fabricated officers, the 2 sources real + on-claim). **ALL 3 confirmed FIXED:** **(MED, UI)** the seat event-log said "he leads **above** his grade" for a BELOW-grade general (contradicting every other surface) вҶ’ "below". **(LOW, anti-fabrication)** the OOB-board attach was keyed by array index, so a real general could be named over a derived **"Garrison"** node (a sub-1200-man fort/detachment, NOT a corps billet) вҶ’ the attach now guards to `/ Corps$/`-labeled nodes only (a probe assertion locks the Garrison guard). **(LOW, citation)** the teaching copy said the CS "created the Lt. Gen. grade in October 1862" вҶ’ corrected to the precise Sept. 18, 1862 authorization + the October promotions + the Nov. 6 reorganization (in `data/ratings.json` + the `35-command.js` comment). The 3 critic-"missed" were non-blocking: the workflow agents could not run the browser probes (the main session ran the full suite вҖ” see below); the Вұ4 cap is secondary to the army-commander's Вұ17 (В§27 holds); and probe step #5 already proved `cmdPromote` reaches Lt. Gen. on the CS side (Stuart eff 74вҶ’82 after promotion).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“`; **combat byte-identity STRUCTURAL** (no combat path reads `cmd.corps`; `commandLeadership += 0` when unseated) + **EMPIRICAL** вҖ” a 132-cell A/B harness (`.tmp/q10-ab.mjs`, base = `git show HEAD:civil_war_generals.html`) over (side Г— appointee Г— date) confirms `commandLeadership`/`bridgeArmy.overall`/`leadership`/the auto-resolve margin reads are **byte-identical to HEAD** (no corps seated), 0 pageerrors; `probe-command` **49/49** (+9 Q10 steps: config В· byte-identical-off [lift 0, absent-record == seeded-empty] В· gate+spend+no-recharge+free-vacate В· bounded-lift [one strong vs full staff capped at 4] В· CS below-grade penalty + the Q9 promote-to-fit synergy + the US floor-met contrast В· one-corps-per-general+reassign+appoint-clears+army-cmd-not-seatable В· save-tamper sanitize В· no-output-gate В· render); `probe-oob` **16/16** (+the Q10 step: seating names the derived CORPS, edge unchanged, the Garrison guard, the enemy never named); FULL no-regression GREEN вҖ” `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-ratings` 21/21, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `probe-field` 13/13, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok, the 9 battles + `probe-csplayer` green (bullrun 15 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· gettysburg 16 В· chancellorsville 24 В· malvern 24 В· shiloh 29 В· vicksburg 18 В· chickamauga 18 В· csplayer 16); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA (3 contrast fixes on the new UI: the below-grade tell `#c9712e`вҶ’`#d17936` 4.54:1, and two T15 commander-name opacities .82/.9вҶ’.92 to 4.50:1). **ENV:** intermittent THREE-CDN headless load-stalls on the heaviest battle probes (chancellorsville/malvern/shiloh) cleared by standalone retry (the documented gotcha); the `domcontentloaded` A/B harness is the authoritative no-regression spine. ## D107 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **Q8b: THE BETWEEN-BATTLE CAVALRY RECONNAISSANCE** ("scout the enemy" вҖ” tier-reveal the enemy OOB, scaled by the appointed general's cavalry) вҖ” [CLAUDE] (overnight run, 2026-06-23)
The camp loop's deferred SCOUTING (RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§15; deferred at D100 until the D106 OOB-mapping substrate existed). On the President's-Desk Command tab, an **"Order a reconnaissance"** control inside the D106 Order-of-Battle board lets the President spend a small amount of **political capital** (`C.clock.capital` вҖ” the EXISTING GM currency, also spent by `cmdAppoint`/`cmdPromote`; no new resource per В§12) to reveal the **enemy** order of battle to a TIER scaled by the appointed army commander's persona **`cavalry`** attribute. Teaches that good cavalry leadership buys good intelligence вҖ” Stuart's reconnaissance rides, and the catastrophic intelligence vacuum at Gettysburg when his cavalry was absent (named as a real Confederate command failure, not glorified). **PICK RATIONALE (decide-&-log within the cleared NEXT menu):** both the GM depth-chart MOVES and Q8b scouting were unblocked by D106; I chose scouting over the depth-chart MOVES because its scaling input (the `cavalry` persona attribute, spread 50вҖ“70 across the 9 generals) and its `reveal` hook in `fldCampaignOOBHtml` BOTH already existed, `36-camp.js` explicitly deferred scouting to exactly this substrate, the D106 board already advertised a dead "Scout the enemy" CTA, and scouting is **pure display + an economy spend (never touches combat)** вҖ” the safest possible byte-identity. The corps-billet depth-chart MOVES need a new officer-slot concept the derived T15 tree lacks (bigger surface) вҖ” deferred next.
- **THREE RECON TIERS (В§15):** **light** (unscouted вҖ” the passive D106 estimate: force grade band + rough brigade count + the CTA) вҶ’ **better** (scouted, cavalry < `cavalryFullThreshold` 65: the enemy commander NAMED + per-corps grade + a posture/terrain advisory, NO per-brigade detail) вҶ’ **full** (scouted, cavalry вүҘ 65: the complete enemy OOB, the exact view). With the 9 generals' cavalry: Grant (66) + Lee (70) вҶ’ full; the rest вҶ’ better; a no-appointee campaign uses the HISTORICAL DEFAULT commander's cavalry (not a flat baseline). Intel is **fresh per engagement** вҖ” the scout record is keyed to the next-battle id, so it reverts to light when the battle changes.
- **ARCHITECTURE (the D106 wall preserved):** the WRITE (`cmdScout`) lives in `src/35-command.js` (it gates on capital like `cmdAppoint`, reads the appointee's `cavalry` via `_cmdGenPersona`, computes the tier via the pure `_cmdScoutTierForCavalry`, and writes ONLY `cmd.scout` + debits `C.clock.capital` вҖ” NEVER the scoreboard); **T15-oob.js stays a PURE READ-OUT** вҖ” `fldCampaignOOBHtml(C, {reveal, reconHtml})` is told the tier + the recon-control HTML by `cmdRenderTab`, and only ADDS the "better"-tier renderer (`_fldOOBSideScouted` + `_fldScoutPosture`). No combat/resolve/tick/conditioning path reads `cmd.scout` (grep-confirmed) вҶ’ a campaign that never scouts is byte-identical to the pre-Q8b build, and the 9 tactical battles are untouched. Build-gate 4d already scans both `35-command.js` + `tactical/T15-oob.js`. `cmd.scout` rides the save (C.president serialized wholesale); `cmdInit` lazily sanitizes a malformed/tampered record (dropвҶ’null; validвҶ’bounded) вҖ” no `_SAVE_VER` bump. Data: a `scout` config block in `data/ratings.json` (cost 3 В· cavalryFullThreshold 65 В· baselineCavalry 54 В· 2 real sources). NO RNG (deterministic).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/byte-identity В· economy/determinism/bounding В· citation/anti-Lost-Cause/no-fabricated-officers В· XSS/escaping В· UI/WCAG/edge-render] Г— default-refute Opus verify Г—3 + a completeness critic; **9 agents; invariantsHold = TRUE** вҖ” the critic independently grep-confirmed no combat path reads `cmd.scout`, cmdScout writes only `cmd.scout`+capital, the 9 battles byte-identical, no fabricated officers, citations real). **1 confirmed LOW + 2 critic-surfaced LOW; all actionable ones fixed:** **(LOW, confirmed)** `cmdScout` gated on `Math.round(capital)` but debited RAW `clk.capital` вҖ” the exact Q9 gate/debit rounding divergence `cmdPromote` was hardened against (byte-identical under today's integer-only capital paths, but a latent fractional bug + a consistency hazard) вҶ’ FIXED to debit `cap - cost` (the hardened idiom). **(LOW, critic-surfaced)** `_fldScoutPosture` read the UN-flipped historical attacker, ignoring `C.flipAtk` (the alt-history attacker swap the resolver applies) вҶ’ the "better"-tier posture could mis-describe who attacks after a recovery refight вҶ’ FIXED by honoring `C.flipAtk` with the SAME non-mutating `Object.assign({}, bd, {atk:swapped})` swap the resolver uses (strength/edge are attacker-symmetric, so only the posture line needs it; a probe assertion locks it). **(LOW, deferred вҖ” critic agreed no action)** `cmd.scout.turn` is a cosmetic provenance stamp nothing reads (bounded on load).
- **Vetting (PROPER VETTING, all GREEN):** `GATE OK В· no-fudge вң“ В· citations вң“`; **combat byte-identity STRUCTURAL** (no combat path reads `cmd.scout`; the source diff is display + an economy spend) and EMPIRICAL (all 10 battle probes land on their historical results, unchanged); `probe-oob` **15/15** (+the SCOUT TIERS step: lightвҶ’betterвҶ’full ladder, "better" names + per-corps + posture + NO per-brigade leak, the flipAtk posture-flip + non-mutation), `probe-command` **40/40** (+6 Q8b steps: tier mapping at the threshold + fresh="light"; cmdScout reveals at the appointee's tier + debits EXACTLY the cost; the gate + idempotence [short capital no-op, no re-charge]; stale-reconвҶ’light; save-tamper sanitize; no-output-gate + unscouted-offers-button); FULL no-regression GREEN вҖ” `probe-desk` 13/13, `probe-ratings` 21/21, `probe-camp` 8/8, `probe-officers` 15/15, `probe-field` 13/13, `t1probe` 14/14, `bootprobe` ok, ALL 9 battles + `probe-csplayer` green (bullrun 15 В· antietam 16 В· fredericksburg 22 В· gettysburg 16 В· chancellorsville 24 В· malvern 24 В· shiloh 29 В· vicksburg 18 В· chickamauga 18 В· csplayer 16); `diag-classic` `nonBlank:346`; 0 pageerrors throughout; `wcag-auditor` AA (one contrast fix `#d66040`вҶ’`#e86840` on the new "Needs capital to scout" span вҖ” the auditor measured `#d66040` at 3.92:1/4.33:1, sub-AA; **NOTE for a future pass: the existing `#d66040` usages elsewhere in `35-command.js` are the same sub-AA вҖ” pre-existing, out of this scope, logged**). **ENV:** the run was PAUSED mid-vet on an Aaron "pause internet" directive (the battle probes fetch THREE from a CDN; the bug-hunt + wcag are API calls) and RESUMED cleanly; intermittent THREE-CDN load-stalls cleared by retry (the documented gotcha). ## D106 вҖ” RATING SYSTEM **THE OOB-MAPPING SUBSTRATE** + a read-only Order-of-Battle board (the В§12.1 roster screen; the shared blocker for the GM depth-chart MOVES + Q8b scouting) вҖ” [OPUS] (overnight run, 2026-06-22)
The shared plumbing the GM depth-chart MOVES (В§12.2) and Q8b SCOUTING (В§15) both depend on: a READ-ONLY layer mapping the strategic next-battle (`_brgNextBattle`) to a STRUCTURED order of battle вҖ” commander вҶ’ corps вҶ’ brigade вҖ” for BOTH sides, each billet carrying its OVR/grade/strength/provenance (the T14 rating spine). New module **`src/tactical/T15-oob.js`** (spliced after T14; `fldOOBForSide`/`fldCampaignOOB`/`fldCampaignOOBHtml` + helpers). Surfaced as a new **"Order of Battle вҖ” the Next Engagement"** section on the President's-Desk Command tab (one render line in `cmdRenderTab`). The recommended-but-FORK-RISKY item was scoped SMALL first per the run plan: a read-only query layer + roster board, **no combat wiring** (the procedural skirmish `_fldCampaignSkirmishParams` is UNCHANGED). Design law: RATING-SYSTEM-DESIGN В§12.1/В§13/В§15. **No new fork surfaced** вҖ” `BATTLES[]` already carries real `cmdUS`/`cmdCS` per battle and the 9 scenarios carry real brigade OOBs, so the substrate is buildable read-only + citation-clean without contradicting a shipped teaching.
- **TWO SOURCES, ONE SHAPE:** a battle WITH a hand-built tactical scenario (`fldScenarioData`) exposes its REAL brigade OOB (real commanders + the authored provenance read straight from each unit note via `_fldOOBProvFromNote`, reusing the Q7 reader `_fldOOBUnits` which scopes a multi-phase battle to phase 0); a procedural battle DERIVES a deterministic corps/brigade tree split from the authored totals (`bd.us`/`bd.cs`/year), seeded by id+side (NO RNG). Derived billets are FORMATION-LABELED (I Corps В· 1st Brigade В· Garrison) with `commander:null` вҖ” **NEVER a fabricated officer** (CLAUDE.md #4 / D92). The army-commander headline names only the player's APPOINTED general (the GM payoff + his `_cmdGenRating` OVR) or the battle's historical `cmd<Side>` (BATTLES вҖ” Verified). NEVER invents.
- **THE WALL (D74/D94/D92):** a PURE READ-OUT + DISPLAY, called ONLY from `cmdRenderTab` вҖ” never a resolve/tick/conditioning path. Writes NOTHING; read at no point in combat resolution вҶ’ the sandbox + all 9 battles are byte-identical **BY CONSTRUCTION** (the generated html diff vs committed HEAD `7df4372` is ALL-ADDITIONS вҖ” the T15 block + one desk-render line, **ZERO removed/modified lines**). build-gate 4d's `RATING_MODULES` now ALSO scans `tactical/T15-oob.js` (the no-fudge OUTPUT-WALL structural over it too).
- **ENEMY-FUZZY (В§15):** the board renders the PLAYER's own OOB EXACT and the ENEMY as a FUZZY estimate (force grade + brigade count + commander, NO per-brigade detail) вҖ” the designed hook **Q8b scouting will DEEPEN via a higher `reveal` tier**. The substrate returns the FULL data for both sides (so the GM/scouting can query it); only the BOARD gates the enemy. Triple-encoded + CVD-safe (OVR = number+letter+word; provenance = hatch+glyph+word; the edge = a labeled % bar); all data names routed through `_fldOOBEsc` (XSS-safe).
- **Adversarial bug-hunt** (5 diverse-lens Opus finders [no-fudge/purity В· determinism/bounding В· citation-honesty/anti-Lost-Cause В· UI/WCAG/XSS В· integration/edge] Г— default-refute Opus verify + a completeness critic; 15 agents; **5 confirmed: 1 HIGH + 4 MED; critic "NOT SAFE AS-IS" until fixed; the hard invariants [no-fudge/byte-identity, determinism, no-fabricated-officers, XSS-safe] independently CONFIRMED HOLD**).
